- Twarabonye kandi uruhara rwa _Anchors_, zizana vyose hamwe (ugucuruza txid, ikimenyamenya c'igiti ca Merkle n'ikimenyamenya ca Taproot) mu gice kimwe.


Mu bikorwa, ugushirwa mu ngiro kw’ubuhinga kugabuwe muma Rust crates yabigenewe ( Kuruhande_rw'ukwemeza kw'umuguzi, _gusuzuma ukwemeza_, _bp_core_, n’ibindi). Ivyiyumviro vy’ishimikiro biri ng’aho:


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/046.webp)


Mu kigabane gikwirikira, turaza kuraba igice ca off-chain gusa ca RGB, nk'amasezerano y'urukwirikirane. Turabona ingene amasezerano ya RGB, atunganijwe nkuko imashine irangiye imeze_, ashika ku vyo guserura vyinshi kuruta inyandiko za Bitcoin, mu gihe azigama ibanga ry'amakuru yabo.


## Intangamarara kuri smart contracts niko imeze


<chapterId>04a9569f-3563-5382-bf53-0c7069343ba0</chapterId>


:::video id=db4ee09f-1352-4ad1-9f7a-c962df7ea9fa::::


Murikino kigabane hamwe n'igikwirikira, turaza kuraba inyigisho za **Smart contract** muri RGB maze tubone uburyo butandukanye ayo masezerano ashobora gusobanura no guhindura *uko ameze*. Turabona igituma unyubako ya RGB, bukoresheje urutonde rw’Ibimenyetso vy'iserire ikora rimwe gusa, butuma bishoboka gukora ubwoko butandukanye bw’**Ibikorwa vya amasezerano*** mu buryo bushobora guhindurwa kandi ata guca mu gitabu c’ivyandikano gihurikiye hamwe. Turaba kandi uruhara rw'***ishoramari rigenda*** mu gutegura iterambere ry'uko amasezerano ameze.


### Smart contracts  n'uburenganzira bw'abatwara


Intumbero ya RGB ni ugutanga ibikorwa remezo vyo gushira ama smart contracts kuri Bitcoin. Mu kuvuga "Smart contract" dushaka kuvuga amasezerano hagati y'imigwi myinshi ashirwa mu ngiro ubwayo kandi akoresheje ubuhinga bwa none, ata muntu yinjiyemwo kugira ngo ashitse ingingo. Mu yandi majambo, itegeko ry'amsezerano rishirwa mu ngiro na porogarama, atari n’uwundi muntu yizigirwa.


Ivyo bikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none bivyura ikibazo c'ukutagira aho riyoboka: twoshobora gute kwibohora mu gitabu c’ivyandikano kiyobowe (nk’akarorero, urubuga ruyobowe canke ubushinguzi bw'amakuru) kugira ngo dushobore gucunga ibikorwa kwitirirwa ikintu canke amasezerano agenda? Iciyumviro c'intango, cafashwe na RGB, ni ugusubira ku buryo bw'ukwitirirwa ikintu buzwi nka "ibikoresho vy'abatwara". Muri kahise, hariho ivyemezo bimwebimwe (amafagitire, ugusangira imitungo, n'ibindi) vyasohorwa mu buryo bw’umuntu afise iyo nyandiko, ivyo bikaba vyatuma umuntu wese yari afise iyo nyandiko ku mubiri ashobora gushitsa uburenganzira bwiwe.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/055.webp)


RGB ikoresha ico ciyumviro kw’isi y’ubuhinga bwa none: uburenganzira (n’inshingano) bushirwa mu makuru akoreshwa nabi off-chain, kandi ikibanza c’ayo makuru kiremezwa n’abaje mu nama ubwabo. Ivyo bituma, a priori, habaho urugero runini cane rw’ibanga n’ukwigenga kuruta uko bitangwa n’izindi nzira zishingiye ku bitabo biri kukarubanda.


### Intangamarara kuri Smart Contract hamwe n'uko RGB imeze


Smart contract muri RGB ishobora kubonwa nk’imashini ya Leta, isigurwa na:




- A **Igihugu**, akarorero urutonde rw'amakuru rwerekana ugushirwaho kuhari kw'amasezerano;
- A **Uko ishoramari rimeze** (urutonde rw’amategeko), vyerekana n'ayahe masezerano canke biciye hehe Ukobimeze bishoborwa guhindurwa.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/056.webp)


Ni vyiza gutahura ko ayo masezerano atagarukira kukurungika ama tokens. Bishobora gukoresha uburyo bwinshi: kuva ku mutungo wa kera ( amatokene, ibigega, amafagitire) gushika ku buhinga bukomeye cane (uburenganzira bwo gukoresha, amajambo y’ubudandaji, n’ibindi). aho bitandukaniye n'izindi blockchains, aho kode y'amasezerano ashobora kubineka kandi agakoreshwa nabose, uburyo bwa RGB buragabanya uburyo bwo gushikira no kumenya Contract ku bari muri iyo nama ("***amasezerano y'abahashika***"). Hariho uruhara rwinshi:




- **Uwutanga** canke uwukora amasezerano, ni we asigura inkomoko y'amasezerano n'ibihinduka vyayo vy'intango;
-  **Ibice vy'uburenganzira** (*Gutunga ikintu*) canke ubundi bushobozi bwo gushitsa amategeko;
- **Abarorere**, bashobora kuba bafise aho babona amakuru amwamye, ariko badashobora gutuma habaho ihinduka.


Ukwo gutandukanya uruhara biratuma habaho ukurinda ibihano, mu kumenya ko abantu bemerewe bonyene ari bo bashobora gukorana n'uko amasezerano ameze. Iha kandi RGB ubushobozi bwo gupima mu buryo buringaniye: ivyemezo vyinshi bibera hanze ya Blockchain, kandi ni vyo vyonyene bifata amabanga (*ukwiyemeza*) vyanditswe kuri Bitcoin.


### Ikibanza n'uko ishoramari rimeze muri RGB


Uvuye ku bijanye n’ibikorwa, amasezerano yuko **ishoramari rimeze** afata uburyo bw’amategeko n’inyandiko, asobanurwa mu co RGB yita **Igicapo**. Igicapo kivuga:




- Inyubako y'uko bimeze (n'ibihe bice bija kukarubanda? Nibihe bice bifiswe nizihe mpande?
- Amategeko y'ukwemerwa (ibishobora kumanza kurabwa imbere y'ukuraba ibishirwa kumwanya?);
- Ivyemezo (ni nde yoshobora gutanguza *uko bishobora guhinduka*? Ninde yoshobora kwihweza gusa?).


Muri ico gihe nyene, **Uko amasezerano ameze** akenshi igabanywamwo ibice bibiri:




- **Ayari kuri bose**: igice ca bose, gishobora kwihwezwa na bose (bivanye n’imiterere);
- **Izifashwe n'abantu**: ibice vy'abigenga, bigenewe cane cane ba nyen'ibihugu biciye ku ma UTXO yerekanwa mu nzira y'uko amasezerano ameze.


Nk'uko tuzobibona mu bigabane bizokwirikira, ivugurura ryose ry'imimerere (*ibikorwa vy'amaserano*) ritegerezwa gushirwa ku _ikwiyemeza_ kwa Bitcoin (biciye kuri `Opret` canke `Tapret`) kandi ryubahirize inyandiko za *uko ishoramari rimeze* kugira ngo ribonwe ko rifise akamaro.


### Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano: ugushiraho n'iterambere ry'uko bimeze


Mu gisata ca RGB, ***Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano*** ni ikintu cose gihindura amasezerano kuva **uko yarameze kera** gushika **uko ameze ubu**. Ivyo bikorwa vyisunga ubu buhinga bukurikira:




- Turaraba uko amasezerano ameze ubu;
- Turashira mu ngiro itegeko canke igikorwa (***Uko ahinduka***, ***Itanguriro*** nimba ari uko yatanguye ameze, canke ***ari ayongeweko*** nimba hari ikimntu kuri kukarubanda gishobora gusubira);
- Dushinga impinduka biciye mukwiyemeza kuri Blockchain, dufunga _iserire ikoreshwa rimwe incuro imwe_ tugakora iyindi;
- Abafise uburenganzira baremeza mu karere (*uruhande rw'umuguzi*) ko iyo mpinduka ihuye n' *igicapo* kandi ko iyo nzira y'ubudandaji ya Bitcoin yanditswe kuri On-Chain.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/057.webp)


Iherezo ry’ivyo n'amasezerano yashizwe, ubu ikaba afise ukundi ameze ifise. Iryo hinduka ntirisaba ko urubuga rwose rwa Bitcoin rwitwararika ido n'ido, kuko urutoke rutoyi gusa ruri kubihinga bw'inabwoko (_ukwiyemeza_) rwanditswe muri Blockchain. Urutonde rwa Serire ikoreshwa rimwe rurabuza Ukuriha kabiri iyo ari yo yose canke gukoresha kabiri kw'uk bimeze


### Uruhererekane rw'ibikorwa: kuva kuntango gushika kw'aho biherera


Kugira ngo ivyo tubishire mu ngiro, Smart contract ya RGB itangura n’ **Intanguriro**, ubwambere. Inyuma y’aho, Ibikorwa bitandukanye vy'amasezerano birakurikirana, bikagira DAG (*Directed Acyclic Graph*) y’ibikorwa:




- Impinduka yose ishingiye uko biheruko kuba bimeze (canke nyinshi, mu gihe c’impinduka zihuye);
- Urutonde rw’ibihe ruremezwa n’ugushiramwo ihinduka ryose mu gitabu caho Bitcoin Ishingiye, gifise ikidodo c’igihe kandi kitahinduka bivuye ku kwumvikana kwa Proof-of-Work;
- Iyo ata bindi bikorwa biriko birakorwa, **Aho biherera** harashikwako: ahamaze gushikwa kandi hakwije vyose kumasezerano.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/012.webp)


Iyi DAG yubatse (aho kuba uruzitiro rworoshe rw’umurongo) yerekana ko bishoboka ko ibice bitandukanye vy'amasezerano bishobora gutera imbere abangabanganijwe, igihe cose bitavuguruzanya. RGB rero yitwararika kwirinda ukudahuza kwose biciye mu kugenzura *ku ruhande rw'ukwemeza kumuguzi* kuri buri muntu wese abirimwo.


### Mumajambo make


Ama Smart contracts muri RGB azana uburyo bw’ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none, bitagira aho biyoboka ariko bishinze imizi muri Bitcoin kugira ngo bimenyeshe igihe no kwemeza urutonde rw’ihanahanwa. Ishirwa mu ngiro ry’ayo masezerano rishingiye kuri:




- **Uko amasezerano ameze**, yerekana uko amasezerano ateye ubu (uburenganzira, uburinganire, ibihinduka, n’ibindi);
- **Uko ishoramari rimeze** (*Igicapo*), isobanura nayahe mahinduka yemerewe nuko ategezwa kwemerwa;
- **Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano**, bishira kugihe ukobimeze intambwe ku yindi, bivuye ku masezerano ashingiye ku bikorwa vya Bitcoin.


Mukigabane gikurikira, tuzoja mu buryo burambuye ku bijanye ***uko bimeze*** n'izo ***n'uko bihinduka*** ico vyokwerekanye kurugero rwa off-chain, n'ingene zifitaniye isano n'ivyo bimenyetso vy'ubuhinga bwa none (UTXOs) n'ibimenyetso vy'ubuhinga bwa none (Serire ikoreshwa rimwe) bishizwe muri Bitcoin. Ivyo bizoba ari akaryo ko kubona ingene ubuhinga bwo mu mutima bwa RGB, bushingiye kuruhande rw'ukwemeza rw'umuguzi, bushobora kuguma buhuye n'ama  smart contracts mu gihe buzigama ibanga ry’amakuru.


## RGB Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano


<chapterId>78c44e88-50c4-5ec4-befe-456c1a9f080b</chapterId>


:::id ya videwo=1caec34d-f214-425b-a1a4-0a40ae7d3e0e:::


Muri kino kigabane, turaza kuraba ingene ibikorwa muma smart contracts no mu guhindura uko ibintu bikorwa, kandi murukwirikirane rwa RGB. Intumbero izoba kandi iyo gutahura ingene abaje mu nama benshi bafatanya mu gutanga Ibibitirirwa vy'imitungo.


### Impinduka zuko bimeze n'uko bigenda


Ingingo rusangi iracari iyo y'ukwemeza kuruhande rw'umuguzi, aho amakuru y'uko bimeze afiswe na nyen’ayo makuru, akaremezwa n’uwuyaronka. Nubwo biruko, ikintu kidasanzwe aha kuri RGB kiri mu kuba Bob, nk’uwuronka, asaba Alice kwinjiza amakuru amwamwe mu makuru y'amasezerano kugira ngo agire ububasha nyakuri ku mutungo yaronse, biciye ku nsiguro yihishije kuri imwe mu ma UTXO yiwe.


Kugira ngo tubone ingene *Uko bimeze bihinduka* ikora (ari yo imwe mu nzira z’ishimikiro ***Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano*** muri RGB), reka dufate akarorero k’intambwe ku yindi k’uguhindura umutungo hagati ya Alice na Bob:


**Ivyabaye mu ntango:**


Alice ifise ***ahashinguwe hakoresha ubuhinga bwa RGB*** y’amakuru yemejwe mu karere (*uruhande rw’umuguzi*). Ubu bushinguzi bwerekeza kuri imwe mu UTXO ziwe kuri Bitcoin. Ivyo bisigura ko _insobanuro y'ikidodo_ muri aya makuru yerekana UTXO ari iya Alice. Iciyumviro ni ukumushoboza kwimurira uburenganzira bumwe bumwe bujanye n'umutungo (nk'ibimenyetso vya RGB) wa Bob.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/058.webp)


**Bob nawe arafise ama UTXO:**


Ku rundi ruhande, Bob afise n’imiburiburi UTXO imwe yiwe bwite, ata sano ry’ukuri n’iya Alice. Iyo Bob ata UTXO afise, birashoboka ko yomurungikira akoresheje *Icabona c'ihanahanwa* ubwayo: igisubizo c'iyi nzira kizobamwo ukwiyemeza (_ukwiyemeza_) kandi kizofatanya Ugutunga nyakwo kw'amasezerano mashasha na Bob.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/059.webp)


**Ubwubatsi bw'umutungi mushasha (*Uko bimeze gushasha*):**


Bob arungikira amakuru ya Alice yigizwe ibanga mu buryo bwa ***Invoice*** (tuzoja mu ndondoro ku bijanye n'ubwubatsi bwa Invoice mu bice bizokurikira), imusaba kurema igihugu gishasha gihuye n'amategeko ya Contract. Iyi leta izobamwo *Seal Definition* nshasha yerekana imwe mu UTXO za Bob. Muri ubwo buryo, Bob ihabwa Ownership y’itunga risobanuwe muri iyo leta nshasha, nk’akarorero umubare kanaka w’ibimenyetso vya RGB.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/060.webp)


**Gutegura urugero rw'ihanahanwa:**


Alice rero arakora ihanahanwa rya Bitcoin  ikoresha UTXO yavuzwe muri Serire iheruka (iyo yamuhaye uburenganzira bwo kuba uwuyifise). Mu gisohoka c'iyi hanahanwa, *Ukwiyemeza* (biciye muri `Opret` canke `Tapret`) yinjizwa muri Mumizi y'uko RGB isigaye imeze. Ukwiyemeza kwa `Opret` canke `Tapret` akomoka ku giti ca *MPC* (nk’uko vyabonetse mubigabane biheruka), gishobora gukoranya amahinduka menshi ava mu masezerano atandukanye.


**Ugutanga *ikintu* kwa Bob:**


Imbere yo gutangaza iryo hanahanwa, Alice arungikira Bob ***ikintu*** irimwo amakuru yose akenewe *yo ku ruhande rw’umuguzi* (*Stash* yiwe) hanyuma uko amakuru mashahsa afashe na Bob. Muri iki gihe, Bob ikoresha amategeko y’uguhurizako ya RGB:




- Iremeza amakuru yose ya RGB ari muri *Ibintu*, harimwo uko bisigaye bimeze muvvyatanzwe mugutunga inomtungo;
- Ishingiye ku *Mubihubakiye* Harimwo *ibibintu*, igenzura urutonde rw'ivyabona vy'ihanahanwa (kuva mwitangiro gushika ku mpinduka iherutse) kandi ikemeza amasezerano ahuye muri Blockchain.


**Uguheza kw'ihinduka:**


Iyo Bob akwihje, arashobora gutanga ukwemeza kwiwe (nk’akarorero, mu gushira umukono mu *ibintu*). Alice arashobora rero gutangaza ivyerekanwa vy’ihanahanwa vyateguwe. Mugihe vyemewe, ivyo bica bifunga Serire yari ifiswe na Alice, bigatuma Bitingwa na Bob. Umutekano wo kurwanya Ukuriha kabiri rero ushingiye ku buryo bumwe nk’ubwo muri Bitcoin: UTXO irakoreshwa, bikaba vyerekana ko Alice atagishobora kuyikoresha.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/061.webp)


Uko bisigaye bimeze rero vyerekana UTXO ya Bob, bigaha Bob Uburenganzira bw'ugutunga ivyaheruka kuba bifiswe na Alice. Igisohoka ca Bitcoin aho amakuru ya RGB ashizweho gica kiba ikimenyamenya kidashobora gusubirwamwo c'ukurungika.


Akarorero k’i DAG ntoyi (*Directed Acyclic Graph*) igizwe n’ibikorwa bibiri vya mumasezerano (**mw'itanguriro** hanyuma ***uko bihinduka***) karashobora kwerekana ingene igihugu ca RGB (*uruhande rw’umuguzi* Layer, mw'ibara ritukura) gifatanya na Blockchain4 G4*W-740). mu rurimi rw’umuhondo).


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/062.webp)


Birerekana ko Itanguro isobanura Iserire (*Insiguro ya Serire*), hanyuma *Uko bisigaye bimeze* igafunga iyo Serire kugira ngo ireme indi nshasha mu yindi UTXO.


Muri ivyo, ng’ibi ivyibutsa bikeyi vy’amajambo:




- ***Umwimenyerezo*** ihuriza hamwe ibi bikurikira:
    - ***Insiguro ya Serire*** (iyikora kuri UTXO);
- Ibihugu vy'ubutunzi, ni ukuvuga amakuru ahuye na **Ownership** (nk'akarorero, igitigiri c'ibimenyetso vyimuriwe).
- **Uko bimeze murirusangi** ihuriza hamwe imiterere rusangi y'amasezerano, Aboneka , kandi igatuma ivy’ubwihindurize bihuye kw’isi yose.


**Impinduka z'uko bimeze**, zavuzwe mu kigabane c'imbere, ni zo nzira nyamukuru z'ibikorwa vy'amasazerano. Bivuga intara imwe canke nyinshi za kera (kuva kw'itanguriro canke iyindi uko impinduka imeze) hanyuma zigasubiramwo intara nshasha.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/063.webp)


Iki kigereranyo kirerekana ingene, muri *Umutekero w'uko imoinduka zimeze*, ibimenyetso vyinshi bishobora gupfungwa mu gucuruza kw’akarorero kamwe, mu gihe nyene bifungura ibimenyetso bishasha. Nkako, ikintu gishimishije c’umurongo wa RGB ni ubushobozi bwawo bwo gupima: inzira nyinshi zishobora guteranirizwa hamwe zigacika mumutekero w'ipinduka, iyo nzira yose ikaba ifatanijwe n’ibabi ridasanzwe ry’igiti ca *MPC* (ikimenyetso kidasanzwe c’umugwi). Kubera uburyo bwa *Deterministic Bitcoin Commitment* (DBC), ubutumwa bwose bwinjizwa mu gisohoka ca `Tapret` canke `Opret`, mu gihe bufunga ibimenyetso vya kera kandi bishoboka ko busobanura ibindi bishasha. `Anchor` ikora nk’ihuriro ry’ukuri hagati y'ukwiyemeza ibitswe muri Blockchain n’imiterere y'ukwmwza kuruhande rw'umuguzi (*uruhande rw’umukiriya*).


Mu bice bikurikira, turaza kuraba ibice vyose n'ingene bigenda mu kwubaka no kwemeza Uko bihinduka. Vyinshi muri ivyobintu biri mu vyo RGB yemeranije, bishirwa mu ngiro mu **Isoko ry’Ibitabo ry’Ishingiro rya RGB**.


### Ukwemeza kw'uko bihinduka

Ku RGB, birashoboka gukoranya Impinduka za Leta zitandukanye ziri mumasezerano imwe (ni ukuvuga gusangira **Ikiranga amasezerano** imwe, ikomoka kwitanguriro **OpId**). Mu buryo bworoshe, nk’uko biri hagati ya Alice na Bob mu karorero kari hejuru, **Umutekero w'impinduka** irimwo inzira imwe gusa. Ariko gushigikira ibikorwa vy’abariha benshi (nk’ama coinjoins, ugufungura imirongo ya Lightning, n’ibindi) bisigura ko abakoresha benshi bashobora gufatanya Impinduka zabo uko bimeze mu mugwi umwe.


Iyo zimaze kwegeranywa, izo mpinduka zishirwako (n’uburyo bwa MPC + DBC) mu gikorwa kimwe ca Bitcoin:




- Uko bizaguhinduka yose irashirwako hashe maze igashirwa mu migwi ikaba Mumutekero w'impinduka;
- Umutekero w'impinduka ubwayo irahashwa maze igashirwa mu ibabi ry’igiti ca MPC rihuye mumasezerano (Ikiranga umutekero);
- Igiti ca MPC gica gikorana na `Opret` canke `Tapret` muri Ukwemeza kw'ihanahanwa, ivyo bikaba bifunga ibimenyetso vyakoreshejwe kandi bikasobanura ibimenyetso bishasha.


Mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, **Ikiranga umutekero** yinjijwe mu rupapuro rwa MPC iboneka ku Hash ikoreshwa ku gukurikirana gukomeye kw'umurima wa *InputMap* w'umugwi:


```txt
BundleId = SHA256( SHA256(bundle_tag) || SHA256(bundle_tag) || InputMap )
```


Mu `umugwi_tag = urn:lnp-bp:RGB:umugwi#2024-02-03` nk'akarorero.


*InputMap* ni urutonde rw'amakuru rutanga urutonde, kuri buri nkuru `i` y'urugero rw'ibikorwa, ivyerekeye *OpId* ya Uko ibihinduka bimeze ihuye. Nk'akarorero:


```txt
InputMap =
N               input_0    OpId(input_0)    input_1    OpId(input_1)   ...    input_N-1  OpId(input_N-1)
|____________________| |_________||______________| |_________||______________|       |__________||_______________|
16-bit Little Endian   32-bit LE   32-byte hash
|_________________________| |_________________________|  ...  |___________________________|

MapElement1                MapElement2                       MapElementN
```




- `N` ni igitigiri cose c'ibintu vyinjijwe mu gucuruza vyerekeye `OpId`;
- opId(input_j)` ni ikimenyetso c'ibikorwa ca kimwe mu bihinduka uko bimeze biri mu mugwi.


Mu gusubiramwo ikintu cose cinjijwe rimwe gusa kandi mu buryo bubereye, turabuza Serire imwe ikoreshwa incuro zibiri mu Nzira zibiri z’uko bimeze zikora icarimwe.


### Gushiraho uko bimeze hamwe n'uko bimeze bikora


Impinduka z'uko bimeze rero zirashobora gukoreshwa mu gukura ukugira ukobi y'umutungo ku muntu umwe ukayijana ku wundi. Ariko rero, si vyo vyonyene bishobora gukorwa mu masezerano ya RGB. Iryo tegeko risobanura ibikorwa bitatu vya **Amasezerano**:




- 792;
- 793;
- 794.


Muri ivyo, **Itanguriro** na **State Extension** rimwe na rimwe vyitwa "*Ibikorwa vyo Guhingura Leta*", kuko bihingura Leta nshasha ata n'imwe ihita ifunga. Iyi ni ingingo ihambaye cane: **Genesis** na **State Extension** ntibirimwo gufunga Seal. Ahubwo, basigura Seal nshasha, itegerezwa rero gukoreshwa n’iyindi **State Transition** ikurikira kugira ngo yemezwe vy’ukuri muri kahise ka Blockchain.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/064.webp)


**Uko bimeze** ivy'amasezerano kenshi biba bisigurwa nk'umugwi w'ibihugu bishasha biva kuri kahise (DAG) k'ihanahanwa, gutangura kw'itanguriro bigakurikira ibishinze mumizi vyose biri muri Blockchain ya Bitcoin. Uko vyari bimeze kwose kera biba vyaravuye kugihe (i.e. zifatanye kugira zikoreshwe ama UTXO) ntizigifatwa nk’izikora, ariko ziguma ari ngirakamaro mu kugenzura ukuntu kahise ihuye.


### Itanguriro


Itanguriro ni intango y'amasezerano ya RGB. Iremwa n'uwayitanga Amasezerano kandi isobanura ibipimo vy'intango, bihuye n' **Igicapo**. Ku bijanye na token ya RGB, Itanguriro ishobora kubivuga neza, akarorero:




- Igitigiri c’ama token yakozwe vy'ukuri n'abayafise;
- Igitigiri cose c’ibibazo bishoboka;
- Amategeko yose yo gusubira gusohora, ayo abayikoresha bashobora gutora.


Kuba  ihanahanwa ryambere mumasezerano, Itanguriro ntakindi citegererezo nakimwe ifise, eka mbere ntaniyindi Serire nimwe yugara. Ariko rero, kugira ngo Itanguriro riboneke muri kahise nakamwe kandi yemerwe, itegerezwa **gukoreshwa** (ipfungwa) n'uko yarimeze imbere  (kenshi ni igikorwa co gucapura/kwikoresha ubwaco ku wuyitanga ubwiwe, canke ugutanga ubwa mbere ku bakoresha).


### Uko bimeze iyongerwako


**Uko bimeze iyongeweko** bitanga ikintu c'umwimerere kuri smart contracts. Bituma bishoboka kwitangira uburenganzira bumwe bumwe bw'ubuhinga bwa none (*Valenties*) buvugwa mu nsobanuro y'amasezerano, ata gufunga Serire ubwo nyene. Akenshi, vyerekeye:




- Ingirane za token zasabikanijwe;
- Uburyo bwo guhindura itunga;
- Gusubira gusohora bifise ivyangombwa (bishobora kubamwo no gusenyura ibindi bintu n’ibindi).


Mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, Uko bimeze iviyongeweko vyerekana *Ukwitanga* (ubwoko bumwe bw’inyungu ya RGB) buhuye na *Valency* yasobanuwe ubuheruka (nk’akarorero, mw'itanguriro canke uwundi uko bimeze ivyongeweko). Isigura Serire nshasha, iboneka ku muntu canke ku kibazo kivyungukirako. Kugira ngo iyo Serire ikore, itegerezwa gukoreshwa n’iyindi ukobimeze ivyongeweko.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/065.webp)


Nk’akarorero: Itanguriro rirema uburenganzira bwo gutanga (*Valency*). Ivyo bishobora gukorwa n’umukinyi yemerewe, aca yubaka uko bimeze ivyongeweko:




- Rivuga igitabu ca Valency (Redeem);
- Irema *Umwimenyerezo* nshasha (amakuru mashasha ya *y'uko bimeze ibifiswe*) yerekana UTXO;
- Uko bimeze ivyongeweko bizoza, isohowe na nyen’iyi UTXO nshasha, mu vy’ukuri izokwimurira canke igatanga ivyo bimenyetso bishasha vyasohowe.


### Ibigizwe n'ibikorwa vy'amasezerano


Ubu rero ndashaka kuraba mu buryo burambuye buri kimwe muduce tugize **Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano** muri RGB. Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano ni igikorwa gihindura uko amasezerano ameze, kandi cemezwa ku ruhande rw’umuguzi, mu buryo bugenwa, n’uwuyironka mu buryo bubereye. Cane cane, turabona ingene Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano ifata mu muzirikanyi, ku ruhande rumwe, **ivya kera** vy'amasezerano, ku rundi ruhande, insobanuro ya **ivya kera** .


```txt
+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
|  Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano                                                                                                 |
|                                                                                                                     |
|  +-----+     +-----------------------+      +--------------------------------+      +---------+     +------------+  |
|  | Ffv |     | Ikoranga amasezerano | Ikiranga igicapo |      | Uko impinduka imeze | Uko ivyiyongerwako bimeze |      | Ivyo ukugerageza |     | AltLayers1 |  |
|  +-----+     +-----------------------+      +--------------------------------+      +---------+     +------------+  |
|                                                                                                                     |
|  +-----------------------------------------------+  +------------------------------------------------------------+  |
|  | Amakuru y'umwimerere                                      |  | Uko bimeze muri rusangi                                              |  |
|  |                                               |  | +----------------------------------+                       |  |
|  | +-------------------------------------+       |  | | +-------------------+ +--------+ |                       |  |
|  | |          Amakuru uko yubatse           |       |  | | | Uko bimeze muri rusangi  | |  Amakuru  | |     ...     ...       |  |
|  | +-------------------------------------+       |  | | +-------------------+ +--------+ |                       |  |
|  |                                               |  | +----------------------------------+                       |  |
|  +-----------------------------------------------+  +------------------------------------------------------------+  |         +------+
|                                                                                                                     +---------> Ikiranga igikorwa |
|  +-----------------------------------------------+  +------------------------------------------------------------+  |         +------+
|  | Ibishirwamwo                                        |  | Imyimenyererezo                                                |  |
|  |                                               |  |                                                            |  |
|  | +-------------------------------------------+ |  | +--------------------------------------------------------+ |  |
|  | | Ibishirwamwo #1                                  | |  | | Umwimenyererezo #1                                          | |  |
+------+       |  | | +----------+ +----------------+ +-------+ | |  | | +----------------+ +-------------+ +-----------------+ | |  |       +--------------+
| Ikiranga igikorwa +--------------> Ibiranga ivyemeza igikorwa | | Ubwoko bw'umwimenyerezo | | Urutonde | | |  | | | Ubwoko bw'umwimenyerezo | | Ukobimeze | | Insiguro ya Serire +--------------> UTXO ya Bitcoin |
+------+       |  | | +----------+ + ---------------+ +-------+ | |  | | +----------------+ +-------------+ +-----------------+ | |  |       +--------------+
|  | +-------------------------------------------+ |  | +--------------------------------------------------------+ |  |
|  |                                               |  |                                                            |  |
|  | +-------------------------------------------+ |  | +--------------------------------------------------------+ |  |
|  | | Ibishirwamwo #2                                  | |  | | Umwimenyerezo #2                                          | |  |
+------+       |  | | +----------+ +----------------+ +-------+ | |  | | +----------------+ +-------------+ +-----------------+ | |  |       +--------------+
| Ikiranga igikorwa +--------------> Ibiranga ivyemeza igikorwa | | Ubwoko bw'umwimenyerezon | | Urutonde | | |  | | | ikieranga umwimenyerezo | | Ukobimeze| | Insiguro ya Serire +--------------> UTXO ya Bitcoin |
+------+       |  | | +----------+ +----------------+ +-------+ | |  | | +----------------+ +-------------+ +-----------------+ | |  |       +--------------+
|  | +-------------------------------------------+ |  | +--------------------------------------------------------+ |  |
|  |                                               |  |                                                            |  |
|  |       ...           ...          ...          |  |     ...          ...             ...                       |  |
|  |                                               |  |                                                            |  |
|  +-----------------------------------------------+  +------------------------------------------------------------+  |
|                                                                                                                     |
|  +-----------------------------------------------+  +------------------------------------------------------------+  |
|  | Ubwitange                                       |  | Valencies                                                  |  |
|  |                                               |  |                                                            |  |
|  | +------------------------------+              |  |                                                            |  |
+------+       |  | | +----------+ +-------------+ |              |  |  +-------------+  +-------------+                          |  |
| Ibiranga igkorwa +--------------> Ibiranga ivyemeza igikorwa | | Ubwoko bwa Valency | |  ...   ...   |  |  | Ubwoko bwa Valency |  | Ubwoko bwa Valency |         ...              |  |
+------+       |  | | +----------+ +-------------+ |              |  |  +-------------+  +-------------+                          |  |
|  | +------------------------------+              |  |                                                            |  |
|  |                                               |  |                                                            |  |
|  +-----------------------------------------------+  +------------------------------------------------------------+  |
|                                                                                                                     |

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
```


Turavye igishushanyo kiri hejuru, turabona ko igikorwa c'amasezerano kirimwo ibintu yerekeza ku **Ibintu bisigaye bimeze** n’izindi zivuga **uko ibintu vyari biri** vyashizwe kugihe.


Ibintu za **v'uko vyahora bimeze** ni:




- **Umwimenyerezo**, muriwo bisiguwe:
 - Ivyo **Insiguro ya Serire**;
 - Ivyo **Uko bimeze bifiswe n'abandi**.
- Ico **Uko bimeze muri rusangi**, bishobora guhindurwa canke bigatunganirizwa;
- **Valencies**, bishobora kuba bisobanuwe muri n'uko bimeze ivyongeweko canke Itanguriro.


**Uko vyaribimeze** vyerekanwa biciye kuri:




- **Ibishirwamwo**, zigaragaza *Ibikorwa* vy'imihindukire y'iko vyari bimeze (ntibiri mw'itanguriro);
- **ukwitanga**, bivugwa ku Valencies zasobanuwe mbere (mu Vy'uko bimeze ivyiyongeweko).


Ikindi, Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano birimwo ibindi bibanza rusangi vyerekeye igikorwa:




- `ffv` (*Verisiyo yihuta*): igitigiri cose c'ama byte 2 cerekana uko amasezerano ameze;
- `Ubwoko Bw'Impinduka` canke `Ubwoko bw'Ukwongerwako`: Umubare w'ibice 16 ugaragaza ubwoko bw'Impinduka canke Ukwaguka, hakurikijwe uko ishoramari rimeze;
- `Id y'amasezerano`: umubare w'amabayiti 32 yerekeye *OpId* y'amasezerano y'itanguriro. Ishizwe mu Nzira z’Impinduka n’Ivyagutse, ariko ntiziri mw'itanguriro;
- schemaId: iri mw'itanguriro gusa, iyi ni Hash y'amabayite 32 iserukira imiterere (*Schema*) y'amasezerano;
- `Testnet`: Igiharuro kigaragaza nimba uri ku rubuga rwa Testnet canke Mainnet. Itanguriro gusa;
- `altlayers1`: umuhinduzi ugaragaza ubundi buryo Layer (Sidechain canke ubundi) bukoreshwa ku makuru ya Anchor yongerako Bitcoin. Iriho gusa mw'itanguriro;
- `metadata`: umwanya ushobora kubika amakuru y'igihe gito, ngirakamaro mu kwemeza amasezerano igoye, ariko udategerezwa kwandikwa mu mateka y'imimerere ya nyuma.


Ubwa nyuma, ivyo bibanza vyose bihurizwa hamwe n'uburyo bwo gukora hashing, kugira ngo bivemwo ikimenyetso c'urutoke kidasanzwe, `OpId`. Iyi `OpId` ica ishirwa muri Umutekero w'impinduka, igatuma ishobora kwemezwa no kwemezwa murukwirikirane.


Buri *Gikorwa c'amasezerano* rero imenyekana n'igice ca Hash c'ama byte 32 citwa `OpId`. Iyi Hash ibarwa n’i SHA256 Hash y’uduce twose igize igikorwa. Mu yandi majambo, *Igikorwa c'amasezerano* yose irafise ukwiyemeza yayo y’ibanga, irimwo amakuru yose akenewe kugira ngo umuntu asuzume ukuri n’uko igikorwa gihuye.


Amasezerano ya RGB rero amenyekana na `ContractId`, ikomoka kw'itanguriro `OpId` (kubera ko ata gikorwa c’imbere y'itanguriro). Mu majambo nyayo, dufata Itanguriro `OpId`, tugahindura urutonde rwa byte maze tugakoresha ubuhinga bwa Base58. Ivyo bituma `ContractId` yoroha gukoresha no kumenya.

### Uburyo bwo kuvugurura ivyangombwa n'amabwirizwa


**Uko amasezerano ameze** igereranya amakuru yose umurongo wa RGB utegerezwa gukurikirana kumasezerano. Igizwe na:




- **Uko bimeze murirsangi** imwe: iki ni igice c'amasezerano ca bose, co kw'isi yose, kiboneka kuri bose;
- Uko bimeze kimwe canke vyinshi vy'Umutungo: **Owned State** yose ifatanye n'iyindi Serire yihariye (kandi rero UTXO kuri Bitcoin). Hariho itandukaniro hagati ya:
    - Uko bimeze **kuri bose**,
    - Uko bimeze **ivy’abikorera ku giti cabo**.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/066.webp)


*Uko bimeze muri rusangi* ishirwa ataco ihinduye muri *Igikorwa c'amasezerano* nk'igice kimwe. *Ibihugu vy'Umutungo* bisobanurwa muri *Umwimenyerezo* wose, iruhande ya *insiguro ya Serire*.


Ikintu nyamukuru kiranga RGB ni uburyo Uko bimeze muri rusangi n’Ibihugu vy’Igihugu bihindurwa. Muri rusangi hari ubwoko bubiri bw'inyifato:




- **Ihinduka**: iyo ikintu c'uko bimeze bidondowe nk'ibihinduka, igikorwa gishasha cose gisubirira uko vyaribimeze ivya kera n'uko bimeze ivyubu. Amakuru ya kera rero abonwa ko ataco amaze;
- **Kwirundanira**: iyo ikintu c'intara gisobanuwe nk'ikirundanira, igikorwa gishasha cose congera amakuru mashasha ku ntara y'imbere, ata kwandikako. Ico bivamwo ni ubwoko bw'amateka yirundanijwe.


Iyo, muma sezerano, ikintu c'uko bimeze bidasiguwe nk'igihinduka canke gitera, ico kintu kizoguma ari ubusa ku bikorwa bikurikira (mu yandi majambo, nta verisiyo nshasha z'iki kibanza). N'igicapo c'amasezerano (i.e. Uko ishoramari ifise kode) igena nimba Leta (Isi yose canke Iy’Umuntu) ihinduka, ishobora kwirundanira canke idahinduka. Igihe itanguriro imaze gusobanurwamwo, ivyo bishobora guhindurwa gusa iyo Amasezerano ubwayo abirekuriye, nk'akarorero biciye kukw'iyongerako ukobimeze yihariye.


Imbonerahamwe iri musi yerekana ingene ubwoko bumwebumwe bwa Contract Operation bushobora gukoresha (canke kutakoresha) Global State na Owned State:


|                                           | Itanguriro | Uko bimeze ivyongeweko | Uko bimeze ivyongeweko |
| ---------------------------- |:-----:     |:---------: |:--------------: |
| **Ivyongegwako kuko bimeze muri rusangi** |    +       |        -        |        +         |
| **Ivyinguruza kuko bimeze muri rusangi**  |   n/a      |        -        |        +         |
| **Ivyongerwako ukobimeze ibifiswe**       |    +       |        -        |        +         |
| **Ivyiguruza ukobimeze ibifiswe**         |   n/a      |       No        |        +         |
| **Ivyiyongerako kuri  Valencies**         |    +       |        +        |        +         |


**`+`**: igikorwa gishoboka iyo Igicapo c'amasezerano kibirekuriye.


**`-`**: igikorwa kigomba kwemezwa na Ibihinduka uko bimeze ikurikira (Ivyongerwako kukobimeze vyonyene ntivyugara Serire ikoreshwa rimwe).


Ikindi, urugero rw’igihe n’uburenganzira bwo guhindura ubwoko bumwebumwe bw’amakuru birashobora gutandukanywa mu mbonerahamwe ikurikira:


|                        | Amakuruy'imitererere                               | Uko bimeze murirusangi                                     | Ibifiswe uko bimeze                                                                                              |
| ---------------------- | --------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------ | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Ahobikorerwa**              | Bisigura kubikorwa vy'isezerano | Bisugura murirusangi amasezerano                | Bisigura kuri buri Serire  (*Umwimenyerezo*)                                                                     |
| **Ninde ashobora kubishira kugihe?** | Ntishobora gushirwa kugihe (Aamakuru afise ahoaherera)          | Igikorwa catanzwe n'abakozi  (Uwutanga, n'ibindi.)        | Bivanye nabemerewe kubitunga bafise Serire (Umwe ashobora kubitanga mwihanahanwa rikurikira) |
| **Aho bikorerwa vy'infatakibanza**     | Gusa kugikorwa kiriko kiraba          | Uko bimeze bishirwa kumpera y'igikorwa | Ukobimeze bisigurwa imbere y'igikorwa (Imbere *y'insiguro ya Serire* Y'ibikorwa biheruka)               |


### Uko bimeze murirusangi


Uko bimeze muri rusangi akenshi idondorwa ngo "nta n'umwe ayifise, bose barabizi". Irimwo amakuru rusangi yerekeye Aamasezerano, ikaba iboneka ku mugaragaro. Nk’akarorero, mumasezerano atanga token, birashoboka ko irimwo:




- Igiharuro (indome ngufi y’ikigereranyo ya token): `igiharuro`;
- Izina ryose rya token: `izina`;
- Ugushikama (Igitigiri c'ibibanza vy'icumi): `ugushikama`;
- Ivyo gutanga vya mbere (na/canke umupaka w’agaciro kanini wa token): `Itangazwa`;
- Itariki y'isohoka: `yaremwe`;
- Amakuru y'amategeko canke ayandi makuru ya bose: `amakuru`.


Uko bimee murirusangi bishobora gushirwa ku bikoresho vya bose (imbuga ngurukanabumenyi, IPFS, Nostr, Torrent, n’ibindi) igashikirizwa abantu bose. Kandi, inguvu z’ubutunzi (ugukenera gufata no gutanga ivyo bimenyetso, n’ibindi) ni vyo bituma abakoresha Amasezerano bo ubwabo babungabunga no gukwiragiza ayo makuru.


### Ibikorwa


*Umwimenyerezo* ni umubumbe w'ishimikiro wo gusigura:




- Igikoresho ca Serire (*Igikoresho c'insiguro ya Serire*), kigaragaza igikoresho ca UTXO kidasanzwe;
- *Uko bimeze*, ni ukuvuga umutungo canke amakuru ajanye n'iyi Serire.


*Umwimenyerezo* ushobora kubonwa nk’ikigereranyo c’igisohoka c’ugucuruza ca Bitcoin, ariko ikaba ifise ubushobozi bwo guhinduranya. Aha niho hari uburyo bwo kwimurira umutungo: *Umwimenyerezo* Ufatanya ubwoko bumwe bw'umutungo canke uburenganzira (`Ubwoko bw'Igikorwa`) na Serire. Uwufise urufunguzo rw’ibanga rwa UTXO rufatanye n’iyi Serire (canke uwushobora gukoresha iyi UTXO) afatwa ko ari nyen’iyi *Owned State*.


Kimwe mu bintu bikomeye bikomeye vya RGB ni ubushobozi bwo *guhishura* canke guhisha (*guhisha*) imirima ya *Insiguroya Serire* na *Uko bimeze birimuminwe y'abantu* uko ushaka. Ivyo bitanga uruvange rukomeye rw’ibanga n’uguhitamwo. Nk’akarorero, urashobora kwemeza ko ihinduka rifise akamaro ata makuru yose utangaje, mu gutanga verisiyo yahishuriwe ku muntu ategerezwa kuyishingira intahe, mu gihe abandi bantu babona gusa verisiyo yihishije (Hash). Mu bikorwa, `OpId` y'ihinduka yama ibarwa ivuye ku makuru *hishijwe*.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/067.webp)


#### Insiguro ya Serire


*Insiguro ya Serire*, mu buryo bwayo bwahishuriwe, ifise ivyicaro bine vy'ishimikiro: `txptr`, `vout`, `uguhuma` na `uburyo`:




- **txptr**: ibi ni ivyerekeye UTXO kuri Bitcoin:
    - Ku bijanye n’indege **Itanguriro rya Serire**, yerekana ata guca ku ruhande UTXO iriho (iyo ifatanye n’iyo Tanguriro);
    - Mu gihe c'**Igishushanyo c'iserire**, dushobora kugira:
        - `txid` yoroshe, iyo yerekana UTXO yihariye,
        - Canke `WitnessTx`, yerekana ikintu umuntu yishingirako: Serire yerekana igikorwa ubwaco. Ivyo birakenewe cane cane iyo ata UTXO yo hanze iriho, nk'akarorero mu gufungura umurongo wa Lightning, canke iyo uwuronka ata UTXO afise.
- **vout**: umubare w'isohoka ry'ibikorwa vyerekanywe na `txptr`. Itangazwa gusa ku gishushanyo gisanzwe Serire (si ku `IcabonaTx`);
- **blinding**: umubare w'ibintu 8 vy'ibanga, kugira ngo hakomezwe ibanga no kubuza gukoresha inguvu z'agahomerabunwa ku bijanye n'akaranga ka UTXO;
- **uburyo**: yerekana uburyo bwo gushingira intahe bukoreshwa (`Tapret` canke `Opret`).


Igishushanyo *cahishijwe* c'insiguro ya Serire ni SHA256 Hash (gifise ikimenyetso) c'uguhuza ivyo bibanza 4, gifise ikimenyetso kidasanzwe kuri RGB.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/068.webp)


#### Uko bimeze bifashwe muminwe


Igice ca kabiri ca *Umwimenyerezo* n'uko bimeze biri muminwe y'uwundi. Udakunze Ukobimeze muri rusangi, ishobora kubaho mu buryo bwa bose canke bw’abantu ku giti cabo:




- **Uko bimeze bifashwe muminwe ya bose**: umuntu wese arazi amakuru ajanye na Serire. Nk'akarorero, ishusho y'abantu bose;
- **Ukobimeze bifashwe muminwe vy'abigenga**: amakuru aranyegezwa, amenyekana gusa na nyen'ayo makuru (kandi bishoboka ko ari uwuyashingira intahe iyo bikenewe). Nk'akarorero, igitigiri c'ibimenyetso bifise.


RGB isobanura ubwoko bune bw'intara bushoboka (*UbwokoBw'intara*) bw'uk bimeze bifashwe muminwe:




- **Itangazo**: nta makuru y'ibiharuro arimwo, uburenganzira bwo gutangaza gusa (nk'uburenganzira bwo gutora). Ivyo bihishijwe n'ivyo bihishuwe birasa;
- **Iyishibotra gusubirirwa**: igereranya igitigiri gshobora guhinduka (nk'ibimenyetso). Mu buryo bwahishuriwe, dufise `igiaruro` n'`uguhuma`. Mu buryo bwihishije, dufise *ukwiyemeza kwa Perdersen* imwe ihisha igitigiri n'uguhuma amaso;
- **Itunganijwe**: ibika amakuru atunganijwe (gushika kuri 64 kB). Mu buryo bwahishuriwe, mu biharuro blob. Mu buryo bwihishije, ni Hash y'iki gice:


```txt
SHA-256(SHA-256(tag_data) || SHA-256(tag_data) || blob)
```


Na, nk'akarorero:


```txt
tag_data = urn:lnp-bp:rgb:state-data#2024-02-12
```




- **Ivyashizweko**: bihuza dosiye (amajwi, ishusho, bibiri, n'ibindi) na Ibifiswe muminwe, bikabika dosiye Hash `file_hash`, ubwoko bwa MIME `ubwoko bw'amakuru` n'umunyu w'ibanga `umunyu`. Dosiye ubwayo iracumbikirwa ahandi. Mu buryo bwihishije, ni Hash ifise ikimenyetso c'ibintu bitatu bibanza:


```txt
SHA-256(SHA-256(tag_attachment) || SHA-256(tag_attachment) || file_hash || media_type || salt)
```


Na, nk'akarorero:


```txt
tag_attachment = urn:rgb:state-attach#2024-02-12
```


Mu ncamake, ng’ubu ubwoko 4 bushoboka bwa Leta mu buryo bwa bose no mu buryo bwihishije:


```txt
Uko bimeze                      Aho kwuzuza hanyegejwe                              Aho kwuzuza haboneka

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
|                                                                                |
Ukwemanga        |                              < Ugugahakana >                                          |
|                                                                                |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

+--------------------------+             +---------------------------------------+
| +----------------------+ |             |         +--------+ +----------+       |
Ishobora guhinduka           | | Ukwiyemeza kwa Pedersen | | <========== |         | Igitigiri | | Umuvuduko |       |
| +----------------------+ |             |         +--------+ +----------+       |
+--------------------------+             +---------------------------------------+

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

+--------------------------+             +---------------------------------------+
| +----------------------+ |             |         +--------------------+        |
Inyubako         | |     Hash yahiswemwo     | | <========== |         |     amakuru ya Blob      |        |
| +----------------------+ |             |         +--------------------+        |
+--------------------------+             +---------------------------------------+

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

+--------------------------+             +---------------------------------------+
| +----------------------+ |             | +-----------+ +------------+ +------+ |
Ibifadikanije        | |     Hash yahiswemwo      | | <========== | | dokima ya Hash | | Uboko bw'ikinyamakuru | | Akabirya | |
| +----------------------+ |             | +-----------+ +------------+ +------+ |

+--------------------------+             +---------------------------------------+

```



| **Ikintu**     | **Ukwemanga** | **Ishobora guhinduka**                      | **Inyubako**       | **Iyifadikanijwe**        |
| --------------- | --------------- | --------------------------------- | -------------------- | ---------------------- |
| **Ibiharuro**        | ntanimwe            | Iyateweko umukono or Iyitateweko umukono 64-bit integer | Ubwoko bw'ibiharuro ivyarivyo vyose | Dokima yariyo yose              |
| **Ubwoko bw'amakuru**   | Oya           | Bwateweko umukono canke butateweko umukono                | Ubwoko bumeze uko         | MIME Type              |
| **Ibanga**     | Ntikenewe    | Pedersen commitment               | Hash with blinding   | Hashed file identifier |
| **Urugero rw;'uko ingana** | N/A             | Ama bytes 256                         | Gushika kuri 64 KB          | Gushika kuri ~500 GB          |


### Injiza


Ibija mu *Bikorwa vy'amasezerano* vyerekeye *Ibikorwa* biriko birakoreshwa muri iki gikorwa gishasha. Injiza yerekana:




- `prevOpId`: ikimenyetso (`OpId`) c'igikorwa c'imbere aho *Umwimenyerezo* yari;
- `UbwokoBw'Igikorwa`: ubwoko bwa *Umwimenyerezpo* (nk'akarorero, `Nyitungo` ku token);
- `Index`: urutonde rw' *Umwimenyerezo* ruri ku rutonde rujanye n'i `OpId` y'imbere, rugenwa inyuma y'ugutoranya kw'inkoranyabumenyi kw'ibimenyetso vyihishijwe.


Ivyinjira ntivyigera biboneka mw'itanguriro, kuko ata Mirimo y’imbere iriho. Eka mbere ntiziboneka mu Vyagutse vy'uko bimeze (kuko Ivyagutse vy'uko bimeze bitafunga ibimenyetso; ahubwo, bisubira gusobanura ibimenyetso bishasha bishingiye ku Valencies).


Iyo dufise Uko bimeze bifashwe muminwe  z’ubwoko `Bushobora guhinduka`, ubuhinga bwo kwemeza (biciye mu nyandiko ya AluVM itangwa mugicapo) burasuzuma ukuntu imibare ihuye: umubare w’ibimenyetso vyinjira (*Ivyinjizwa*) utegerezwa kuba ungana n’umubare w’ibimenyetso bisohoka (mu *As* nshasha).


### Amakuru


**Ubwoko bw'amakuru y'biharuro** Murubuga ishobora gushika kuri 64 KiB kandi ikoreshwa mu gushiramwo amakuru y'igihe gito ngirakamaro mu kwemeza, ariko ntashizwe mu gihe c'ubudasiba c'amasezerano Nk'akarorero, ibihinduka vy'imibare yo hagati y'inyandiko zikomeye birashobora kubikwa hano. Ico kibanza ntikigenewe kubikwa mu mateka y'isi yose, ni co gituma kiri hanze y'ububasha bw'Ibihugu vy'Igihugu canke Uko bimeze muri rusangi.


### Ivyiza


**Ivyiyumviro** ni uburyo bw'umwimerere bw'amasezerano ya RGB. Bishobora gusangwa mw'itanguriro, Impinduka z'iko bimeze canke Impinduka z'iko biri. Bigereranya uburenganzira bw’imibare bushobora gukoreshwa na Iyongengwa ry'uko imeze (biciye muri *Redeems*), hanyuma bikarangizwa n’Impinduka ikurikira. Buri Valency imenyekana n'`UbwokoBw'Uburemere` (ibice 16). Insobanuro yayo (uburenganzira bwo gusubira gusohora, guhindura token, uburenganzira bwo guturira, n'ibindi) zisobanurwa murico gicapo.


Mu majambo nyayo, twoshobora kwiyumvira Itanguriro isobanura "uburenganzira bwo gusubira gusohora" Valency. Ukwongerako ukobimeze izoyirya (*Redeem*) iyo hari ibintu bimwe bimwe bishitse, kugira ngo haboneke umubare mushasha w’ibimenyetso. Hanyuma, Uko bimeze vyongerwako iva ku wufise Serire yaremwe gutyo irashobora kwimurira ivyo bimenyetso bishasha.


### Gucungura


Ivyo gucungura ni Valency bingana n’Ivyinjira mu bikorwa. Biboneka gusa mu Vyagutse vy'uko bimeze, kuko ni ho Valency yari yarasobanuwe mbere ikoreshwa. Redeem igizwe n’ibice bibiri:




- `PrevOpId`: `OpId` y'igikorwa aho Valency yari yaravuzwe;
- `UbwokoBw'Ubushobozi`: ubwoko bwa Valency wipfuza gukoresha (buri `UbwokoBw'Ubushobozi` bushobora gukoreshwa rimwe gusa na Uko bimeze ivyongerwako).


Akarorero: Redeem ishobora guhura n'ugushirwa mu ngiro kwa CoinSwap, bivanye n'ivyo vyari vyashizwe muri Valency.


### Ibiranga ikibanza ca RGB


Ubu tugiye kuraba ibiranga Uko bimeze vyinshi vy'ishimikiro muri RGB. Cane cane, turaza kuraba:




- **Uburyo bw’ubwoko bukomeye**, butegeka gutunganya amakuru mu buryo bubereye kandi bufise ubwoko;
- Akamaro ko gutandukanya **kwemeza** na **Ukuvyitirirwa**;
- Uburyo bwa **ugutera imbere kw'uguhurizako** muri RGB, burimwo ivyiyumviro vy'*ugutera imbere vyihuta* n'*ugusubira inyuma*.


Nk’uko bisanzwe, uzirikane ko ikintu cose gifitaniye isano n’ivy’uburenganzira bw'amasezerano cemezwa ku ruhande rw’umuguzi hakurikijwe amategeko y’uguhurizako ashizweho mu masezerano, kandi ko ishingiro ryayo ry’iherezo ry’ubuhinga bwa none rishingiye ku bikorwa vya Bitcoin.


#### Ubwoko bukomeye


RGB ikoresha *Ubwoko bukomeye* n'uburyo bwo gukurikirana (*Ugushiramwo amakode bikomeye*). Iryo shirahamwe ryagenewe gutuma amakuru y'amasezerano ashobora gusubirwamwo neza kandi akagira ukuri mu gusigura, agafita kandiakemeza amasezerano ashingiye kubiharuro.


Mu bice vyinshi v'ama porogaramu (JSON, YAML...), imiterere y’amakuru irashobora guhinduka, mbere n’ugushobora kwemera cane. Ku rundi ruhande, muri RGB, Imiterere y'uko urubuga bisigurwaamwo ibintu bigaragara. Nk'akarorero:




- Ihinduka ryose rifise ubwoko bwihariye (nk'akarorero, igiharuro c'ibice 8 udafise ikimenyetso `u8`, canke igiharuro c'ibice 16 gifise ikimenyetso, n'ibindi);
- Ubwoko burashobora kugirwa (ubwoko bushizwemwo). Ibi bisigura ko ushobora gusobanura ubwoko bushingiye ku bundi bwoko (nk'ubwoko bw'umugwi burimwo umwanya `u8`, umwanya `bool`, n'ibindi);
- Amakoraniro arashobora kandi gusigurwa atandukaniye: kurutonde (*urutonde*), kumirwi (*kumirwi*) canke kuri zikazinduzi (*indanga merekero*), n'urutonde rw'iterambere ry'ibintu;
- Buri rubuga urafise urubibi (*urubibi rwo hasi* / *urubibi rwo hejuru*). Turashiraho kandi imipaka ku mubare w’ibintu mu makoraniro (ugukingira);
- Amakuru ni byte ashizwe kumurongo kandi urutonde rurasobanuwe neza kandi atakwihenda kurimwo.


Bivuye kuri porotokole y'ugushiramwo ama kode:




- Urutonde rw’ibibanza rwama ari rumwe, tutitayeho ugushirwa mungiro canke ubuhinga bwa porogaramation bwakoreshejwe;
- Hash yaharuwe ku rutonde rumwe rero birashobora gusubirwamwo kandi birasa (*imihigo* y’ugushingira intahe);
- Imipaka ibuza iterambere ritagenzuwe mu bunini bw’amakuru (nk’akarorero, imbuga nyishi cane);
- Ubwo buryo bwo gushiramwo ama kode butuma hashoboka gusuzuma bikoresheje inyandiko zinyegeje, kuko umwe wese mu bari muri iyo nyigisho azi neza ingene yoshiramwo amakuru mu rutonde no gukora Hash.


Mu bikorwa, inyubako (*Igicapo*) n’ikode rivamwo (*Uruhande tubona twese* n’urukwirikirane bijanye) birashirwa hamwe. Ururimi rudondora rukoreshwa mu gusigira ano masezerano (ubwoko, urubuga, amategeko) rukazana kandi uburyo bukomeye bw’ibice bibiri. Iyo bishizwe hamwe, inyishu ni:




- *Ikibanza ca nyabwonko* kuri buri rubuga;
- Ivyerekana insiguro (vyerekana nimba guhindura izina ry’igihinduka bifise ingaruka ku nsiguro, naho nyene inyubako ya nyabwonko iguma iri kwakundi).


Uburyo bw’ubwoko bukomeye kandi burashoboza gukurikirana neza amahinduka: uguhindura kwose kw’uko imeze (naho iba impinduka kugice c'izina ) kuramenyekana kandi gushobora gutuma haba uguhinduka kw’ikirenge cose.


Ubwa nyuma, ihuriro ryose ritanga ikimenyetso c’urutoke, ikimenyetso c’ibanga gishingira intahe kuburyo nyabwo y’iyo kode (amakuru, amategeko, ukwemeza). Akarorero, ikimenyetso c'aho kwuzuza:


```txt
BEiLYE-am9WhTW1-oK8cpvw4-FEMtzMrf-mKocuGZn-qWK6YF#ginger-parking-nirvana
```


Ivyo bituma bishoboka gucunga ivyagezwe vy’uguhurizako canke ivy’ugushirwa mu ngiro, mu gihe bishoboka ko umuntu ashobora gukurikirana mu buryo burambuye amaverisiyo akoreshwa mu rubuga.


Mukwirindako amasezerano ya RGB kugirango  ntagore cane ku ruhande rw’umuguzi, amategeko y'ibihano aratanga urugero ntarengwako mukuja musi ari `2^16` bytes (64 Kio) ku makuru yose ari mu biharuro vy’ukwemeza. Bino bikoreshwa kuri buri biharuro canke inyubako: ntibirenze ama bytes 65536, canke ivyo bingana mubiharuro (32768 16-bit integers, n’ibindi). Ivyo birakoreshwa kandi kwishirwa hamwe (urutonde, imigwi, indanga merekero), bidashobora kurenga imice `2^16`.


Iyi nzira iremeza:




- Igenzura ubunini butarengwako ubw’amakuru azokoreshwa mu gihe c'uko ihinduka rimeze;
- Uguhuza n'imashini y'ikorera kuri ngurkana bumenyi (*AluVM*) ikoreshwa mu gukoresha inyandiko zo kwemeza.


#### Ivyemezo != Ingendo ngenderwako z'ugutunga ibintu


Kimwe mu bintu bikomeye RGB yakoze ni ugutandukanya cane ivyiyumviro bibiri:




- **Kwemeza**: gusuzuma uko impinduka imeze bikwirikiza mategeko y;amasezerano (Uko ishoramari rimeze, kahise, n'ibindi);
- **Ukwitirirwa ibintu** (Ukwitirirwa ibintu, canke ubugenzuzi): ukuri ko umuntu afise Bitcoin UTXO ishobora gutuma Uwukoresa Serire ikoreshwa rimwe ikoreshwa (canke igafungwa), gutyo uko ihinduka rimeze rigafata ikibanza.


**Ukwemeza** bibera ku rugero rw'ikirundo ca nyabwonko zirikuri RGB (Ububiko bw'inyandiko, *amasezerano*, n'ibindi). Uruhara rwayo ni ugutuma amategeko y'indani mu masezerano (Igitigiri, uruhusha n’ibindi) yubahirizwa. Abarorerezi canke abandi bari muri iyo nama na bo nyene barashobora kwemeza kahise k'inyandiko.


**Ukwitirirwa ikintu**, ku rundi ruhande, yizigiye gusa umutekano wa Bitcoin. Kugira urufunguzo rw’ibanga rwa UTXO bisigura kugenzura ubushobozi bwo gutanguza ihinduka rishasha (kwugara Serire ikoreshwa rimwe). Rero, naho umuntu yoshobora kubona canke kwemeza amakuru, ntashobora guhindura Leta iyo atagira UTXO ireba.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/069.webp)


buno buryo buragabanya ubukomezi buke buhura muri Blockchain zigoye (aho amakode yose ya Smart contract ari kukarunda kandi agashobora guhindurwa na burimuntu, ibitumwa rimwe narimwe vyerekeza kukwibwa). Ku RGB, uwutera ntashobora gusa gukorana nuko On-chain imeze, kuko uburenganzira bwo gukora kuri Leta (*Ukwitirirwa ikintu*) burindwa na Layer ya Bitcoin.


Iciyongerako ni, uku gutandukanya bituma RGB ishobora kwifatanya na Lightning Network. Imirongo y’umuravyo ishobora gukoreshwa mu gukorana no kwimurira ivy’ubutunzi vya RGB ata gukorana n’*imihigo* ya On-Chain igihe cose. Tuzokwihweza neza uku gushiramwo RGB ku Muravyo mubigabane bizokurikira vy’icigwa.


#### Iterambere ry'uko bigenda muri RGB


Uretse guhindura kode y’insiguro, RGB irimwo uburyo bwo guhindura canke guhindura amategeko y’uguhurizako ya Contract uko igihe kigenda kirarenga. Hari uburyo bubiri nyamukuru bw'iterambere:




- **Gutera imbere**
- **Gusubira inyuma**


Ugutera imbere bituma iyo itegeko ryari ritagira akamaro mbere rigira akamaro. Nk'akarorero, iyo rino Sezerano rihinduka kugira ngo yemere ubwoko bushasha bw' `Ubwoko bw'imyimenyerezo` canke umwanya mushasha:




- Ivyo ntibishobora kugereranywa n’ivyuma bikomeye vya kera vya Blockchain, kuko RGB ikora kuruhande rw'ukwemeza rw'umuguzi kandi ntigira ico ikoze ku bijanye n’uguhuza muri rusangi kwa Blockchain;
- Mubikorwa, ubwo bwoko bw’ihinduka bugaragazwa n’umwanya `Ffv` (*verisiyo y’imbere yihuta*) kurubuga rw'ibikorwa vy'amasezerano;
- Abafise ubu ntibagirirwa nabi: ikibanza cabo kiguma cemewe;
- Abaronse vuba(Canke abasigaye bakoresha), mukindi gice, bakeneye gushira kugihe inyabwonko zabo(Ingodo zabo) kugirango bamenye amategeko mashasha.


Gusubira inyuma bisigura ko itegeko ryari rifise akamaro mbere rihinduka ubusa. Ni rero "ugukomantaza" amategeko, ariko si mu kuvuga ataco twishimikije:




- Abafise ivy’ubutunzi bariho bashobora gushikirwa n’ingorane (boshobora kwisanga bafise ivy’ubutunzi vyahinduwe bitagira akamaro canke bitagira akamaro muri verisiyo nshasha);
- Turashobora kubona ko mu vy’ukuri turiko turarema umurongo mushasha: uwuzokwemera itegeko rishasha aca ava ku rya kera;
- Uwutanga ashobora gufata ingingo yo gusubira gutanga itunga muri iyo porotokole nshasha, agahatira abakoresha kuguma bafise ingodo abiri atandukanye (imwe y’iporotokole ya kera, iyindi y’iyindi nshasha), nimba bashaka gucunga ubwo bwoko bwose.


Muri iki gice kivuga ku bikorwa vy'amasezerano ya RGB, twasuzumye ingingo ngenderwako z’ishimikiro zishingiye kuri iyi porotokole. Nk’uko muzoba mwabibonye, ​​ukuntu umurongo wa RGB ugoranye cane bisaba ko hakoreshwa amajambo menshi y’ubuhinga. Rero, mu kigabane gikurikira, nzobaha urutonde rw'amajambo ruzoca irya n'ino ivyiyumviro vyose bivugwa muri iki gice ca mbere c'inyigisho, n'insobanuro z'amajambo yose y'ubuhinga yerekeye RGB. Hanyuma, mu gice gikurikira, tuzokwihweza mu buryo ngirakamaro insobanuro n’ugushirwa mu ngiro kw’amasezerano ya RGB.


## RGB Insobanuro y'amajambo


<chapterId>545e16a4-3cca-44a3-9fd5-dbc5868abf97</chapterId>


Nimba ukeneye kugaruka muri uru rutonde rugufi rw’amajambo y’ubuhinga ahambaye akoreshwa mw’isi ya RGB (yashizwe ku rutonde rw’indome), uzosanga ari ngirakamaro. Iki gice si ngombwa nimba umaze gutahura ivyo twavuze vyose mu gice ca mbere.


#### AluVM


Indome ngufi AluVM ihagarariye "_Imashini y'ubuhinga bwa none_", imashini y'ubuhinga bwa none ishingiye ku nzira y'ubuhinga bwa none yagenewe kwemeza Smart contract no gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none. Ikoreshwa (ariko ntiyihariye gusa) mu kwemeza amasezerano ya RGB. Ivyanditswe canke ibikorwa biri mu masezerano ya RGB birashobora rero gukorwa mu bidukikije vya AluVM.


Ushaka kumenya vyinshi: [Urubuga rwemewe rwa AluVM]


#### Aho bishingiye


Aho bishingiye hagereranya urutonde rw'amakuru y'uruhande rw'umuguzi akoreshwa mu kwemeza ko hariho _ukwiyemeza_ kwihariye mu gucuruza. Mu masezerano ya RGB, Aho bishingiye hagizwe nibi bikwirikira:




- Igiharuro c’ibikorwa vy’ubudandaji (txid) c’i **Ihanahanwa ry'icabona**;
- Ivyo **Multi Protocol Commitment (MPC)**;
- Ivyo **Igitabu-1058 (DBC)**;
- **Extra Transaction Proof  (ETP)** iyo uburyo bwa **Tapret** Ubuhinga bw'ukwiyemeza burakoreshwa (raba igice kigenewe iki kigereranyo).


Aho bishingiye rero hakoreshwa mu gushinga isano rishobora kugenzurwa hagati y’ugucuruza kwihariye kwa Bitcoin n’amakuru y’ibanga yemejwe n’amasezerano ya RGB. Biremeza ko ayo makuru ari muri Blockchain vy’ukuri, ata vyo arimwo vy’ukuri bimenyeshwa abantu bose.


#### Umwimenyerezo


Mu nzira ya RGB, Umwimenyerezo ni nk'inyishu y'ibikorwa bihindura, bihindura canke bikora ibintu bimwe bimwe mu gihe c'amasezerano. Igikoresho c'umwimenyerezo gifise ama ibintu bibiri :




- **Insiguro ya serire** (ivyerekeye UTXO yihariye);
- **Uko bimeze ibiri muminwe y'umuntu** (amakuru asigura uko bimeze arikumwe n'umuntu ayifise).


Umwimenyerezo rero werekana uko igice kimeze (nk’akarorero, umutungo) aha ushirwa kuwundi muntuubu gihabwa uwufise, kimenyekana biciye kuri serire ikoreshwa rimwe na UTXO.


#### Uko ishoramari rimeze


Ishora mari uko rimeze rihuriza hamwe amategeko yose n’imikorere yo mu mutima y'amasezerano, idondorwa n' **Ibicapo** yayo (ni ukuvuga uko amasezerano ameze ). Irategeka ingene igihugu c'amasezerano gishobora guhinduka, kandi mu bihe ibihe.


#### Uruhande rw'ukemeza rw'umuguzi


Uruhande rw'ukwemeza rw'umuguzi rwerekana uburyo buri ruhande (umukiriya) asuzuma urutonde rw’amakuru ahindurwa mu bwiherero, hakurikijwe amategeko y’amasezerano. Ku bijanye na RGB, ayo makuru yahinduwe ashirwa hamwe mu vyo bita **ibirungikwa**. Udakunze umurongo wa Bitcoin, usaba ko amafaranga yose akoreshwa atangazwa kuri On-Chain, RGB yemera gusa _imigambi_ (ishingiye kuri Bitcoin) kubikwa mu ruhame, mu gihe amakuru y'ingenzi y'amasezerano asigaye hagati ya On-Chain, ibimenyamenya gusa) ivyerekeye.


#### Ukwiyemeza


Ukwiyemeza (mu buryo bw'ibanga) ni ikintu c'ibiharuro, kigaragazwa na `C`, kiva ku gikorwa ku makuru atunganijwe `m` (ubutumwa) n'agaciro k'imburakimazi `r`. Twandika:


$$
C = \text{commit}(m, r)
$$


Ubu buryo bugizwe n'ibikorwa bibiri nyamukuru:




- **kwemeza**: igikorwa c'ibanga gikoreshwa ku butumwa `m` n'umubare w'imburakimazi `r` kugira ngo uvemwo `C`;
- **Gusuzuma**: dukoresha `C`, ubutumwa `m` n'agaciro ka `r` kugira ngo tugenzure ko iyi Ukwiyemeza ari ukuri. Igikorwa kigarura `Ukuri` canke `Ikinyoma`.


Ukwiyemeza gutegerezwa itegerezwa kwubahiriza ibintu bibiri:




- **Binding**: bitegerezwa kuba bidashoboka kuronka ubutumwa bubiri butandukanye butanga `C` imwe:


$$
m': \, | \,: m' \neq m \quad \text{and} \quad r': \, | \,: r' \neq r \quad
$$


Nka nka:


$$
\text{verify}(m, r, C) = \text{verify}(m', r', C) \rightarrow \text{True}
$$




- **Hiding**: ubumenyi bwa `C` ntibutegerezwa guhishura ibirimwo muri `m`.


Mu masezerano ya RGB, Ukwiyemeza ishirwa mu gikorwa ca Bitcoin kugira ngo yerekane ko hari amakuru kanaka ariho mu gihe kinaka, ata makuru ubwayo ahishuriwe.


#### Consignment


A **Consignment** ihuriza hamwe amakuru yashikirijwe hagati y'ababuranyi, hakurikijwe Ukwemeza kuruhande rw'umuguzi muri RGB. Hariho ivyiciro bibiri nyamukuru vya Consignment:




- **Amasezerano ya Consignment**: itangwa n'uwutanga (uwatanga Amasezerano), irimwo amakuru y'intango nka Igicapo, Itanguriro, Ahabneka hamwe n'ahaboneka hashirwa mungiro.
- **Kwimurira Consignment**: bitangwa n'uwuriha (*uwuriha*). Irimwo amateka yose y'impinduka za Leta zishikana aho Consignmentiherera (ni ukuvuga Uko bimeze ubwanyuma yaronse n'uwuyitanga).


Ivyo bintu birungitswe ntivyandikwa ku mugaragaro ku rupapuro rwa Blockchain; birahanahana ata guca ku ruhande hagati y’ababijejwe biciye ku nzira y’itumanaho bahisemwo.


#### Amasezerano


Amasezerano ni urutonde rw’uburenganzira bushirwa mu ngiro mu buryo bwa digitale hagati y’abakozi benshi biciye ku masezerano ya RGB. Ifise igihugu gikora na Uko ishoramario rimeze, isobanurwa y'igicapo, igaragaza ibikorwa vyemewe (uguhindura, kwongera, n’ibindi). Ivy'amasezerano imeze, hamwe n'amategeko agenga ukuri kwayo, bivugwa mugicapo. Igihe cose, Amasezerano iratera imbere gusa bivanye n’ivyo vyemewe n’ico gicapo be n’inyandiko zo kwemeza (Ukwiruka, nk’akarorero, muri AluVM).


#### Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano


Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano ni uguhindura uko amasezerano ameze gukorwa hakurikijwe amategeko y'igicapo. Ibikorwa bikurikira biri muri RGB:




- 1117;
- 1118;
- 1119.


Igikorwa kimwekimwe cose gihindura igihugu mu kwongerako canke gusubirira amakuru amwamwe (Uko bimeze muri rusangi, Uko bimeze bifiswe n'abantu...).


#### Amasezerano y'abahari


Amasezerano y'abatonze ni umukinyi agira uruhara mu bikorwa bijanye n'amasezerano. Muri RGB, hariho itandukaniro hagati ya:




- Uwutanga amasezerano, ari we arema Itanguriro (inkomoko y'Amasezerano);
- Abagize Amasezerano, ni ukuvuga abafise uburenganzira uko amasezerano ameze;
- Uko imice imeze, ashobora kwubaka Ivyumba vy'uko amasezerano ameze itanga Ivyumba vy’Igihugu bishobora gushikirwa na bose.


#### Uburenganzira bw'amsezerano


Uburenganzira bw'amasezerano yerekeza ku burenganzira butandukanye bushobora gukoreshwa n’abafise uruhara muma sezerano ya RGB. Bica mu mice myinshi:




- Uburenganzira bw'**Ukwitirirwa ibintu**, bujanye n'uburenganzira bw'ukwitirirwa ibintu bwa UTXO kanaka (biciye mu _Nsobanuro y'Ikidodo_);
- Uburenganzira bw'ubutegetsi, ni ukuvuga ubushobozi bwo kwubaka inzira imwe canke nyinshi (Uko inzira zimeze) hakurikijwe Igicapo;
- **Uburenganzira bwa bose**, iyo Igicapo cemera gukoresha ibintu bimwe bimwe vya bose, nk'akarorero kurema uvyongerwa kuko bimeze biciye mu gucungura Valency.


#### Uko amasezerano ameze


Uko amasezerano amaze ihuye n’ingene amasezerano ari ubu mu gihe kanaka. Ishobora kuba igizwe n'amakuru ya bose n'ay'abikorera ku giti cabo, yerekana uko Amasezerano ameze. RGB itandukanya:




- **Uko bimeze murirusangi**, irimwo ivy’abantu bose vy'amasezerano (vyashizweho mw'itanguriro canke vyongeweko biciye mu guhindura vyemewe);
- Uko bimeze bifise uburenganzira, ari vyo vy'abafise uburenganzira bwihariye, bimenyekana n'ama UTXO yabo.


#### Deterministic Bitcoin Commitment - DBC


Deterministic Bitcoin Commitment (DBC) ni urutonde rw'amategeko akoreshwa mu kwandika mu buryo bugaragara kandi budasanzwe _ukwiyemeza_ mu gucuruza Bitcoin. Mu masezerano ya RGB, hari uburyo bubiri nyamukuru bwa DBC:




- **Opret**
- **Tapret**


Ubu buryo burasobanura neza ingene _ukwiyemeza_ gushirwa mu gisohoka canke mu mibumbe y'isoko rya Bitcoin, kugira ngo bimenyekane ko uko kwiyemeza gushobora gukurikiranywa no kugenzurwa.


#### Directed Acyclic Graph - DAG


DAG (canke *Acyclic Guided Graph*) ni igishushanyo kitagira umuzingi, gishoboza gutegura urutonde rw'ibintu. Ivyuma vy’amabara, nk’ibice _vy’amasezerano ya RGB, bishobora guserukirwa n’ama DAG.


Mushaka amakuru yimbitse : [Directed Acyclic Graph](Igishushanyo_c'Igishushanyo_C'Igishushanyo_C'Igishushanyo)


#### Gucapura


Gucapura ni urudodo rw’amakuru rwo guhitamwo abafise Amasezerano bakurikirana bashobora kwinjira muri kahise k'amasezerano. Ico kintu kiriho, nk’akarorero, muri **RGB21** Ahaboneka kandi kiratuma amakuru y’icibutso canke y’insobanuro yongerwa kuri kahise k'amasezerano.


#### Ikimenyamenya c'ibikorwa vy'inyongera - ETP


ETP (*Extra Transaction Proof*) ni igice c'aho bashimikira harimwo amakuru y'inyongera asabwa kugira ngo umuntu yemeze **Tapret** *ukwiyemeza* (mu bijanye na _taproot_). Harimwo, mu bindi, urufunguzo rwa bose rw'imbere rw'inyandiko ya Taproot (_internal PubKey_) n'amakuru yihariye ku _Inzira y'inyandiko zarungitswe_.


#### Itanguriro


Itanguriro ryerekana ku rutonde rw'amakuru, ayoborwa n'igicapo, igize igihugu c'intango c'amasezerano iyo ari yo yose muri RGB. Bishobora kugereranywa n’iciyumviro ca Bitcoin ca _Genesis Block_, canke n’iciyumviro c'ihanahanwa rya Coinbase, ariko hano ku rugero rwa _uruhande rw’umugzi_ n’urwa Token rya RGB.


#### Uko bimeze muri rusangi


Uko buimeze muri rusangi ni urutonde rw'ibintu vya bose biri mu masezerano y'uko bimeze. Isobanurwa kw'itanguriro kandi, bivanye n’amategeko y'amasezerano, ishobora guhindurwa n’ihinduka ryemewe. Mu buryo butandukanye n’Ibihugu Bifise Ububasha, Ukobimeze muri rusangi ntabwo ari iy’ikigo kinaka; ni hafi cane y’inyandiko ya bose iri mumasezerano.


#### Ahakorerwa


Ahakorerwa ni urutonde rw'amabwirizwa akoreshwa mu gusobanura amakuru abiri akoranijwe mugicapo canke mu bikorwa vy'amasezerano n'imibereho yayo, kugira ngo ashobore gusomwa n'uwukoresha canke ingodo yiwe. Ikora nk'insobanuro Layer.


#### Aho gukorera mugushira mungiro


Aho gukorera mugushira mungiro ni umugwi w'amatangazo ahuza **Ahakorerwa** n' **Igicapo**. Bishoboza ubuhinduzi bw’insobanuro bukorwa n'ahakorerwa ubwayo, kugira ngo amakuru atagiramwo ivyatsi yo mumasezerano ashobore gutahurwa n’uwukoresha canke porogarama irimwo (amasakoshi).


#### Fagitire


Fagitire ifata uburyo bwa URL ishizwe muri [base58](https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/Binary-to-text encoding#Base58), ikaba ishiramwo amakuru akenewe kugira ngo umuntu yubake **Uko yahindutse** (n’uwuyitanga). Mu yandi majambo, ni Invoice ishoboza uwundi (*uwuriha*) gukora ihinduka rihuye n'iryo kugira ngo yimure umutungo canke avugurure uko amasezerano ameze.


#### Lightning Network


Lightning Network ni urubuga rwigenga rw’imihora yo kuriha  (canke _imihora y'uko bimeze_) kuri Bitcoin, rugizwe n’ibipapuro 2/2 vy’imikono myinshi. Bishoboza gukora amafaranga yihuta, ataco atwara _inyuma y’uruzitiro_, mu gihe yizigira Layer 1 ya Bitcoin ku bijanye n’ubukemurampaka (canke gufunga) iyo bikenewe.


Kugira ngo umenye vyinshi ku buryo Lightning ikora, ndagusavye ukwirikirane kino cigwa:


https://planb.academy/courses/34bd43ef-6683-4a5c-b239-7cb1e40a4aeb

#### Multi Protocol Commitment - MPC


Multi Protocol Commitment (MPC) yerekeza uko igiti ca Merkle kimeze uko gikoreshwa muri RGB kugira ngo ishiremwo, mu gikorwa kimwe ca Bitcoin, **Imigwi y’Impinduka** myinshi iva mu masezerano atandukanye. Iciyumviro ni ugushira hamwe amasezerano menshi (ashobora guhura n’amasezerano atandukanye canke itunga ritandukanye) mu ntumbero imwe y'aho bishingiye kugira ngo umuntu ashobore gukoresha neza ikibanza c’amabuye.


#### Ibifashwe mumaboko


Ibifashwe mumaboko ni igice c'Uko amasezerano ameze gipfutse mumyimenyerezo kandi gifitaniye isano n’umuntu yihariye afise (biciye kuri Serire ikoreshwa rimwe yerekana UTXO). Ivyo bigereranya nk’akarorero umutungo wo kuri interineti canke uburenganzira bumwe bumwe bw’amasezerano uwo muntu yahawe.


#### Ukwitirirwa ikintu


Ukwitirirwa ikintu cerekana ku bushobozi bwo kugenzura no gukoresha UTXO yerekanwa n'Insiguro ya serire. Iyo Ibifashwe muminwe gufatanye na UTXO, nyen'iyo UTXO arafise uburenganzira, bishoboka, bwo kwimurira canke guhindura igihugu gifatanye, hakurikijwe amategeko y'amasezerano.


#### Partially Signed Bitcoin Transaction - PSBT


PSBT (_Igice ca Bitcoin gishizweko umukono_) ni igitabu ca Bitcoin kitarashirwako umukono ku buryo bwemewe. Ishobora gusangizwa hagati y’ibigo vyinshi, kimwe cose kikaba gishobora kwongerako canke kugenzura Ibintu zimwe zimwe (imikono, inyandiko...), gushika iyo nzira y’ugucuruza ibonwa ko yiteguriye gukwiragizwa On-Chain.


Ku bindi bisobanuro: [BIP-0174](BIP-0174.mediawiki)


#### Ukwiyeza kwa Pedersen


Ukwiyemeza kwa Pedersen ni ubwoko bw'ibara ry'ibanga ry'Ukwiyemeza rifise akamaro ko kuba **homomorphic** ku bijanye n'igikorwa co kwongerako. Ivyo bisigura ko bishoboka kwemeza igitigri w’imihigo ibiri ata guhishura agaciro k’umuntu ku giti ciwe.


Mu buryo busanzwe, nimba:


$$
C1=\text{commit}(m1,r1) \quad C2=\text{commit}(m2,r2)
$$


none:


$$
C3=C1⋅C2=\text{commit}(m1+m2, r1+r2)
$$


Iyi nzira ni ngirakamaro, nk'akarorero, mu guhisha amafaranga y'ibimenyetso vyahinduwe, mu gihe ushobora kugenzura igitigiri cose.


Ibindi bisobanuro: [Pedersen commitment](igice ca 10.1007/3-540-46766-1_9)


#### Uguhindura


Muvyongeweko, Uguhindura yerekeza ku gikorwa co gusubira gusaba (canke gukoresha nabi) **Valency** yari yatangajwe mbere. Kubera ko Valency ari uburenganzira bwa bose, Muvyongeweko iremeza uwufise uburenganzira bwo gusaba amasezerano y'ukwongerwako  yihariye.


#### Igicapo


Igicapo muri RGB ni igice c'itangazo ry'itegeko ridondora urutonde rw'ibihinduka, amategeko n'uko ishoramari rimeze (*Uko ishoramari rimeze*) bigenzura ibikorwa vy'amasezerano. Igicapo isoba gisigura uko bimeze, ubwoko bw’ihinduka ryemewe n’ivyo kwemeza.


#### Insiguro ya Serire


Insiguro ya Serire ni igice c'amasezerano gifatanya _ukwiyemeza_ na UTXO y'uwuyifise mushasha. Mu yandi majambo, yerekana aho ivyangombwa biri (aho UTXO iri), kandi igashinga n'ibifiswe n'abantu y’umutungo canke uburenganzira.


#### Shard


Shard igereranya ishami muri DAG y'amateka y'Impinduka z'uko amasezerano ya RGB ameze. Mu yandi majambo, ni igice gihuye cakahise yose kumasezerano, gihuye, nk'akarorero, n'urutonde rw'ibintu bisabwa kugira ngo umuntu yerekane ko umutungo kanaka ufise ukuri kuva mu _Itanguriro_.


#### Serire ikoreshwa rimwe


Serire ikoreshwa rimwe ni ubuhinga bw’ibanga bw'ukwiyemeza ku butumwa butaramenyekana, buzoshirirwa ahabona rimwe gusa muri kazoza kandi butegerezwa kumenyekana n’abagize umuryango w’abantu bose. Intumbero ni ukubuza gushinga amasezerano menshi y'uguhiganwa kuri Serire imwe.


#### Stash


Stash ni urutonde rw’amakuru y’uruhande rw’umuguzi, umukoresha abika ku masezerano imwe canke menshi ya RGB, kugira ngo yemezwe (*Kuruhande rw'ukwemeza rw'umuguzi*). Ivyo birimwo amateka y’ihinduka, ivy’ugurungika, ibimenyamenya vy’ukuri, n’ibindi.Umuntu wese afise aguma afise gusa ibice vyakahise akeneye (*shards*).


#### Uko ivyiyongerako bimeze


Uko vyongerwako bimeze n'ibikorwa vy'amasezerano akoreshwa mu gusubira gutera ivyagezwe vy'uko gucungura bimeze **Ivy'agaciro** vyamenyeshejwe mbere. Kugira ngo uko ivyongerwako bimeze, itegerezwa rero gupfungwa na ivyiyongerako bimeze (ihindura uko amasezerano ameze ).


#### Uko impinduka imeze


Uko impinduka imeze ni igikorwa gihindura ikibanza c'amasezerano ya RGB kikaja mu kibanza gishasha. Ishobora guhindura amakuru ya Uko imeze muri rusangi na/canke ibifashwemuminwe. Mu bikorwa, uguhinduka kwose kugenzurwa n'amategeko y'igicapo kandi gushirwa muri Blockchain ya Bitcoin biciye ku _ukwiyemeza_.


#### Taproot


Ivuga ku buryo bwo gukoresha Bitcoin bwa SegWit v1, bwashizweho na [BIP341] [BIP342](Ubuhinga bwo gusoma amakuru). Taproot itera imbere ibanga n’uguhinduranya inyandiko, cane cane mu gutuma amafaranga akoreshwa akora neza kandi akagora gutandukanya n’ayandi.


#### Icerekana aho bigarukira - Aho bigarukira vyose


Aho bigarukira vyose (canke _Iherezo ry’Ibirungikwa_) ni *Aho bigarukira vyose* irimwo ivy’iherezo vy'amasezerano, harimwo n'uko bihinduka yaremwe ivuye kuri Fagitire y’uwuyironka (*uwuhembwa*). Ni co rero gisozera ukwimurirwa, harimwo amakuru akenewe kugira ngo yerekane Ukwitirirwa ibintu canke uko bimeze yimuriwe.


#### Umutekero w'impinduka


Umutekerao w'imoinduka ni umugwi w'Impinduka za Leta (ziri muri mumasezerano amwe) zose zikora ***Ivyabna y'ihanahanwa*** Bitcoin imwe. Ivyo bituma bishoboka gukoranya ibintu vyinshi bishasha canke kwimurirwa muri On-Chain Anchor imwe.


#### UTXO


Bitcoin UTXO (*Igisubizo c’Ibikorwa Bitakoreshejwe*) isobanurwa na Hash y’ibikorwa n’urutonde rw’ibikorwa (*vout*). Rimwe na rimwe ryitwa kandi _isonga_. Mu masezerano ya RGB, kwerekeza kuri UTXO (biciye kuri **Insiguro ya Serire**) bishoboza aho **Uko bimeze ibifashwe muminwe** iri, ni ukuvuga umutungo ufise kuri Blockchain.


#### Valency


Valency ni uburenganzira bwa bose budasaba ububiko bw'uko bimeze nk'uko buri, ariko bushobora gucungurwa biciye k' **Ukwiyongera uko bimeze**. Ni uburyo rero bw’ubushobozi bufunguriye bose (canke abakinyi bamwebamwe), bumenyeshwa mu nzira y’ubwenge y'amasezerano, kugira ngo hakorwe ukwongerekana kw’igihe kinaka mu nyuma.


#### Icemeza c'ihanahanwa


Icemeza c'ihanahanwa ni igikorwa ca Bitcoin cugara Serire ikoreshwa rimwe gikikuje ubutumwa burimwo Multi Protocol Commitment (MPC). Ivyo bicuruzwa bikoresha UTXO canke bikabirema, kugira ngo Ukwiyemeza kwa Serire ihuye n’umurongo wa RGB. Ikora nk’ikimenyamenya ca On-Chain c’uko bimeze yashizweho mu gihe kinaka.


# Porogaramu kuri RGB


<partId>148a7436-d079-56d9-be08-aaa4c14c6b3a</partId>


## Gushira mu ngiro amasezerano ya RGB


<chapterId>8333ea5f-51c7-5dd5-b1d7-47d491e58e51</chapterId>


:::id ya videwo=97d81b85-5a82-40a5-b111-7d96be5afd0f:::


Muri iki gice, turaza kuraba neza ingene amasezerano ya RGB asigurwa kandi igashirwa mu ngiro. Turabona ibice bigize amasezerano ya RGB ni ibiki, uruhara rwavyo n’ingene vyubatswe.


### Ibice bigize amasezerano ya RGB


Kugeza ubu, twamaze kuvuga ku **Ntangamarara**, igereranya intango y'amasezerano, kandi twabonye ingene ihuye n'ubwenge bwa *Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano* n'ingene porotokore imeze. Insobanuro yuzuye y'amasezerano ya RGB, ariko, ntigarukira kw'itanguriro yonyene: irimwo ibice bitatu vyuzuzanya, vyose hamwe, bikaba bigize umutima w’ugushirwa mu ngiro.


Igice ca mbere citwa **Igicapo**. Iyi ni dosiye idondora uko ivyibanze vy'uko ishoramari rimeze (*Uko ishoramari rimeze*) kuma Sezerano. Irasobanura ubwoko bw’amakuru akoreshwa, amategeko yo kwemeza, ibikorwa vyemewe (nk’ugutanga token mu ntango, ukwimurira, ivyangombwa bidasanzwe, n’ibindi) - muri make, inzego rusangi zitegeka ingene Amasezerano ameze.


Igice ca kabiri ni **Uko hameze**. Bishimikiye cane ku kuntu abakoresha (kandi mu kwagura, porogaramu y'ibikorwa) bazokorana n'iy' amasezerano. Iradondora insiguro, ni ukuvuga uguserukira gusomwa kw’ibice bitandukanye n’ibikorwa. Rero, mu gihe c'igicapo isobanura ingene Amasezerano akora mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, Ahakorerwa isobanura ingene yoshikiriza no gushikiriza ivyo bikoresho: amazina y’uburyo, kwerekana amakuru, n’ibindi.


Igice ca gatatu ni **Ugushira mungiro uko bikora**, kikaba kizuza ibindi bibiri vyabanje mu gukora nk'ikiraro hagati y'igicapo n'ahakorerwa ibintu. Mu yandi majambo, rifatanya insobanuro yerekanwa n'ahakorerwa ibintu n’amategeko ashingiyeko asobanuwe kugicapo. Iryo shirwa mu ngiro ni ryo rizocungera, nk’akarorero, uguhindura hagati y’umurongo winjijwe mungodo n’imiterere y’ibice bibiri itegekanijwe n’umurongo, canke gukoranya amategeko y’ukwemeza mu rurimi rw’imashini.


Ubwo buhinga ni ikintu gishimishije muri RGB, kuko butuma imigwi itandukanye y’abahinguzi bakora ukwabo kuri ivyo bintu (*Igicapo*, *Ahakorerwa ibintu*, *Ishirwa mu ngiro*), igihe cose bakurikije amategeko y’uguhurizako y’amasezerano.


Mu guca irya n’ino, Amasezerano yose agizwe na:




- **Intanguriro**, ​​ari ryo ry'intango ry'amasezerano (kandi rishobora kugereranywa n'ugucuruza kudasanzwe gusobanura Ukwitirirwa ibintu ya mbere y'umutungo, uburenganzira, canke ayandi makuru yose ashobora guhindurwa);
- **Igicapo**, idondora uko amasezerano y'ishoramari ameze (ubwoko bw'amakuru, amategeko yo kwemeza, n'ibindi);
- **Ahakorerwa ibintu**, itanga insiguro ya Layer ku bikoresho vyose n'abakoresha abantu, isobanura ugusoma n'ugushirwa mu ngiro kw'ibikorwa;
- Ishirwa mu ngiro **ry'ahakorera ibintu**, igabanya ikinogo kiri hagati y'uko ishoramari rimeze n'ugushikiriza, kugira ngo isoiure amasezerno ihure n'ubumenyi bw'ukoresha.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/070.webp)


Ni ngombwa kumenya ko kugira ngo Ingodo ishobore gucunga umutungo wa RGB (yaba token ishobora guhindurwa canke uburenganzira bw’ubwoko bwose), itegerezwa kuba ifise izo Ibintu zikoresha zose zikoranijwe: *Igicapo*, *Ahakorerwa ibintu*, *GW-134*35. Ivyo birungikwa biciye ku ***hakorerwa amasezerano***, ni ukuvuga amakuru arimwo vyose bikenewe kugira ngo wemeze Amasezerano y'umukiriya.


Kugira ngo dufashe gusobanura ivyo vyiyumviro, ng’iyi imbonerahamwe y’incamake igereranya ibice vy'amasezerano ya RGB n’ivyiyumviro bimaze kumenyekana haba mu gukora porogarama zishingiye ku bintu (OOP) canke mu bidukikije vya Ethereum:


| Ibigize amasezerano ya RGB       | Insiguro                        | OOP Bingana                                    | Icobingana muri Ethereum               |
| ----------------------------     | ------------------------------  | ---------------------------------------------  | ---------------------------------- |
| **Itanguriro**                   | Uko amasezerano yarameze muntango  | Iyubako ry'amasomo                          | Inyubako y'amasezeranpo               |
| **Igicapo**                   | Uko amasezerano y'ishoramari ameze | Ishure                                         | Amsezerano                           |
| **Ahakorerwa ibintu**           | Uko amasezerano ameze      | Ahakorerwa ibintu (Java) / Akarongo (Rust) / Porotokore (Swift) | ERC Ihurizwako nabose          |
| **Aho ibintu bishirirwa mungiro** | Igicapo c'ukoinyandiko zimeze n'ukobigenda | Impl (Rust) / Gushirwa mungiro (Java)                    | Apirikasiyo ifise ahakorerwa habiri (ABI) |


Inkingi y’ibubamfu yerekana Ibice yihariye ku bijanye n’umurongo wa RGB. Inkingi yo hagati yerekana igikorwa nyaco c’igice kimwekimwe cose. Hanyuma, mu nkingi ya "OOP Bingana", dusanga ijambo ringana muri porogarama zishingiye ku kintu:




- **Itanguriro** ifise uruhara rusa n'urw'umuhinguzi w'Ikigo: niho igihugu c'amasezerano gitangura;
- **Igicapo** ni insobanuro y’umugwi, ni ukuvuga insobanuro y’uko umeze, uburyo bwawo n’intumbero yawo;
- **Ahakorerwa ibintu** ihuye n' *ibimenyetso* (Java), *ibiranga* (Rust) canke *amasezerano* (Swift): ivyo ni vyo bisobanuro vya bose vy'ibikorwa, ibintu, imirima...;
- **Aho ibintu bushirirwa mungiro** ihuye na *Impl* muri Rust canke *Ugushira mungiro* muri Java, aho dusobanura ingene kode izokora uburyo bwamenyeshejwe muhakorerwa ibintu.


Mu bijanye n'ivy'ubuhinga bwa Ethereum, Itanguriro iri hafi cane y'umwubatsi w' **Amasezerano**, Igicapo Kiri hafi y'insobanuro y'amasezerano, Ahakorerwa ibintu iri hafi y'urugero nka ERC-20 canke ERC-721, na Ahakorerwa ibintu hari hafi y'insobanuro ya **ABI**, uburyo bwo gukorana kw'Amasezerano.


Inyungu y’uko RGB ishobora gukoreshwa mu buryo bw’ibice (ukobimeze) na yo iri mu kuba abafatanyabikorwa batandukanye bashobora kwandika, nk’akarorero, Aho ibintu bishirwa mungiro yabo, igihe cose bubaha ubusobanuro bw' *Igicapo* n’insobanuro ya *Ahkorerwa ibintu*. Gutyo, uwutanga amakuru yoshobora gutegura imbere nshasha, ikoreshwa neza cane (Ahakorerwa ibintu), ataco ahinduye ku nsiguro y'amasezerano, canke ibihushanye n’ivyo, umuntu yoshobora kwagura Igicapo kugira ngo yongereko ibikorwa, maze agatanga verisiyo nshasha y’ibikorwa vy’ishimikiro vya Ahakorerwa ibintu vyahinduwe, mu gihe ibikorwa vya kera vy’ishimikiro vyogumaho.


Iyo dukoranye n'amasezerano mashasha, dukora Itanguriro  (intambwe ya mbere yo gutanga canke gutanga umutungo), hamwe n’ibigize (Igicapo, Ahakorerwa ibintu, Aho ibintu bishirwa mungiro). Inyuma y’ivyo, Amasezerano arakora neza kandi arashobora gukwiragizwa kungodo no ku bakoresha. Ubu buryo, aho Itanguriro ifatanijwe n’ivyo bice bitatu, butanga icemezo c’urugero rwo hejuru rw’uguhindura (buri Mumasezerano ishobora kugira ivyiyumviro vyayo), kwegereza ubutegetsi (umuntu wese ashobora gutanga umusanzu ku gice kinaka), n’umutekano (ugushingira intahe biguma bisobanuwe cane n’umurongo w’amategeko, ata gushingira ku arbitry onG on8- izindi nzira z’amabuye).


Ubu rero ndashaka kwihweza neza kimwe cose muri ivyo bice: **Igicapo**, **Aho bakorera** na **Interface Implementation**.


### Igicapo


Mu gice ca mbere, twabonye ko mu bidukikije vya RGB, Amasezerano agizwe n’ibidukikije vyinshi: Itanguriro, bishinga intahe ivy’intango, n’ibindi bihimba vyinshi vy’inyongera. Intumbero yiGicapo ni ugusobanura neza uko ishoramari rimeze ry'amasezerano, ni ukuvuga uko amakuru ameze, ubwoko bukoreshwa, ibikorwa vyemewe n’ingene bimeze. Ni ikintu gihambaye cane rero mu gutuma Amasezerano akora ku ruhande rw’umuguzi, kuko uwuriko arayigiramwo wese (Ingodo, nk’akarorero) ategerezwa kugenzura ko amahinduka y'uko bimeze aronka ahuye n’ubwenge busobanuwe murikino gicapo.


Igicapo gishobora kugereranywa n'"umugwi" mu gukora porogarama zishingiye ku bintu (OOP). Muri rusangi, ikora nk’akarorero gasigura ibice bigize Amasezerano, nk’akarorero:




- Ubwoko butandukanye bw’Ibihugu vy’Igihugu n’Ibikorwa;
- Valencies, ni ukuvuga uburenganzira budasanzwe bushobora guterwa (*gucungurwa*) ku bikorwa bimwebimwe;
- Uko bimeze murirusangi, zidondora ivy’isi yose, ivy’abantu bose n’ivy’abantu bose vy'amasezerano;
