- Igishushanyo c'itanguriro (igikorwa ca mbere nyene gikora Amasezerano);
- Uburyo bwemewe bw’Impinduka z'uko bimeze n’Ivyaguwe vy'uko bimeze, n’ingene ivyo bikorwa bishobora guhindura;
- Amakuru ajana n’igikorwa cose, kugira ngo ubike amakuru y’igihe gito canke y’inyongera;
- Amategeko agena ingene amakuru yo mu mutima y'amasezerano ashobora gutera imbere (nk’akarorero, nimba umurima ushobora guhinduka canke ushobora kwirundanira);
- Urutonde rw’ibikorwa bibonwa ko bifise akamaro: nk’akarorero, urutonde rw’ihinduka ry’ibintu ryubahirizwa canke urutonde rw’ibintu bihuye n’ubwenge bikwiye gushitswako.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/071.webp)


Iyo *uwutanga* umutungo uri kuri RGB asohoye Amasezererano, atanga Itanguriro na Igicapo Bijana nawo. Abakoresha canke ama ingodo bipfuza gukorana n’itunga bararonka iyi Igicapo kugira ngo batahure ivyiyumviro biri inyuma y'amasezerano, no kugira ngo bashobore kugenzura mu nyuma ko amahinduka bazogiramwo uruhara ari ay’ukuri.


Intambwe ya mbere, ku muntu wese aronka amakuru yerekeye umutungo wa RGB (nk'akarorero, ukwimurira token), ni ukwemeza ayo makuru kugicapo. Ivyo birimwo gukoresha igitabu Igicapo kugira ngo:




- Suzuma ko Ibihugu vy’Umutungo, Ibikorwa n’ibindi Bintu bisobanuwe neza kandi ko vyubahiriza ubwoko bwategetswe (ivyo bita *strict type system*);
- Suzuma ko amategeko y’uguhindura (inyandiko zo kwemeza) yuzuye. Izo nyandiko zishobora gukoreshwa biciye ku AluVM, iri ku ruhande rw’umukiriya kandi ishinzwe kwemeza ukoishoramari rimeze ihuye (amahera yoherezwa, ivyangombwa bidasanzwe, n’ibindi).


Mu bikorwa, Igicapo si kode ishobora gukorwa, nk’uko bishobora kubonwa mu ma blockchain abika kuri kode ya On-chain (EVM kuri Ethereum). Ahubwo, RGB itandukanya n'uko ishoramari rimeze (itangazo) na kode ishobora gushirwa mu ngiro kuri Blockchain (iyigarukira ku nzitizi z’ubuhinga). Gutyo, Igicapo ni yo igena amategeko, ariko ugushira mu ngiro ayo mategeko bibera hanze ya Blockchain, ku kibanza c’uwuje mu nama wese, hakurikijwe ingingo ngenderwako y'ukwemeza kuruhande rw'umuguzi.


Igicapo gitegerezwa gukoranirizwa imbere y’uko ikoreshwa n’ibikorwa vya RGB. Iyi nkuru itanga dosiye y'ibice bibiri (nk'akarorero `.RGB`) canke dosiye y'ibice bibiri (`.rgba`). Iyo Wallet yinjije iyi dosiye, iramenya:




- Ivyo ubwoko bumwe bumwe bw’amakuru (igitigiri cose, Uko kimeze, imirongo...) busa kubera uburyo bw’ubwoko bukomeye;
- Uko Itanguriro rikwiye gutunganirizwa (kugira ngo umuntu atahure intango y’itunga);
- Ubwoko butandukanye bw’ibikorwa (Impinduka z'uko bimeze, Ukwagura Ukobimeze) n’ingene bishobora guhindura Ukobimeze;
- Amategeko y’inyandiko (yashizwe mugicapo) moteri ya AluVM izokoresha kugira ngo isuzume ko ibikorwa bifise ukuri.


Nk’uko vyasiguwe mu bice vyatanguye, *uburyo bw’ubwoko bukomeye* buraduha uburyo bwo gushiramwo amakuru buhamye, bushingiye ku vyo umuntu abona: ibihinduka vyose, vyaba Ibihugu vy’Umutungo, Ibihugu vy’Isi yose canke Ivy’Uburemere, biradondaguwe neza (ubunini, imbibe zo hasi n’izo hejuru nimba bikenewe, ubwoko bufise umukono canke butashizweko umukono, n’ibindi). Birashoboka kandi gusigura imiterere y'ivyatsi, nk'akarorero gushigikira ibibazo vy'ikoreshwa bikomeye.


Mu buryo bw'ubushake, Igicapo gishobora gukoresha umuzi `Ikiranga igicapo`, bifasha gusubira gukoresha imiterere y'ishimikiro iriho (ikigereranyo). Muri ubu buryo, ushobora guhindura Amasezerano canke guhingura ibintu bihinduka (nk'ubwoko bushasha bwa token) uhereye ku citegererezo camaze kwemezwa. Ukwo guhinduranya amasezerano kurarinda gusubira gukora amasezerano yose, kandi kuraremesha uguhuza ingendo nziza.


Ikindi kintu gihambaye ni uko ubuhinga bwo gutera imbere y'uko bimeze (uguhindura, guhindura, n’ibindi) budondora mugicapo mu buryo bw’inyandiko, amategeko n’ivyangombwa. Rero, nimba umuhinguzi w'amasezerano yipfuza kwemerera gusubira gusohoka canke gushinga uburyo bwo guturira (ugusambura ibimenyetso), arashobora gusobanura inyandiko zihuye na AluVM mu gice co kwemeza Igicapo.


#### Itandukaniro n'ibindi bishobora gukorwa On-Chain


Udakunze ubuhinga nka Ethereum, aho kode ya Smart contract (ishobora gukorwa) yandikwa muri Blockchain ubwayo, RGB ibika Amasezerano (ubwenge bwayo) off-chain, mu buryo bw’inyandiko y’imenyekanisha ikoranijwe. Ivyo bisigura ko:




- Nta VM yuzuye ya Turing ikora mu nzira yose y’urubuga rwa Bitcoin. Amategeko y'amasezerano ya RGB ntashirwa mu ngiro kuri Blockchain, ariko mu mukoresha wese yipfuza kwemeza ukobikora;
- Amakuru y'amasezerano ntahumanya Blockchain: ibimenyamenya vy’ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru (*ivyemezo*) vyonyene ni vyo bishirwa mu bikorwa vya Bitcoin (biciye muri `Tapret` canke `Opret`);
- Igicapo kirashobora guhindurwa canke kigakurwako (*kwihuta-imbere*, *gusunika-inyuma*, n'ibindi), ataco bisaba ivyuma vyokuri Blockchain ya Bitcoin  . Ingodo zirakenera akeneye gusa kwinjiza mukoigicapo kimeze nshasha no kumenyera amahinduka y’ubumwe.


#### Ikoreshwa n'uwutanga n'abakoresha


Iyo *umutanga* aremye umutungo (nk’akarorero, token idashobora guhinduka), ategura:




- Igitabo c'ibicapo bisigura amategeko agenga ivy’ugusohora, uguhindura n’ibindi;
- Itanguriro rihuye n’ivy'igicapo (irimwo umubare wose w’ibimenyetso vyasohowe, akaranga ka nyen’ivyo bimenyetso vya mbere, Valencies zidasanzwe zo gusubira gusohoka, n’ibindi).


Ica ituma Igicapo (dosiye `.RGB`) yashizwe hamwe iboneka ku bakoresha, kugira ngo umuntu wese yaronse ubutumwa bwo muri iyo token ashobore kugenzura ukuntu igikorwa gihuye mu karere. Iyo atagicapo, uwuyikoresha ntiyoshobora gusigura amakuru y’ivy’imimerere canke ngo asuzume ko yubahiriza amategeko y'amasezerano.


Rero iyo ingodo nshasha ishaka gushigikira umutungo, ikeneye gusa gushiramwo igicapo kiberete ibereye. Ubu buryo buratuma bishoboka kwongerako uguhuza ku bwoko bushasha bw’itunga rya RGB, ata guhindura mu buryo buteye ubwoba urufatiro rwa porogarama y'Ingodo: ibisabwa vyose ni ukuzana mu gihugu igicapo kigizwe n'imice ibiri no gutahura imiterere yayo.


Igicapo gisigura uko ishoramari rimeze muri RGB. Iratanga urutonde rw’amategeko y’iterambere ry’igikoresho c'amasezerano, uko amakuru ameze yaco (Ibihugu vy’ubutunzi, Uko imeze muri rusangi, Ivyiyumviro vy’agaciro) n’inyandiko z’ukwemeza zijana (zishobora gukorwa na AluVM). Kubera iyi nyandiko y’itangazo, isigura amasezerano (dosiye ikoranijwe) itandukanye neza n’ugushirwa mu ngiro nyakuri kw’amategeko (uruhande rw’umukiriya). Ivyo bituma RGB ishobora guhindura cane, bikaba bishoboza gukoresha ibintu vyinshi (ibimenyetso bishobora guhinduka, NFT, amasezerano ateye igomwe) mu gihe yirinda ugusobanuka n’amakosa asanzwe mu bikoresho vya On-Chain bishobora gutegurwa.


#### Akarorero k'Igicapo


Reka turabe akarorero nyako k'Igicapo c'amasezerano ya RGB. Iyi ni igice kiri muri Rust muri dosiye `nia.rs` (indome z'intango za "*Itunga Ridashobora Gukura*"), risobanura akarorero k'ibimenyetso bishobora guhinduka bidashobora gusubira gusohoka birenze ibikoreshwa yabo ya mbere (itunga ridashobora gutera). Ubwo bwoko bwa token bushobora kubonwa nk’ubungana, mu gisata ca RGB, bwa ERC20 kuri Ethereum, ni ukuvuga ibimenyetso bishobora guhinduka vyubahiriza amategeko amwe amwe y’ishimikiro (nk’akarorero ku kwimurira, gutangura Ibikoreshwa, n’ibindi).


Imbere yo kwisuka muri kode, birabereye kwibuka uko murirusangi igicapo ca RGB kimeze. Hari urutonde rw'amatangazo ashinzwe:




- `Umwidondoro w'igicapo` ishoboka yerekana ikoreshwa ry'ikindi gicapo c'ishimikiro nk'akarorero;
- **Ibihugu vy’Isi yose** na **Ibihugu vy’Igihugu** (n’ubwoko bwavyo bukomeye);
- **Ivyiza** (niba biriho);
- Ivyo **Ibikorwa** (Itanguriro, Uko impinduka zimeze, Ukwaguka kw’Igihugu) bishobora kwerekeza kuri ivyo bihugu n’ivyo bihugu;
- **Ubwoko bukomeye** bukoreshwa mu kudondora no kwemeza amakuru;
- **Ivyanditswe vyemeza** (bikoreshwa biciye kuri AluVM).


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/072.webp)


Kode iri musi yerekana insoiguro yuzuye y'igicapo ca Rust. Tuzobivuga igice ku kindi, dukurikije insiguro (1) gushika kuri (9) biri aha hepfo:


```rust
// ===== PART 1: Function Header and SubSchema =====
fn nia_schema() -> SubSchema {

// definitions of libraries and variables

// ===== PART 2: General Properties (ffv, subset_of, type_system) =====
Schema {
ffv: zero!(),
subset_of: None,
type_system: types.type_system(),

// ===== PART 3: Global States =====
global_types: tiny_bmap! {
GS_NOMINAL => GlobalStateSchema::once(types.get("RGBContract.DivisibleAssetSpec")),
GS_DATA => GlobalStateSchema::once(types.get("RGBContract.ContractData")),
GS_TIMESTAMP => GlobalStateSchema::once(types.get("RGBContract.Timestamp")),
GS_ISSUED_SUPPLY => GlobalStateSchema::once(types.get("RGBContract.Amount")),
},

// ===== PART 4: Owned Types =====
owned_types: tiny_bmap! {
OS_ASSET => StateSchema::Fungible(FungibleType::Unsigned64Bit),
},

// ===== PART 5: Valencies =====
valency_types: none!(),

// ===== PART 6: Genesis: Initial Operations =====
genesis: GenesisSchema {
metadata: Ty::<SemId>::UNIT.id(None),
globals: tiny_bmap! {
GS_NOMINAL => Occurrences::Once,
GS_DATA => Occurrences::Once,
GS_TIMESTAMP => Occurrences::Once,
GS_ISSUED_SUPPLY => Occurrences::Once,
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
OS_ASSET => Occurrences::OnceOrMore,
},
valencies: none!(),
},

// ===== PART 7: Extensions =====
extensions: none!(),

// ===== PART 8: Transitions: TS_TRANSFER =====
transitions: tiny_bmap! {
TS_TRANSFER => TransitionSchema {
metadata: Ty::<SemId>::UNIT.id(None),
globals: none!(),
inputs: tiny_bmap! {
OS_ASSET => Occurrences::OnceOrMore,
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
OS_ASSET => Occurrences::OnceOrMore,
},
valencies: none!(),
}
},

// ===== PART 9: Script AluVM and Entry Points =====
script: Script::AluVM(AluScript {
libs: confined_bmap! { alu_id => alu_lib },
entry_points: confined_bmap! {
EntryPoint::ValidateGenesis => LibSite::with(FN_GENESIS_OFFSET, alu_id),
EntryPoint::ValidateTransition(TS_TRANSFER) => LibSite::with(FN_TRANSFER_OFFSET, alu_id),
},
}),
}
}
```




- (1) - **Uko hejuru hameze hamwe nomusi y'igicapo**


`nia_schema()` igikorwa kigarura `Igishushanyo gito`, kigaragaza ko icogicapo gishobore kuragwa igice c'igicapo rusangi. Mu bidukikije vya RGB, ukwo guhinduranya gutuma bishoboka gusubira gukoresha Ibintu bimwe bimwe y’umukuru W'igicapo, hanyuma ugasobanura amategeko yihariye kumasezerano iriko iravugwa. Aha, duhitamwo kudashoboza iragi, kuko `subset_of` izoba `Nta`.




- (2) - Ibirango rusangi: ffv, igice_c', **ubwoko_bw'uburyo**


Igikoresho ca `ffv` gihuye n'ivyo *vyihuta* vya Amasezerano. Agaciro ka `ubusa!()` hano kerekana ko turi kuri verisiyo 0 canke verisiyo ya mbere y'iyi Igicapo. Niba mu nyuma wipfuza kwongerako ibikorwa bishasha (ubwoko bushasha bw'ibikorwa, n'ibindi), ushobora kwongera iyi verisiyo kugira ngo werekane ihinduka ry'ukwemeranya.


I `subset_of: Nta` umutungo wemeza ko ata n'iragi. `ubwoko_uburyo` umwanya werekeye ubwoko bukomeye bwa sisitemu busanzwe busobanuwe mu `ubwoko` ububiko bw'ibitabo. Uyu murongo werekana ko amakuru yose akoreshwa n'Amasezerano akoresha ugushirwa mu ngiro kw’urutonde gukomeye gutangwa n’ububiko bw’ibitabu buvugwa.




- (3) - Ibihugu vyo kw'isi yose


Mu `ubwoko_bw'isi yose`, dutangaza Ibintu bine. Dukoresha urufunguzo, nka `GS_IZINA` canke `GS_ISOHOKA_ITANGA`, kugira ngo tubikoreshe mu nyuma:




- `GS_NOMINAL` yerekeza ku bwoko bwa `DivisibleAssetSpec`, budondora ivyicaro bitandukanye vya token yaremwe (izina ryose, ikimenyetso, ukuri...);
- `GS_DATA` igereranya amakuru rusangi, nk'ukwiyamiriza, amakuru y'imbere, canke uwundi munyandiko;
- `GS_TIMESTAMP` yerekana itariki y'isohoka;
- `GS_ISSUED_SUPPLY` ishiraho igitigiri cose c'ibitangwa, ni ukuvuga igitigiri kinini c'ibimenyetso bishobora gukorwa.


Ijambo ry'ingenzi `rimwe(...)` risigurako ko buri kimwe muri ivyo bibanza gishobora kugaragara rimwe gusa.




- (4) - Ubwoko bw'ibintu


Mu `ubwoko_bufise`, dutangaza `OS_ASSET`, idondora uko bimeze gishobora guhinduka. Dukoresha `Ukoigicapo Kimeze::Ukundahindurwa(Ubwoko::Unsigned64Bit)`, vyerekana ko igitigiri c'itunga (ibimenyetso) ubitswe nk'igitigiri cose kidashizweko umukono w'ibice 64. Gutyo, igikorwa cose kizorungika umubare kanaka w’ibice vy’iyi token, ivyo bikaba bizokwemezwa hakurikijwe ivyobitigiri vyanditswe neza.




- (5) - **Ivyiza**


Twerekana `valency_types: none!()`, bisigura ko ata Valencies ziri muri icogicapo, mu yandi majambo nta burenganzira budasanzwe canke bwongerekanye (nk'ugusubira gusohora, guturira bitegekanijwe, n'ibindi). Ico gicapo kirimwo ivyo, vyomenyeshwa muri iki gice.




- (6) - Itanguriro: ibikorwa vya mbere


Aha twinjira mu gice kimenyesha Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano. Itanguriro idondorwa na:




- Kubura `amakuru y'imbere` (umurima `amakuru y'imbere: Ty::<SemId>::UNIT.id(Nta)`);
- Ibihugu vyo kw’isi yose bitegerezwa kubaho rimwe kuri kimwe cose (`Rimwe`);
- Urutonde rw'ibikorwa aho `OS_ASSET` itegerezwa kugaragara `RimweCanke N'ibindi`. Ivyo bisigura ko Itangurire isaba nibura `OS_ASSET` imwe Umwimenyerezo (uwuyifise mu ntango);
- Oya Valency: `ubushobozi: nta n'umwe!()`.


Uko ni ko duca ku rugero rw'insobanuro y'ikibazo ca mbere ca token: dutegerezwa kumenyesha Ibisabwa yasohowe (`GS_ISSUED_SUPPLY`), twongereko n'imiburiburi uwuyifise (ibifashwe muminwe y'ubwoko `OS_ASSET`).




- (7) - Ukwagura


`Ivyagutse: nta!()` vyerekana ko ata vyiyongeyeko itegekanijwe muri iyiri mumasezerano. Ivyo bisigura ko ata gikorwa co gukora Redeem uburenganzira bwakurinyabwonko (Valency) canke gukora Iciyongerwako imbere y’Impinduka. Ivyo vyose bikorwa biciye kwitanguriro canke ku nzira y'uko bimeze.




- (8) - Impinduka: TS_GUHINDURA


Mu `mihindukire`, dusobanura `TS_TRANSFER` ubwoko bw'igikorwa. Turasigura ko:




- Nta nkuru y’imbere ifise;
- Ntihindura Iba murirusangi (ivyo bikaba vyaramaze gusobanurwa mw;itanguriro);
- Bifata `OS_ASSETs` imwe canke nyinshi nk'ivyo kwinjiza. Ivyo bisigura ko itegerezwa gukoresha Uko bimeze Zifise Ubutunzi zisanzweho;
- Irema (`ibikorwa`) nibura `OS_ASSET` imwe nshasha (mu yandi majambo, uwuronka canke abaronka baronka ibimenyetso);
- Nta Valency nshasha itanga.


Ivyo bigereranya inyifato y’ukwimurira kw’ishimikiro, gufungura ibimenyetso kuri UTXO, hanyuma bikarema ukobemeze nshasha zifise ububasha ku neza y’abaronka, gutyo bikazigama uburinganire bw’amahera yose hagati y’ivyo yinjiza n’ivyo isohoka.




- (9) - **Inyandiko ya AluVM n'Ivyiyumviro vy'Injira** (mu gifaransa)


Ubwa nyuma, dutangaza inyandiko ya AluVM (`Inyandiko::AluVM(Inyandiko ya Alu { ... })`). Iyi nyandiko irimwo:




- Isoko rimwe canke menshi ry'inyuma (`libs`) rizokoreshwa mu gihe co kwemeza;
- Ivyinjira vyerekana ibikorwa bihinduka muri kode ya AluVM, bihuye n'ukwemeza kw'itanguriro (`Kwemeza Itanguriro`) na buri mpinduka yatangajwe (`KwemezaImpinduka(TS_TRANSFER)`).


Iyi kode y'ukwemeza ni yo ishinzwe gukoresha Uko ishoramari rimeze. Nk'akarorero, izosuzuma:




- Ko `GS_ISOHOKA_IBIMENYETSO` itarenze mu gihe c'itanguriro;
- Ko umubare w'ibintu vyinjijwe` (ibimenyetso vyakoreshejwe) ungana n'umubare w'ibikorwa` (ibimenyetso vyakiriwe) ku `TS_TRANSFER`.


Iyo ayo mategeko atubahirijwe, iyo mpinduka izobonwa ko ata co imaze.


Aka karorero k'"*Itunga Ridashobora Gufutwa*" Ibicapo biduha ugutahura neza imiterere y'Itunga ryoroshe kumasezerano ya yoken ya RGB. Turashobora kubona neza itandukaniro riri hagati y’insobanuro y’amakuru (Ibihugu vy’Isi yose n’Ibihugu vy’Igihugu), itangazo ry’ibikorwa (Itangiriro, Impinduka, Ukwagura) n’ugushirwa mu ngiro kw’ivyemezo (inyandiko za AluVM). Kubera iki kigereranyo, token yitwararika nk’iyitwa token, ariko iguma yemejwe ku ruhande rw’umuguzi kandi ntiyivana n’ibikorwa remezo vya On-Chain kugira ngo ikore kode yayo. Ivyemezo vy'ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru ni vyo vyonyene bishingiye kuri Blockchain na Bitcoin .


### Ahakorerwa ibintu


Ahakorerwa ibintu ni Layer yagenewe gutuma amasezerano anosmwa kandi ikoreshwa, n’abayikoresha (ugusoma kw’abantu) be n’ibitabo (ugusoma kwa porogarama). Ahakorerwa ibintu rero hafise uruhara rugereranywa n’urw’ahakorerwa ibintu mu rurimi rw’iporogarama rushingiye ku bintu (Java, akaranga ka Rust, n’ibindi), kuko igaragaza kandi igasobanura neza nuko amasezerano ameze, ataco isobanura ku bijanye n’ivyo Amasezerano ikora.


Udakunze Igicapo, ivuga gusa kandi ikoranijwe muri dosiye y’ibice bibiri igoye gukoresha uko iri, Ahakorerwa ibintu hatanga imfunguruzo zo gusoma zikenewe kugira ngo:




- Gutanga urutonde no gusigirura ukobimeze vyo kw’Isi yose n’Ibihugu vy’Igihugu biri mu masezerano;
- Ushobora gushika ku mazina n’agaciro k’umwanya wose, kugira ngo bishobore kwerekanwa (nk’akarorero ku token, umenye igiharuro cawo, igitigiri kinini, n’ibindi);
- Gisigura no kwubaka Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano (Itanguriro, Ukobiinduka, canke Ivyiyongerako) mu gufatanya amakuru n'amazina atahurwa (nk'akarorero, gukora ukwimurira mu gusobanura neza "Igitigiri" aho gukoresha ikimenyetso c'ibice bibiri).


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/073.webp)


Ushimira Aho kubikorera, urashobora, nk'akarorero, kwandika kode mungodo iyo, aho gukoresha ivyatsi, ikoresha ataco ihinduye ibimenyetso nk'"umubare w'ibimenyetso", "izina ry'umutungo", n'ibindi. Muri ubwo buryo, uburongozi bw'amasezerano burarushiriza kuba ubw’agaciro.


#### Ibikorwa rusangi


Ubwo buryo burafise ivyiza vyinshi:




- Gushinga urugero:


Ubwo bwoko bumwe bw'amasezerano burashobora gushigikirwa n'ahakorerwa isanzwe, isangiwe hagati y'ibikorwa vyinshi vy'ingodo. Ivyo bituma vyoroha guhuza no gusubira gukoresha kode.




- **Gutandukanya neza hagati y'igicappo na Interface:**


Mu guhingura RGB, Igicapo (Uko ishramari rimeze) n'Ahakorerwa ibintu (ugushikiriza no gukoresha) ni ibigo bibiri vyigenga. Abahinguzi bandika ubuhinga bw'Amasezerano barashobora kwibanda kugicapo, batababazwa n’ubuhinga bwo gukora canke guserukira amakuru, mu gihe uwundi mugwi (canke uwo mugwi umwe, ariko ku rutonde rw’igihe rutandukanye) ushobora gukora ahakorerwa ibintu.




- **Uguhinduka guhinduka:**


Ahakorerwa ibintu harashobora guhindurwa canke kwongerwako inyuma y’aho umutungo usohokeye, ataco ukeneye guhindura Amasezerano ubwayo. Ivyo ni itandukaniro rikomeye n'ibindi bikoresho vya ama Smart contract ya On-Chain, ahokorerwa ibintu (kenshi ivangwa n'itegeko ry'ugushitsa) ikonjeshwa muri Blockchain.




- Ubushobozi bw'ahakorerwa ibintu bwinshi


Iryo Amasezerano nyene ryoshobora gushirwa ahabona biciye ku nzira zitandukanye zihuye n’ivyo umuntu akeneye: Aakorerwa ibintu horoshe ku muntu akoresha, iyindi iteye imbere cane ku muntu atanga akeneye gucunga ibikorwa vy’Ukobimeze. Ingodo irashobora rero guhitamwo Ahakorerwa ibintu ahitamwo, bivanye n’ingene ikoreshwa.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/074.webp)


Mu bikorwa, iyo Ingodo ironse amasezerano ya RGB (biciye muri dosiye `.RGB` canke `.rgba`), irazana kandi Aho bkorerwa hajana, na yo nyene irakoranywa. Mu gihe co gukora, Ingodo ishobora, nk'akarorero:




- Suzuma urutonde rw’ibihugu maze usome amazina yavyo, kugira ngo ugaragaze Ticker, Amahera wahereyeko, Itariki y’Isohoka, n’ibindi ku mukoresha ahakorerwa ibintu, aho kugaragaza ikimenyetso c’igitigiri kitasomwa;
- Kubaka igikorwa (nk'uguhindura) ukoresheje amazina y'ibipimo asobanutse: aho kwandika `ibikorwa { OS_ASSET => 1 }`, bishobora guha umukoresha umwanya "Umubare" mu rupapuro, maze ugahindura aya makuru mu bibanza vyanditswe neza vyitezwe na GW-156.


#### Itandukaniro na Ethereum n'izindi sisitemu


Ku Ethereum, Ahakorerwa ibintu (idondora biciye ku ABI, *Ikoreshwa ry’Ibikoresho Bibiri Vy'ahorerwa ibintu*) muri rusangi ikomoka kuri kode yabitswe ya On-Chain (Smart contract). Bishobora gutwara amahera menshi canke bikaba bigoye guhindura igice kinaka c'ahakorerwa ibintu utakoze kumasezerano ubwayo. Ariko rero, RGB ishingiye ku nsiguro yose ya off-chain, n'amakuru ashingiye ku *masezerano* kuri Bitcoin. Iyi nzira ituma bishoboka guhindura Ahakorerwa ibintu (canke ugushirwa mu ngiro kwayo) ataco bihinduye ku mutekano w’ishimikiro w'amasezerano, kuko kwemeza amategeko y’ubudandaji kuguma mugicapo n’itegeko rya AluVM ryerekanwa.


#### Ahakorerwa ibintu gukoranya


Nk'uko biri kugucipo, Ahakorerwa ibintu isobanurwa muri kode y'inkomoko (kenshi muri Rust) kandi igakoranywa muri dosiye `.RGB` canke `.rgba`. Iyi dosiye ibiri irimwo amakuru yose asabwa n'ingodo kugira ngo:




- Kumenya imirima mu mazina;
- Huza umwanya wose (n’agaciro kawo) n’ubwoko bw’urutonde rukomeye rwasobanuwe mumumasezerano;
- Menya ibikorwa bitandukanye vyemewe n’ingene wovyubaka.


Igihe Ahakorerwa ibintu hamaze kwinjizwa, Ingodo irashobora kwerekana ne'amasezeramo no gusaba imigenderanire ku wuyikoresha.


### Ibikoresho vyashizweho n'ishirahamwe LNP/BP


Mu bidukikije vya RGB, Ahaokorerwa ibintu hakoreshwa mu gutanga insiguro kandi ikoreshwa ku makuru n'imikorere y'aasezerano. Ahakorerwa ibintu rero yuzuza igicapo, idondora Uko ishoramari rimeza imbere (ubwoko bukomeye, inyandiko zo kwemeza, n’ibindi). Muri iki gice, turaza kuraba ahakorerwa ibintu zisanzwe zateguwe n’ishirahamwe LNP/BP ku bwoko rusangi bwa amasezerano (ibimenyetso bishobora guhinduka, NFT, n’ibindi).


Nk’ukwibutsa, iciyumviro ni uko ahakporera ibintu hose isigura ingene yogaragaza no gukoresha Amasezerano ku ruhande rw'ingodo, ikavuga neza amazina y’ibibanza (nk’i `spec`, `ticker`, `issuedSupply`...) kandi igasobanura ibikorwa bishoboka (nk’i, `T `Guhindura izina`...). Ahakorerwa ibintu henshi nyinshi zirasanzwe zikora, ariko hazoba izindi muri kazoza.


#### Ibikoresho bimwe bimwe vyiteguye gukoreshwa


**RGB20** n'ahakorerwa ibintu ku mitungo ishobora guhinduka, ishobora kugereranywa n’itegeko rya Ethereum ERC20. Ariko rero, iratera intambwe imbere, itanga ibikorwa vyinshi:




- Nk’akarorero, ubushobozi bwo guhindura izina ry’umutungo (guhindura *ticker* canke izina ryose) umaze gusohoka, canke guhindura ukuri kwawo (*stock splits*);
- Ishobora kandi gusobanura uburyo bwo gusubira gusohora ubwa kabiri (bifise aho bigarukira canke bitagira aho bigarukira) no guturira hanyuma bikasubirizwa, kugira ngo bihe uburenganzira uwubitanga bwo gusenya no gusubira kurema ivy’ubutunzi mu gihe hari ibintu bimwebimwe;


Nk’akarorero, RGB20 Ahakorerwa ibintu hashobora guhuzwa n’umugambi wa **Itunga Ridashobora Gufutwa (NIA)**, utegeka Ugusaba ibintu y’intango idashobora gufutwa, canke n’iyindi migambi iteye imbere cane nk’uko bisabwa.


**RGB21** yerekeye amasezerano y’ubwoko bwa NFT, canke mu buryo bwagutse, ibirimwo vyose vy’ubuhinga bwa none, nk’uguserukira ibinyamakuru vy’ubuhinga bwa none (amashusho, umuziki, n’ibindi). Uretse gusobanura ikibazo no kwimurira umutungo umwe, harimwo n’ibintu nk’ibi:




- Infashanyo yunze ubumwe yo gushiramwo dosiye (ishika kuri 16 MB) mumasezerano (kugira ngo umuntu ayironke ku ruhande rw’umukiriya);
- Ubushobozi bwa nyen'itongo bwo kwinjira "*igicapo*" muri kahise kugira ngo yerekane Koyitirirwa ikintu ca kera ya NFT.


**RGB25** ni urugero rw'ivy'ubuhinga buhurikiyemwo ibintu bishobora guhinduka n'ibidashobora guhinduka. Igenewe imitungo ishobora guhinduka igice, nk'uguhindura ikimenyetso c'amazu, aho ushaka gucapura umutungo mu gihe uguma ufise uruja n'uruza rw'umutungo w'umuzi umwe (mu yandi majambo, ufise ibice vy'inzu bishobora guhinduka, bihuye n'inzu idashobora guhinduka). Mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, ahakorerwa ibintu ishobora guhuzwa n'**Itunga Rishobora Gukusanywa (CFA) Igicapo**, ifata mu muzirikanyi iciyumviro co gucapura mu gihe ikurikirana itunga ry'intango.


#### Ibikoresho biriko birategurwa


Ibindi bikoresho biteguwe gukoreshwa mu buryo bwihariye, ariko ntibiraboneka:




- **RGB22**, yihariye ku bijanye n'ibimenyetso vy'ubuhinga bwa none, kugira ngo icunge ibimenyetso n'imirongo ya On-Chain mu bidukikije vya RGB;
- **RGB23**, ku gutera ikidodo c'igihe giteye imbere, ukoresheje bimwe mu vyiyumviro vya *Opentimestamps*, ariko n'ibiranga gukurikirana;
- **RGB24**, igamije gukorana n'uburyo bw'amazina y'itongo (DNS) busa n'ubwa *Serivisi y'izina rya Ethereum*;
- **RGB26**, igenewe gucunga ama DAO (**Ishirahamwe ryigenga ryegerejwe**) mu buryo bugoranye cane (ubutegetsi, amatora, n'ibindi);
- **RGB30**, isa cane na RGB20 ariko ifise ubudasa bwo kwitwararika ugusohoka kw'intango kwegerejwe no gukoresha Ivyagutse vy'uko bimeze. Ivyo vyokoreshwa ku mitungo iyo gusubira gusohoka kwayo icungiwe n'inzego nyinshi, canke ikaba ishingiye ku bintu vyiza kuruta.


Ego ni ko, bivanye n’itariki ubona kuri iri shure, izo nzira zishobora kuba zisanzwe zikora kandi zishobora gukoreshwa.


#### Akarorero k'ahakorerwa ibintu


Iyi kode ya Rust yerekana [RGB20](umutungo ushobora guhinduka). Iyi kode yakuwe muri dosiye `rgb20.rs` iri mu bubiko bw'ibitabu bwa RGB. Reka tuvyihweze kugira ngo dutahure imiterere ya Interface n’ingene itanga ikiraro hagati, ku ruhande rumwe, Business Logic (isobanuwe muri Schema) n’ibikorwa vyerekanwa n’amasakoshi n’abakoresha.


```rust
// ...
fn rgb20() -> Iface {
let types = StandardTypes::with(rgb20_stl());

Iface {
version: VerNo::V1,
name: tn!("RGB20"),
global_state: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("spec") => GlobalIface::required(types.get("RGBContract.DivisibleAssetSpec")),
fname!("data") => GlobalIface::required(types.get("RGBContract.ContractData")),
fname!("created") => GlobalIface::required(types.get("RGBContract.Timestamp")),
fname!("issuedSupply") => GlobalIface::one_or_many(types.get("RGBContract.Amount")),
fname!("burnedSupply") => GlobalIface::none_or_many(types.get("RGBContract.Amount")),
fname!("replacedSupply") => GlobalIface::none_or_many(types.get("RGBContract.Amount")),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("inflationAllowance") => AssignIface::public(OwnedIface::Amount, Req::NoneOrMore),
fname!("updateRight") => AssignIface::public(OwnedIface::Rights, Req::Optional),
fname!("burnEpoch") => AssignIface::public(OwnedIface::Rights, Req::Optional),
fname!("burnRight") => AssignIface::public(OwnedIface::Rights, Req::NoneOrMore),
fname!("assetOwner") => AssignIface::private(OwnedIface::Amount, Req::NoneOrMore),
},
valencies: none!(),
genesis: GenesisIface {
metadata: Some(types.get("RGBContract.IssueMeta")),
global: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("spec") => ArgSpec::required(),
fname!("data") => ArgSpec::required(),
fname!("created") => ArgSpec::required(),
fname!("issuedSupply") => ArgSpec::required(),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("assetOwner") => ArgSpec::many(),
fname!("inflationAllowance") => ArgSpec::many(),
fname!("updateRight") => ArgSpec::optional(),
fname!("burnEpoch") => ArgSpec::optional(),
},
valencies: none!(),
errors: tiny_bset! {
SUPPLY_MISMATCH,
INVALID_PROOF,
INSUFFICIENT_RESERVES
},
},
transitions: tiny_bmap! {
tn!("Transfer") => TransitionIface {
optional: false,
metadata: None,
globals: none!(),
inputs: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("previous") => ArgSpec::from_non_empty("assetOwner"),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("beneficiary") => ArgSpec::from_non_empty("assetOwner"),
},
valencies: none!(),
errors: tiny_bset! {
NON_EQUAL_AMOUNTS
},
default_assignment: Some(fname!("beneficiary")),
},
tn!("Issue") => TransitionIface {
optional: true,
metadata: Some(types.get("RGBContract.IssueMeta")),
globals: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("issuedSupply") => ArgSpec::required(),
},
inputs: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("used") => ArgSpec::from_non_empty("inflationAllowance"),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("beneficiary") => ArgSpec::from_many("assetOwner"),
fname!("future") => ArgSpec::from_many("inflationAllowance"),
},
valencies: none!(),
errors: tiny_bset! {
SUPPLY_MISMATCH,
INVALID_PROOF,
ISSUE_EXCEEDS_ALLOWANCE,
INSUFFICIENT_RESERVES
},
default_assignment: Some(fname!("beneficiary")),
},
tn!("OpenEpoch") => TransitionIface {
optional: true,
metadata: None,
globals: none!(),
inputs: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("used") => ArgSpec::from_required("burnEpoch"),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("next") => ArgSpec::from_optional("burnEpoch"),
fname!("burnRight") => ArgSpec::required()
},
valencies: none!(),
errors: none!(),
default_assignment: Some(fname!("burnRight")),
},
tn!("Burn") => TransitionIface {
optional: true,
metadata: Some(types.get("RGBContract.BurnMeta")),
globals: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("burnedSupply") => ArgSpec::required(),
},
inputs: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("used") => ArgSpec::from_required("burnRight"),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("future") => ArgSpec::from_optional("burnRight"),
},
valencies: none!(),
errors: tiny_bset! {
SUPPLY_MISMATCH,
INVALID_PROOF,
INSUFFICIENT_COVERAGE
},
default_assignment: None,
},
tn!("Replace") => TransitionIface {
optional: true,
metadata: Some(types.get("RGBContract.BurnMeta")),
globals: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("replacedSupply") => ArgSpec::required(),
},
inputs: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("used") => ArgSpec::from_required("burnRight"),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("beneficiary") => ArgSpec::from_many("assetOwner"),
fname!("future") => ArgSpec::from_optional("burnRight"),
},
valencies: none!(),
errors: tiny_bset! {
NON_EQUAL_AMOUNTS,
SUPPLY_MISMATCH,
INVALID_PROOF,
INSUFFICIENT_COVERAGE
},
default_assignment: Some(fname!("beneficiary")),
},
tn!("Rename") => TransitionIface {
optional: true,
metadata: None,
globals: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("new") => ArgSpec::from_required("spec"),
},
inputs: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("used") => ArgSpec::from_required("updateRight"),
},
assignments: tiny_bmap! {
fname!("future") => ArgSpec::from_optional("updateRight"),
},
valencies: none!(),
errors: none!(),
default_assignment: Some(fname!("future")),
},
},
extensions: none!(),
error_type: types.get("RGB20.Error"),
default_operation: Some(tn!("Transfer")),
type_system: types.type_system(),
}
}
```


Ahakorerwa ibintu, turabona ibisa n’imiterere y'Igicapo: turasanga itangazo ry'uko bimeze muri rusangi, Ibihugu vy’Umutungo, Ibikorwa vy'amasezerano (Itanguriro n’Impinduka), hamwe n’ugutorera umuti amakosa. Ariko Ahakorerwa ibintu yibanda ku kwerekana no gukoresha iz'ibintu vy'ingodo canke ikindi gikorwa ico ari co cose.


Itandukaniro riri hagati y'igicapo n’ubwoko bwavyo. Igicapo gikoresha ubwoko bukomeye (nk'ubwoko `Ubwoko::Unsigned64Bit`) n'ibindi bimenyetso vy'ubuhinga. Ahakoresha amazina y'ibibanza, ama macro (`izina ry'f!()`, `tn!()`), n'ibisobanuro vy'imigwi y'imvo (`ArgSpec`, `Igishushanyo::Uburenganzira`...). Intumbero aha ni ugufasha gutahura no gutunganya ibikorwa mungodo.


Ikindi, Ahakorerwa ibintu ishobora gushiramwo ibindi bikorwa y'igicapo y'ishimikiro (nk'ugucungera uburenganzira bwa `burnEpoch`), igihe cose ivyo biguma bihuye n'ubwenge bwa nyuma bwemejwe ku ruhande rw'umukiriya. Igice ca AluVM "inyandiko" mugicapo kizotuma habaho ukuri kw'inyandiko, ahakorerwa ibintu isigura ingene umukoresha (canke Ingodo) akorana n'izo ntara n'ihinduka.


#### Ukobimeze murirusangi n’Ibikorwa


Mu gice ca `ukobimeze murirusangi`, dusanga ivyicaro nka `spec` (insobanuro y'umutungo), `amakuru`, `yaremwe`, `Itanga`, `Itanga yaturiwe`, `Itanga yasubirijwe`. Ivyo ni ibibanza vy'ingodo ishobora gusoma no gushikiriza. Nk'akarorero:




- `spec` izokwerekana imiterere ya token;
- `issuedSupply` canke `burnedSupply` biduha umubare wose w'ibimenyetso vyasohowe canke vyaturiwe, n'ibindi.


Mu gice ca `ibikorwa`, turasobanura uruhara canke uburenganzira butandukanye. Nk'akarorero:




- `assetOwner` ihuye n'ugufata ibimenyetso (ni *Owned State* ishobora guhinduka);
- `burnRight` ihuye n'ubushobozi bwo guturira ibimenyetso;
- updateRight` ihuye n'uburenganzira bwo guhindura izina ry'umutungo.


Ijambo ry'ingenzi `ry'abantu bose' canke 'ry'ibanga` (nk'akarorero `AssignIface::iry'abantu bose(...)`) ryerekana nimba izo ntara ziboneka (`abantu bose`) canke ibanga (`ibanga`). Naho `Req::NtaCankeIbindi`, `Req::Ihitamwo`, vyerekana ivyitezwe.


#### Itanguriro n'uko bihinduka


Igice c' `itanguriro` kidondora ingene umutungo utangura:




- Ivyo `ibisobanuro`, `amakuru`, `vyaremwe`, `vyasohowe` ni ngombwa (`ArgSpec::bisabwa()`);
- Ibikorwa nka `assetOwner` bishobora kuba biri mu makopi menshi (`ArgSpec::many()`), bikaba vyemerera ibimenyetso gukwiragizwa ku bafise benshi b'intango;
- Ivyimburwa nka `Igihe c'Iterambere` canke `Igihe c'Igihe` bishobora (canke ntibishobora) gushirwa muri Genesis.


Hanyuma, ku Nzira yose (`Kwimurira`, `Ikibazo`, `Guturira`...), Ahakorerwa ibintu isigura ivyicaro igikorwa citeze nk'inyungu, ivyicaro igikorwa kizotanga nk'isohoka, n'amakosa yose yoshobora kubaho. Nk'akarorero:


**Guhinduka:**




- Ivyinjijwe: `ibiheruka` → bitegerezwa kuba `Uwufise umutungo`;
- Umwimenyerezo: `uwubikoresha` → utegezwa kuba `Uwufise umutungo` mushasha;
- Ikosa: `AMAHERA_BITANGANA_` (ingodo izoshobora rero gukorana n'ibibazo aho igitigiri cinjira kidahuye n'igitigiri gisohoka).


**Ikibazo `Impinduka`:**




- Ntibitegerezwa (`Uguhitamwo: ukuri`), nk'uko ivyimburwa vy'inyongera bitakoreshwa vy'ukuri;
- Ivyinjijwe: `vyakoreshejwe` → `Ugukingira itakaza ry'agaciro`, ni ukuvuga uruhusha rwo kwongerako ibindi bimenyetso;
- Ivyutegerezwa : `uwuronka inyungu` (ibimenyetso bishasha vyaronswe) n' `akazoza` (ibisigaye `Ugukingira yitakaza ry'agaciro`);
- Amakosa ashoboka: `GUTANGA_NTIBIHUYE`, `IKIBAZO_KIRENZE_IBIMENYETSO`, n'ibindi.


**Ihinduka ry'uguturira:**




- Ivyinjijwe: `vyakoreshejwe` → a `Ivyogukuramwo iburyo`;
- Ivyo murirusangi: `Ivyo Gutanga` vyaturitse` birakenewe;
- Inshingano: `kazoza` → ugukomeza gushoboka kwa `Ivyogukuramwo iburyo` nimba tutaturiye vyose;
- Amakosa: `GUTANGA_BITAHURA`, `IKIMENYETSO_KIDAKORA`, `IBIMENYETSO_BITAHAGIJE`.


Burigikorwa cose rero kiradondaguwe mu buryo bushobora gusomwa kungodo. Ivyo bituma bishoboka kugaragaza igishushanyo Ahakorerwa ibitu aho umukoresha ashobora kubona neza: "Ufise uburenganzira bwo gukuraha. Woba wipfuza gukuramwo igitogiri kanaka? Kode irazi kwuzuza umwanya wa `Gukuramwo ibisabwa` maze ikagenzura ko `  Gukuramwo iburyo` ari ukuri."


Mu ncamake, birahambaye kwibuka ahakorerwa ibintu, naho yoba yuzuye gute, ubwayo itasobanura ivyiyumviro vy'imbere vy'amasezerano. Umutima w’igikorwa ukorwa n' **igicapo**, uimwo ubwoko bukomeye, imiterere y'itanguriro, inzira z’uguhinduka n’ibindi. Ahakorerwa ibintu gusa igaragaza z'ivyobintu mu buryo busanzwe kandi bufise izina, kugira ngo zikoreshwe mu gikorwa.


Kubera ubuhinga bwa RGB, Ahakorerwa ibintu harashobora gusubirwamwo (nk'akarorero, mu kwongerako `Guhindura izina`, gukosora iyerekanwa ry'umurima, n'ibindi) ataco ukeneye kwandika Amasezerano yose. Abakoresha ahakorerwa ibintu harashobora rero kwungukira kuri ivyo bintu vyiza, bakimara guhindura dosiye `.RGB` canke `.rgba`.


Ariko umaze gutangaza Ahakorerwa ibintu, ukeneye kuyihuza n;igicapo bihuye. Ibi bikorwa biciye kuri ***Ahakorerwa ibintu***, igaragaza ingene woshiramwo ikarita y'umwanya wose ufise izina (nk'izina ry'f!("Nyitungo")`) ku ikaranga ibintu ikomeye (nk'iyi `OS_ASSET`) isobanuwe murikinogicapo . Ivyo bituma, nk'akarorero, iyo Ingodo ikoresheje ibintu wa `burnRight`, iyo ni yo nzira, mugicapo, Isigura ubuhobozi bwo guturira ibimenyetso.


### Ahakorerwa ibintu


Mu nyubakwa ya RGB, twabonye ko igice cose (Igicapo, Ahakorerwa ibintu, n’ibindi) gishobora gutegurwa no gukoranirizwa ku giti caco. Ariko rero, haracariho ikintu kimwe gihambaye gihuza ivyo bice vy'inyubako bitandukanye: ***Ahakorerwa ibintu***. Ivyo ni vyo bigaragaza neza ibimenyetso canke ivyicaro vyasiguwe muri mugicapo (ku ruhande rwa Uko ishoramari rimeze) ku mazina yamenyeshejwe Ahakorerwa ibintu (ku ruhande rw’ugushikiriza n’ugukorana n’abakoresha). Rero iyongodo ishize Amasezerano, irashobora gutahura neza neza ikibanza gihuye n'iki, n'ingene igikorwa citwa Ahakorerwa ibintu gifitaniye isano n'ubwenge bw'igicapo.


Iciyumviro gihambaye ni uko Interface Ahakorerwa ibintu atari ngombwa ko igaragaza ibikorwa vyose vy'igicapo, canke ivyicaro vyose vy'ahakorerwa ibintu: ishobora kugarukira ku gice gitoyi. Mu bikorwa, ivyo bituma bishoboka kubuza canke gucungera imice imwimwe y'igicapo. Nk'akarorero, woshobora kugira Igicapo ifise ubwoko bune bw'ibikorwa, ariko Ahakorerwa ibintu igaragaza bibiri gusa muri vyo mu gihe kinaka. Ku rundi ruhande, iyo ahakorerwa ibintu hatanga izindi ntumbero z’iherezo, turashobora guhitamwo kutazishira mu ngiro hano.


Aha ni akarorero ka kera k'ahakorerwa ibintu, aho dufatanya *Itunga Ridashobora Gufutwa* (NIA) Igicapo na RGB20 IAhakorerwa ibintu:


```rust
fn nia_rgb20() -> IfaceImpl {
let schema = nia_schema();
let iface = Rgb20::iface();

IfaceImpl {
version: VerNo::V1,
schema_id: schema.schema_id(),
iface_id: iface.iface_id(),
script: none!(),
global_state: tiny_bset! {
NamedField::with(GS_NOMINAL, fname!("spec")),
NamedField::with(GS_DATA, fname!("data")),
NamedField::with(GS_TIMESTAMP, fname!("created")),
NamedField::with(GS_ISSUED_SUPPLY, fname!("issuedSupply")),
},
assignments: tiny_bset! {
NamedField::with(OS_ASSET, fname!("assetOwner")),
},
valencies: none!(),
transitions: tiny_bset! {
NamedType::with(TS_TRANSFER, tn!("Transfer")),
},
extensions: none!(),
}
}
```


Muri iyi Nshirwa mu ngiro ry'ahakorerwa ibintu:




- Turavuga neza Igicapo, biciye ku `nia_schema()`, n'ahakorerwa ibintu, biciye ku `Rgb20::iface()`. Ivyo bimenyetso bikoreshwa kugira ngo ahakorerwa ibintu  ku ruhande rwo gukoranya (ivyo bifatanya ibimenyetso vy'ibanga vy'ivyo bice bibiri);
- Ikarata ishirwaho hagati ya y'ibntuvy'igicapo n'ahakorerwa ibintu. Nk'akarorero, `GS_NOMINAL` umwanya mugicappo uhuye n'ikidodo `"spec"` ku ruhande rw'ahakorerwa ibintu (`UmwanyaWizina::na(GS_IZINA, fizina!("spec"))`). Turakora ukwo nyene ku bikorwa, nka `TS_TRANSFER`, ivyo duhuza na `"Kwimurira"` ahakorerwa ibintu...;
- Turashobora kubona ko ata n’imwe ifise ubushobozi (`ubushobozi: nta n’umwe!()`) canke ivyungura (`ivyungura: nta n’imwe!()`), bikaba vyerekana ko iy'amasezerano ya NIA idakoresha ivyo bimenyetso.


Igisubizo inyuma yo gukoranya n'idosiye itandukanye `.RGB` canke `.rgba`, izokwinjizwa mungodo yongerako Igicapo n'ahakorerwa ibintu. Gutyo, iyo porogarama irazi ingene yohuza neza iyiamsezerano ya NIA (iyo ivyiyumviro vyayo bidondora n'igicapo yayo) na "RGB20" Ahakorerwa ibintu (itanga amazina y'abantu n'uburyo bwo gukorana n'ibimenyetso bishobora guhinduka), ikoresha iyi GW-166 nk'inzira ibiri hagati y'ivyo bibiri.


#### Ni kuki twotandukanya Ahakorerwa ibintu?


Gutandukana biratuma umuntu ashobora guhindura uko abona ibintu. Igicapo kimwe coshobora kugira Ibikorwa vyinshi bitandukanye vy'ahakorerwa ibintu, kimwe cose kikaba kigaragaza ibikorwa bitandukanye. Ikindi, Ahakorerwa ibintu ubwayo birashobora guhinduka canke gusubira kwandikwa ataco bisaba guhindura haba mugicapo canke Ahakorerwa ibintu. Ivyo bigumya ingingo ngenderwako ya RGB y’uguhinduranya: igice cose (Igicapo, Ahakorerwa ibintu,Ahakorerwa ibintu ija mungiro) gishobora guhindurwa no guhindurwa kidasanzwe, igihe cose amategeko y’uguhuza yashizweho n’amasezerano yubahirijwe (ibimenyetso bimwe, uguhuza ubwoko, n’ibindi).


Mu gukoresha beton, iy'ngodo itwara Amasezerano, itegerezwa:




- Ishiremwo ry'**Igicapo** yashizwe hamwe (kugira ngo umenye uko ishoramari rimeze);
- Ugushiramwo **Ahakorerwa ibintu** (kugira ngo utahure amazina n'ibikorwa vyo ku ruhande rw'ukoresha);
- Umuzigo washizwe hamwe **Ahakorerwa ibintubishirwa mungiro** (kugira ngo uhuze ubuhinga bw'Igicapo n'amazina y'ahakorerwa ibintu, igikorwa ku gikorwa, Ahantukuhantu).


Ubu buhinga bwo kwubaka buratuma bishoboka gukoresha ibintu nk'ibi:




- Guhagarika ibikorwa bimwebimwe ku bakoresha bamwebamwe: gutanga igice c’Ishirwa mu ngiro c'ahakorerwa ibintu gitanga gusa uburenganzira bwo gukoresha amafaranga y’ishimikiro, ata gutanga ibikorwa vyo guturira canke guhindura, nk’akarorero;
- Guhindura ukuntu ivyerekanywe: guhingura Ahakorerwa ibintu ihindura izina ry’umurima uri muhakorerwa ibintu canke ukayishushanya mu buryo butandukanye, ata guhindura ishingiro ry'amasezerano;
- Gushigikira imigambi myinshi: Ingodo ishobora gushiramwo Ibikorwa vyinshi vy'ahakorerwa ibintu ku bwoko bumwe bw'ahakorerwa ibintu, kugira ngo ikoreshe imigambi itandukanye (imirongo itandukanye ya token), igihe cose imiterere yayo ihuye.


Mu gice gikurikira, turaza kuraba ingene uguhererekanya amafaranga y'Amasezerano gukora, n’ingene amafagitire ya RGB akora.


## Amaseerano kwimurira


<chapterId>f043a307-d420-5752-b0d7-ebfd845802c0</chapterId>


:::id ya videwo=75eb5a8d-1910-4155-b5e3-81204c9a8901:::


Muri iki gice, turaza gusuzuma ingene Amasezerano agenda mubihabera vya RGB. Kugira ngo ivyo tubigereranye, turaza kuraba Alice na Bob, abakinyi bacu basanzwe, bipfuza ko Ihanahanwa iba umutungo wa RGB. Tuzokwereka kandi ibice bimwe bimwe vy'amabwirizwa bivuye mu gikoresho c'umurongo w'amabwirizwa `RGB`, kugira ngo turabe ingene bikora mu bikorwa.


### Gutahura amasezerano ya RGB kwimurira


Reka dufate akarorero k'uguhindura hagati ya Alice na Bob. Muri aka karorero, twiyumvira ko Bob ariko aratangura gukoresha RGB, mu gihe Alice asanzwe afise itunga rya RGB mungodo yiwe. Turabona ingene Bob ashiraho ibikotresho vyiwe, akazana Amasezerano bibereye, hanyuma agasaba kwimurirwa kuri Alice, n'ingene Alice akora igikorwa nyaco kuri Blockchain ya Bitcoin.


#### 1) Gushiramwo Ingo ya RGB


Mbere na mbere, Bob akeneye gushiramwo Ingodo ya RGB, ni ukuvuga porogarama ihuye n’itegeko. Ivyo nta masezerano arimwo mu ntango. Bob nawe nyene azokenera:




- Igikoresho c'ingodo ya Bitcoin co gucunga ama UTXO yawe;
- Ihuzwa n’ikidodo ca Bitcoin (canke n’umurongo wa Electrum), kugira ngo ushobore kumenya UTXO zawe no gukwiragiza amafaranga yawe ku rubuga.


Nk’ukwibutsa, **Ibihugu vy’Igihugu** muri RGB vyerekeye UTXO za Bitcoin. Tubwirizwa rero kwama dushobora gucunga no gukoresha UTXOs mu bikorwa vya Bitcoin birimwo amasezerano y’ubuhinga bwa none (`Tapret` canke `Opret`) yerekana amakuru ya RGB.


#### 2) Amasezerano kuronka amakuru


Bob rero arakeneye kugarura amakuru y'amasezerano akunda. Aya makuru ashobora gukwiragira biciye ku nzira iyo ari yo yose: urubuga, e-mail, ubutumwa... Mu bikorwa, ashirwa hamwe muri ***Gushiramwo ibintu***, ni ukuvuga agapaki gatoyi k'amakuru karimwo:




- **Intanguriro**, isigura uko Amasezerano yari ameze muntango;
- **Igicapo**, Gisobanura uko ishoramari rimeze (ubwoko bukomeye, inyandiko zo kwemeza, n’ibindi);
- **Ahakorerwa ibintu**, isobanura ikiganiro Layer (amazina y'ibibanza, ibikorwa bishobora gushikwako);
- **Ahakorerwa ibintu bishirwa mungiro**, ihuza neza Igicapo na ahakorerwa ibintu.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/075.webp)


Ingano yose hamwe akenshi iba ingana n’amakilobyte makeyi, kuko igice kimwekimwe cose muri rusangi gipima amabayite makeyi. Bishobora kandi gushoboka gutangaza iyi Consignment muri Base58, biciye ku nzira zidashobora gucengera (nka Nostr canke biciye ku Lightning Network, nk’akarorero), canke nk’akarorero ka kode ya QR .


#### 3) Kwinjiza no kwemeza amasserano


Igihe Bob amaze kwakira Ishirwamwo, arayishira mungodo ya RGB yiwe. Ivyo bizoheza:




- Suzuma ko Utanguriro n'Igicapo gifise akamaro;
- Umuzigo w'ahakorerwa ibintu na ahakorerwa ibintu;
- Kuvugurura amakuru y'umuguzi wawe Stash.


Bob ubu arashobora kubona umutungo uri mungodo yiwe (naho yoba atarawugira) agatahura ibibanza bihari, ibikorwa bishoboka... Aca akenera guhamagara umuntu afise vy’ukuri uwo mutungo azokwimurirwa. Mu karorero kacu, uyo ni Alice.


Inzira yo kumenya uwufise umutungo kanaka wa RGB isa n’ukurondera uwuyitanga Bitcoin. Ivyerekeye iyo nzira y’uguhuza bivana n’ikoreshwa (amasoko, imihora y’ubutumwa bwigenga, gutanga fagitire, ugurisha ibintu n’ibikorwa, umushahara...).


#### 4) Gutanga urupapuro rwa Fagitire


Kugira ngo utangure kwimurira umutungo wa RGB, Bob ategerezwa kubanza gutanga Fagitire. Iyi Fagitire ikoreshwa mu:




- Bwira Alice ubwoko bw'igikorwa kizokorwa (nk'akarorero, `Ukwimurira` kuva kuri RGB20 Ahakorerwa ibintu);
- Gutanga Alice *Insiguro ya Serire* ya Bob (ni ukuvuga UTXO aho yipfuza kwakira umutungo);
- Sigura igitigiri w’ibintu bikora bisabwa (nk’akarorero, ibice 100).


Bob akoresha igikoresho `RGB` ku murongo w'amabwirizwa. Twibaze ko ashaka ibice 100 vya token `ikiranga ikintuc'amasezerano` caco kizwi, ashaka kwizigira `Tapret`, kandi agasobanura UTXO yayo (`456e3..dfe1:0`):


```bash
bob$ rgb invoice RGB20 100 <ContractId> tapret1st:456e3..dfe1:0
```


Turaza kuraba nezauko amafagitireameze ya RGB mu mpera y’iki kigabane.


#### 5) Ugutanga Fagitire


Fagitire yashizweho (nk'akarorero nk'URL: `RGB:2WBcas9.../RGB20/100+utxob:...`) irimwo amakuru yose Alice akeneye gutunga ngo ategure ukwimurira. Nk'uko biri mubitangwa, ishobora gushirwa mu buryo bubereye (Base58 canke ubundi buryo) maze ikarungikwa biciye ku butumwa, e-mail, Nostr...


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/076.webp)


#### 6) Gutegura ibikorwa ku ruhande rwa Alice


Alice yakira fagitire ya Bob. Mu gitabu ciwe c'ingodo ya RGB, afise igitabu ca Stash kirimwo umutungo azokwimurirwa. Kugira ngo akoreshe UTXO irimwo umutungo, ategerezwa kubanza gutanga PSBT (*Partially Signed Bitcoin Transaction*), ni ukuvuga Bitcoin idatunganye, akoresheje UTXO afise:


```bash
alice$ wallet construct tx.psbt
```


Iyi nzira y'ishimikiro (itashizweko umukono muri iki gihe) izokoreshwa kuri Ukwiyemeza kwimbitse kw'ibanga ihuye n'uguhindura kuri Bob. Alice azokoreshwa, kandi mu gisohoka, tuzoshiramwo `Tapret` canke `Opret` Ukwiyemeza kwa Bob.


#### 7) Uruvyaro rw'uguhindura ibishirwamwo


Inyuma y'aho, Alice yubaka ***Ibishirwamwo vyanyuma*** (rimwe na rimwe yitwa "kwimurira Ibishirwamwo") biciye kwitegeko:


```bash
alice$ rgb transfer tx.psbt <invoice> consignment.rgb
```


Iyi dosiye nshasha irimwo:




- Amateka yose y’Impinduka za Leta zasabwa kugira ngo umutungo wemezwe gushika n’ubu (kuva kw'Itanguriro);
- Itegeko rishasha ry'Ukobihinduka ryimura ivy’ubutunzi kuva kuri Alice rikaja muri Bob, hakurikijwe fagiture ya Bob ryasohoye;
- Igikorwa kidatunganye ca Bitcoin (*Ihanahanwa ry'icabona*) (`tx.PSBT`), gikoresha Alice ca Alice, cahinduwe kugira ngo kigiremwo Ukwiyemeza kwa Bob.


Muri iki gihe, iyo nzira y’ugucuruza ntiyigeze itangazwa ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin. Ibitagwa ni nini kuruta Ibitangwa vy’ishimikiro, kuko irimwo kahise kose (*uruzitiro rw’ibimenyamenya*) kugira ngo yerekane ko umutungo ubereye.


#### 8) Bob aragenura kandi yemera Ibitangwa


Alice arungika **Ahanyuma bishikira** kwa Bob. Bob azoca:




- Gusuzuma ko igitabu c'uko bihinduka gifise ukuri (kumenya ko kahise gahuye, ko amategeko y'amasezerano yubahirizwa, n’ibindi);
- Wongereko Stash yo mu karere iwanyu;
- Birashoboka ko gutanga umukono (`sig:...`) kubitangwa, kugira ngo yerekane ko yasuzumwe kandi yemejwe (rimwe na rimwe yitwa "*igitabu c'umushahara*").


```bash
bob$ rgb accept consignment.rgb
sig:DbwzvSu4BZU81jEpE9FVZ3xjcyuTKWWy2gmdnaxtACrS
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/077.webp)


#### 9) Uburyo: Bob arungika ivyemeza kwa Alice (*igitabu c'amahera*)


Nimba Bob abishaka, arashobora gusubiza icogikumu kwa Alice. Ivyo vyerekana:




- Ko yemera ko iyo mpinduka ari ngirakamaro;
- Ko yemera ko igikorwa ca Bitcoin gishirwa ahabona.


Ivyo si ngombwa, ariko birashobora gutuma Alice yizera ko ata ntambara zizokurikira ku bijanye n’uguhindurwa.


#### 10) Alice ishira umukono kandi atangaza ivy’ugucuruza


Alice ashobora rero:




- Gusuzuma ikidodo ca Bob (`RGB suzuma <sig>`);
- Gusinya kw' *Ihanahanwa ry'icabona* ikiri ikimenyetso ca PSBT (`Ikimenyetso c'ingodo`);
- GusohoraIhanahanwa ry'icabona ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin (`-sohora`).


```bash
alice$ rgb check <sig>
alice$ wallet sign —publish tx.psbt
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/078.webp)


Iyo yemejwe, iyo nzira y’ugucuruza ikimenyetso c’iherezo ry’ugutanga. Bob aba ari we nyen’umutungo mushasha: ubu afise Ikintu gifashwe munzira yerekana UTXO igenzura, ivyo bikaba vyemezwa n’ukubaho kw'ukwiyemeza mu gucuruza.


Mu ncamake, ng’iyi inzira yose yo kwimurira:


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/079.webp)


### Akamaro kokurungika na RGB




- **Ibanga**:


Alice na Bob nibo bonyene bashobora kuronka amakuru yose y'ihinduka. Bahanahanira ano makuru hanze ya Blockchain, biciye mukurugikwa. Ivyemezo vy’ubuhinga bwa none bw'ukunyegeza inkuru, mwihanahanwa rya Bitcoin ntibishira ahabona ubwoko b'imitungo canke igitigiri c'amahera, ivyo bikaba bitanga ibanga rikingiwe cane kuruta ibindi izindi sisitemu y'ama token yokuri On-Chain.




- **Kwemeza uruhande rw'umuguzi**:


Bob arashobora kugenzura ukuntu ivyo kurungika abigereranije n' **Ibirungikwa** n'ibishinga imizi muri Blockchain ya Bitcoin. Ntakeneye kobirinda biremezwa n'umuntu n'uwundi. Alice ntibikenewe ko yirigwa arashira kukarubandaa kahise kose kuri Blockchain, ivyo bigabanya umuzigo ku bijanye nuko n'umurongo w'ishimikiro kandi bikongerereza ibanga.




- **Ugucagagura muduce vyoroshe**:


Ihanahanwa rigoye (ihanahanwa ry'uduce dutoyi hagati ya BTC n'umutungo wa  RGB, nk’akarorero) rishobora gukorwa mw'ihanahanwa rimwe, bikirind gukenera inyandiko za HTLC canke PTLC. Iyo amasezerano adashizwe ahabona, umuntu wese arashobora gusubira gukoresha ama UTXO yiwe mu bundi buryo.


### Igishushanyo c'incamake c'ukurungika


Imbere yo kuraba amafagitire mu buryo bwimbitse, ng’iki igishushanyo c’incamake c’urugendo rwose rw’uguhanahana ama RGB:




- Bob arashiramwo ingodo ya RGB maze akakoronka amasezerano y'ibanze y'ukurungika;
- Bob aratanga fagitire ashiramwo UTXO aho yakirira umutungo;
- Alice arakira fagitire, akubaka PSBT maze hagatanga ahogushiriramwo hanyuma;
- Bob aravyemera, agasuzuma, akongerako amakuru kuri Stash yiwe, agashirako umukono (*payslip*) iyo bikenewe;
- Alice arashira kukarubanda ihanahanwa kurubuga rwa Bitcoin;
- Ukwemeza ihanahanwa  bituma ukurungika bija mumatgeko.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/080.webp)


Irungikwa ryerekana ububasha bwose n’ugudhonora guhinduka kw’amasezerano ya RGB: Ihanahanwa ryigenga, ryrmrjwe kuruhande rw'umukiriya, ishizweho mu buryo buke kandi bw'ibanga ryinshi kuri Blockchain ya Bitcoin, kandi igumya umutekano mwiza w’amasezerano (nta woba bw'uko umuntu ashobora kuriha kabiri). Ivyo bituma RGB iba ikibanza ciza co gutanga agaciro k’ibintu bifise ibanga kandi bishobora guhindurwa kuruta blockchain za  On-Chain  zishobora gukoreshwa.


### Fagitire ya RGB


Muri kano gace, tuzosigura mu buryo bwimbitse ingene **amafagitire** akora mumuryango wa RGB n'ingene ashoboza ibikorwa (Vy'umwihariko) bikorwa vy'amasezerano. Ubwa mbere, turaza kuraba ibimenyetso bibiranga bikoreshwa, hanyuma turabe ingene bishirwa muma kode, hanyuma turabe uko fagitire imeze ishirwa ahabona nk’URL (uburyo bubereye gukoreshwa mungodo).


#### Ibiranga n'ugushira muma kode


Ikimenyetso kidasanzwe kirasigurwa kuri kimwe muribimwe mubikwirikira :




- Amasezerano ya RGB;
- N'igicapo (uko ishoramari rimeze);
- Ahakorerwa ibintu n'aho bishirirwa hanze;
- N'imitungo (token, NFT, n’ibindi),


Ukukwisa n'ikintu gihambaye cane, kuko burigace ka sisitemu gategezwa kwisa. Nk’akarorero, Amasezerano X ntategerezwa gusa n'amasezerano Y, kandi ahakorerwa ibintu bibiri bitandukanye (RGB20 vs. RGB21, nk’akarorero) birategerezwa kuba bifise ibimenyetso bitandukanye.


Kugira ngo ivyo bimenyetso bibe vyiza (vy'igipimo gito) kandi bishobore gusomwa, dukoresha:




- Ishingiro 58 rya kode, irinda gukoresha indome zitera zikora makenga (nk'akarorero `0` n'urudome `O`) kandi itanga imirongo miremire;
- Inyitangizo yerekana kamere y’ikimenyetso, akenshi mu buryo bwa `RGB:` canke URN isa n’iyo.


Nk'akarorero, `Inyidondoro y'amasezerano` yoshobora guserukirwa n'ikintu nk'iki:


```txt
rgb:2WBcas9-yjzEvGufY-9GEgnyMj7-beMNMWA8r-sPHtV1nPU-TMsGMQX
```


Inyitangizo ya `RGB:` yemeza ko iki ari ikimenyetso ca RGB, kandi atari ihuriro rya HTTP canke uwundi murongo. Kubera iyo nyitangizo, ingodo zirashobora gusigura neza urukwirikirane rw'indome.


#### Uduce tw'ivyerekana ibintu


Ivyerekana RGB akenshi aba aribirebire cane, kuko ibiciweko akarongo (ubuhinga bwo) umutekano ushobora gusaba ikibanza vy'uduce dutoyi cana 256 canke turenga. Kugira ngo umuntu ashobore gusoma no kugenzura, *duca* iyo mirongo mu bice vyinshi bitandukanijwe n'akarongo (`-`). Rero, aho kugira uruzitiro rurerure rw’ibimenyetso rudacitse, turarugabanyamwo ibice bigufi. Ico gikorwa kirasanzwe ku bijanye n’ikarata y’inguzanyo canke inomero za telefone, kandi kirakora no ngaha kugira ngo umuntu ashobore kugenzura neza. Rero, nk'akarorero, umukoresha canke umufatanyabikorwa arashobora kubwirwa ati: "*Ndagusavye usuzume ko igice ca gatatu ari `9GEgnyMj7`*", aho kugereranya vyose icarimwe. Igipande ca nyuma gikoreshwa kenshi nk'**iteranywa ry'ugusuzuma**, kugira ngo hagire uburyo bwo kumenya amakosa canke amakosa yo kwandika.


Nk'akarorero, `idanakintu y'amasezerano` mwitanguriro rya 58 rishobora kuba :


```txt
2WBcas9-yjzEvGufY-9GEgnyMj7-beMNMWA8r-sPHtV1nPU-TMsGMQX
```


Imwe muri izo nzira imenagura urukwirikirane rw'indome muduce tumwetumwe. Ivyo ntibigira ico bikoze ku nsobanuro y’itegeko, ahubwo bigira ico bikoze ku kuntu ryerekanwa gusa.


#### Gukoresha ama URLs ku mafagitire


Fagitire ya RGB itangwa nka URL. Ivyo bisigura ko umuntu ashobora kuyifyondako canke kuyisikana (nk’uko ari kode ya QR), hanyuma ingodo ishobora kuyitahura ata guca ku ruhande kugira ngo umuntu akore ihanahanwa. Ukwo gukorana kworoshe gutandukanye n’izindi nzira zimwe zimwe aho utegerezwa gukopa no gushiramwo amakuru atandukanye mu bice bitandukanye vyo muri porogarama.


Fagitire ku token ishobora guhinduka (nk'akarorero token ya RGB20 ) ishobora gusa n'iyi:


```txt
rgb:2WBcas9-yjzEvGufY-9GEgnyMj7-beMNMWA8r-sPHtV1nPU-TMsGMQX/RGB20/100+utxob:egXsFnw-5Eud7WKYn-7DVQvcPbc-rR69YmgmG-veacwmUFo-uMFKFb
```


Reka twihweze neza ino URL:




- `RGB:`** (inyitangizo): yerekana ihuriro rikoresha umurongo wa RGB (bisa n'ivyo `http:` canke `Bitcoin:` mu bindibintu);
- **igereranya**: igereranya `indangurakintuy'amasezerano` ya token ushaka gukoresha;
- `/RGB20/100`: yerekana ko `RGB20` Ahakorerwa ibintu hakoreshwa kandi ko ibice 100 vy'umutungo bisabwa. Inndime  ni: `/Ahakorerwa ibintu/Igitigiri`;
- `+utxob:`**: insiguro yuko amakuru yerekeye uwuronka UTXO (canke, mu buryo bubereye, insobanuro ya Serire ikoreshwa rimwe) yongeweko;
- **Serire**: iyi ni *blinded* UTXO (canke SInsiguro ya Serire). Mu yandi majambo, Bob yarapfutse UTXO yiwe nyayo, rero uwuyirungitse (Alice) ntazi ico Aderesi nyayo ari co. Azi gusa ko hariho Serire ikora yerekeza kuri UTXO igenzurwa na Bob.


Kuba vyose bikwira muri URL imwe bituma ubuzima bworoha ku muntu abikoresha: gufyonda canke gucapura ingodo, igikorwa kikaba giteguwe gukorwa.


Umuntu yoshobora kwiyumvira uburyo aho igiharuro coroshe (nk'akarorero `USDT`) gikoreshwa aho gukoresha `Indangamuntu y'amasezerano`. Ariko ivyo vyotuma haba ingorane zikomeye z’ukwizigirana n’umutekano: igiharuro si ikintu kidasanzwe (amasezerano menshi yoshobora kuvuga ko yitwa `USDT`). Na RGB, turashaka ikimenyetso kidasanzwe, kitagiramwo amakenga. Ni co gituma kwemera urukwirikirane rw'indome rw’ibice 256, rwashizwe muri base58 kandi rwaciwemwo ibice. Uwukoresha arazi ko ariko arakoresha neza na neza Indangakintu y'amasezerano yayo ari `2WBcas9-yjz...` atari uwundi.


#### Ibindi bipimo vya URL


Ushobora kandi kwongerako ibindi bipimo kuri URL, mu buryo bumwe na HTTP, kurya kwa :


```txt
rgb:2WBcas9-yjzEvGufY-9GEgnyMj7-beMNMWA8r-sPHtV1nPU-TMsGMQX/RGB20/100+utxob:egXsFnw-5Eud7WKYn-7DVQvcPbc-rR69YmgmG-veacwmUFo-uMFKFb?sig=6kzbKKffP6xftkxn9UP8gWqiC41W16wYKE5CYaVhmEve
```




- `?sig=...`: igereranya, nk'akarorero, umukono ufitaniye isano na Invoice, uwo amasakoshi amwe amwe ashobora kugenzura;
- Iyo Wallet idacungera iyo sinyatire, yirengagiza gusa iyo parametere.


Reka dufate urugero rwa NFT biciye ahantu hakrerwa ha RGB21. Nk’akarorero, twoshobora kuba dufise:


```txt
rgb:7BKsac8-beMNMWA8r-3GEprtFh7-bjzEvGufY-aNLuU4nSN-MRsLOIK/RGB21/DbwzvSu-4BZU81jEp-E9FVZ3xj-cyuTKWWy-2gmdnaxt-ACrS+utxob:egXsFnw-5Eud7WKYn-7DVQvcPbc-rR69YmgmG-veacwmUFo-uMFKFb
```


Aha turabona:




- `RGB:`**: Inyitangizo ya URL;
- 7BKsac8-beMNMWA8r-3GEprtFh7-bjzEvGufY-aNLuU4nSN-MRsLOIK: Ikiranga amasezerano (NFT);;
- **rGB21**: Ahakorerwa ibintu humutungo udasubirizwa  (NFT);
- **`DbwzvSu-4BZU81jEp-...`**: ivyerekeye igice kidasanzwe ca NFT, nk'akarorero Hash y'amakuru (ikimenyeshamakuru, ahabikwa amakuru...);
- `+utxob:egXsFnw-...: insiguro ya Serire.


Iciyumviro ni kimwe: kurungika linki Ingodo ishobora gutahura, rugaragaza neza umutungo udasanzwe uzorungikwa.


#### Ibindi bikorwa biciye kuri URL


URLs za RGB ntizikoreshwa gusa mu gusaba kurungika. Bashobora kandi gushiramwo ibikorwa biteye imbere cane, nk’ugutanga ama token mashasha (*issuance*). Nk'akarorero:


```txt
rgb:2WBcas9-yjzEvGufY-9GEgnyMj7-beMNMWA8r-sPHtV1nPU-TMsGMQX/RGB20/issue/100000+utxob:egXsFnw-5Eud7WKYn-7DVQvcPbc-rR69YmgmG-veacwmUFo-uMFKFb
```


Aha niho dusanga:




- `RGB:`: urukwirikirane;
- `2Ibibazo9-...`: Ikiranga amasezerano;
- `/RGB20/ikibazo/100000`: yerekana ko ushaka guhamagara "*Ikibazo*" kugira ngo ukore ayandi ma token 100.000;
- `+Igisubizo:`: Insiguro ya Serire.


Nk'akarorero, Ingodo ishobora gusoma ngo: "Nasabwe gukora igikorwa co gukuraho ikibazo kuva ahakorerwa ibintu `RGB20`, kumasezerano nk'iyo, ku bice 100.000, ku nyungu y'amasezerano nk'iyo".


None ko twabonye Ibintu nyamukuru ya porogarama ya RGB, nzobajana mu kigabane gikurikira ku buryo bwo gukora amasezerano ya RGB.


## Kwandika amasezerano ya smart contracts


<chapterId>0e0a645c-0049-588d-8965-b8c536590cc9</chapterId>


:::id ya videwo=a3ad6dcd-90b8-4272-9dfc-76c85c859167::


Muri iki gice, tuzofata intambwe ku yindi uburyo bwo kwandika Amasezerano, dukoresheje igikoresho c'umurongo w'amabwirizwa `RGB`. Intumbero ni ukwerekana ingene woshiramwo no gukoresha CLI, ugakoranya **Igicapo**, ​​ugashiramwo **Ahakorerwa ibintu** na **Aho ibintu bishirirwamungiro**, hanyuma ugatanga (*ugutanga*) umutungo. Turaza kuraba kandi ivyiyumviro bishingiyeko, harimwo n’ugukoranya n’ugushingira intahe. Mu mpera z’iki gice, ukwiye kuba ushoboye gusigura iyo nzira no kwikorera amasezerano yawe bwite ya RGB.


Nk’ukwibutsa, ubuhinga bwo mu mutima bwa RGB bushingiye ku masomero ya Rust mwebwe nk’abahinguzi, mushobora kwinjiza mu migambi yanyu kugira ngo mucunge igice c'Ukwemeza kuruhande rw'umukiriya. Ikindi, umugwi w’ishirahamwe LNP/BP uriko urakora ibijanye n’ugufatanya ibitabu vy’izindi ndimi, ariko ivyo ntibiraheza. Ikindi, izindi nzego nka Bitfinex ziriko zirategura ibirundo vyazo vy’ubufatanye (ivyo tuzobivuga mubigabane 2 vya nyuma vy’icirwa). Kugeza rero, `RGB` CLI ni co gikoreshwa mu buryo butegekanijwe, naho coba kiguma kidasukuye cane.


### Gushiramwo no gushikiriza igikoresho ca RGB


Itegeko nyamukuru ryitwa gusa `RGB`. Igenewe kwibutsa `git`, ifise amategeko mato mato yo gukoresha amasezerano, kuyahamagara, gutanga itunga n'ibindi. Ingodo ya Bitcoin ubu ntabwo iri muri iyo nkuru, ariko izoba iri mu nsiguro iri hafi (0.11). Iyi verisiyo ikurikira izotuma abakoresha bashobora gukora no gucunga ingodo yabo (biciye mu bisobanuro) kuva kuri `RGB`, harimwo n'ivya PSBT, guhuza n'ibikoresho vyo hanze (nk'akarorero Hardware Wallet) vyo gutera umukono, no gukorana na porogaramu nka Sparrow. Ivyo bizotuma igikorwa cose co gutanga no kwimurira umutungo coroha.


#### Gushiramwo biciye ku mizigo


Turashiramwo igikoresho muri Rust na:


```bash
cargo install rgb-contracts --all-features
```


(Zirikana: iyo sandugu yitwa `RGB-contracts`, kandi itegeko ryashizweho rizokwitwa `RGB`. Nimba iyo sandugu yitwa `RGB` iba yaramaze kubaho, hariho ugutombora, ni co gituma iryo zina)


Iryo shirwaho rikoranya igitigiri kinini w'ibintu bifise ico biyoboka (nk'ugusesangura amabwirizwa, gushiramwo Electrum, gucunga ibimenyamenya bitagira ubumenyi, n'ibindi).


Igihe gushiramwo birangiye,:


```bash
rgb
```


Gukoresha `RGB` (ata mpamvu) yerekana urutonde rw'amabwirizwa mato ariho, nka `imirongo`, `Igicapo`, `kwinjiza`, `gusohora`, `ikibazo`, `Fagitire`, `kwimurira ububiko`, n'ibindi. ibitabo, ibishushanyo n'ibishirwa mu ngiro), uhitemwo urubuga (Testnet, Mainnet) canke utunganye umukozi wawe wa Electrum.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/081.webp)


#### Incamake ya mbere y'ibigenzura


Iyo ukoresheje itegeko rikurikira, uzobona ko `RGB20` Ahakorerwa ibintu hasanzwe hinjijwe:


```bash
rgb interfaces
```


Niba aha hakorerwa ibintu hadashizwemwo, idashizwemwo, kora clone ya:


```bash
git clone https://github.com/RGB-WG/rgb-interfaces
```


Bishire hamwe:


```bash
cargo run
```


Hanyuma ushiremwo ahakorerwa ibintu wishakiye:


```bash
rgb import interfaces/RGB20.rgb
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/082.webp)


Ku rundi ruhande, tubwirwa ko atagicapo kirasirwa muri iyo porogarama. Eka mbere ntana masezerano ari mu Stash. Kugira ngo uyibone, koresha itegeko:


```bash
rgb schemata
```


Ushobora rero gukora clone y'ububiko kugira ngo ubone ibishushanyo bimwe bimwe:


```bash
git clone https://github.com/RGB-WG/rgb-schemata
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/083.webp)


Ubu bubiko burimwo, mu bubiko bwayo bwa `src/`, amadosiye menshi ya Rust (nk'akarorero `nia.rs`) asobanura imirongo (NIA ku "*Itunga Ridashobora Gufutwa*", UDA ku "*Itunga ry'Igihugu*", n'ibindi). Kugira ngo ukoreshe, ushobora gukoresha:


```bash
cd rgb-schemata
cargo run
```


Ivyo bituma habaho amadosiye menshi `.RGB` na `.rgba` ahuye n'imirongo yashizwe hamwe. Nk'akarorero, uzosanga `Itunga ridashobora gutera.RGB`.


#### Kuzana ibicuruzwa vy'igicapo n'ahakorerwa ibintu


Ubu ushobora kwinjiza igishushanyo muri `RGB`:


```bash
rgb import schemata/NonInflatableAssets.rgb
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/084.webp)


Ivyo bica biyongera kuri Stash yo mu karere. Nitwakoresha itegeko rikurikira, turabona ko Igicapo ubu kibonetse:


```bash
rgb schemata
```


### Gukora amasezerano (kuyatanga)


Hari uburyo bubiri bwo gukora umutungo mushasha:




- Canke dukoreshe inyandiko canke kode muri Rust yubaka Amasezerano mu gushiramwo ivyicaro vy'Ibicapo (Uko bimeze muri rusangi, Ibifashwe muminwe, n'ibindi) maze igatanga dosiye `.RGB` canke `.rgba`;
- Canke ukoreshe itegeko rito `issue` ataco rihinduye, n'idosiye ya YAML (canke TOML) idondora imiterere ya token.


Ushobora gusanga uburorero muri Rust muri dosiye `ingero`, zigaragaza ingene wubaka `Uwukora Amasezerano`, wuzuze `Uko bimeze murirusangi` (izina ry'umutungo, ikimenyetso, ugutanga, itariki, n'ibindi), usobanure Ibifiswe muminwe (ivyo bifiswe muminwe ari comp it muri vyose-1). *Amasezerano yogushinga uwundi* ushobora kurungika hanze, kwemeza no kwinjiza mu Stash.


Ubundi buryo ni uguhindura n'amaboko dosiye ya YAML kugira ngo uhindure `amakode`, `izina`, `Ako biva`, n'ibindi. Twibaze ko dosiye yitwa `RGB20-demo.yaml`. Ushobora gusobanura:




- `spec`: amakode, izina, gutumbereza;
- `amajambo`: ikibanza c'amatangazo y'amategeko;
- `Ivyasohowe`: igitigiri c'ama token yasohowe;
- `ibikorwa`: vyerekana Serire ikoreshwa rimwe (*Insiguro ya Serire*) n'ingero zifunguwe.


Aha ni akarorero ka dosiye ya YAML yo gukora:


```yaml
interface: RGB20Fixed

globals:
spec:
ticker: Plan ₿ Academy
name: Plan ₿ Academy
details: "Pay attention: the asset has no value"
precision: 2
terms:
text: >
SUBJECT TO, AND WITHOUT IN ANY WAY LIMITING, THE REPRESENTATIONS AND WARRANTIES OF ANY SELLER. PROPERTY IS BEING SOLD “AS IS”...
media: ~
issuedSupply: 100000000

assignments:
assetOwner:
seal: tapret1st:b449f7eaa3f98c145b27ad0eeb7b5679ceb567faef7a52479bc995792b65f804:1
amount: 100000000 # this is 1 million (we have two digits for cents)
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/085.webp)


Hanyuma ukoreshe itegeko:


```bash
rgb issue '<SchemaID>' ssi:<Issuer> rgb20-demo.yaml
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/086.webp)


Ku bijanye nanje, ikimenyetso kidasanzwe c'igicapo (kizoshirwa mu bimenyetso bimwe bimwe) ni `RDYhMTR! Rero itegeko ryanje ni:


```txt
rgb issue 'RDYhMTR!9gv8Y2GLv9UNBEK1hcrCmdLDFk9Qd5fnO8k' ssi:anonymous rgb20-demo.yaml
```


Niba utazi ikiranga Igicapo, koresha itegeko:


```bash
rgb schemata
```


CLI yishura ko hariho Amasezerano mashasha yasohowe kandi yongerwa ku Stash. Nitwandika iri tegeko rikurikira, turabona ko ubu hariho Amasezerano y’inyongera, ihuye n’iyiherutse gusohoka:


```bash
rgb contracts
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/087.webp)


Hanyuma, itegeko rikurikira ryerekana ibihugu vyo kw’isi yose (izina, ikimenyetso, Ahatangirwa ikintu...) n’urutonde rw’ibihugu vy’ubutunzi, ni ukuvuga ivy’ugutanga (nk’akarorero, ibimenyetso vy’imiliyoni 1 `Plan ₿ Academy` vyasobanuwe muri UTXO `b449f7eaa3f98c145b27ad0eeb7b5679ceb567faef7a52479bc995792b65f804:1`).


```bash
rgb state '<ContractId>'
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/088.webp)


### Gusohora hanze, kwinjiza mu gihugu no kwemeza


Kugira ngo usangire Ayomasezerano n'abandi bakoresha, ushobora kuyirungika hanze kuva kuri Stash ikaja kuri:


```bash
rgb export '<ContractId>' myContractPBN.rgb
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/089.webp)


Dosiye `myContractPBN.RGB` ishobora gushikirizwa uwundi mukozi, ashobora kuyishira kuri Stash yiwe n'itegeko:


```bash
rgb import myContractPBN.rgb
```


Ku bijanye no kwinjiza, nimba ari *Amasezerano yogushinga uwundi* yoroshe, tuzoronka ubutumwa "`Kuzana Gushinga uwundi RGB`". Niba ari * Uko gushinga uwundi bihinduka* nini, itegeko rizoba ritandukanye (`RGB yemera`).


Kugira ngo umenye neza ko ari ukuri, ushobora kandi gukoresha igikorwa co kwemeza co mu karere. Nk'akarorero, woshobora kwiruka:


```bash
rgb validate myContract.rgb
```


#### Stash ikoreshwa, kugenzura no kugaragaza


Nk’ukwibutsa, Stash ni urutonde rw’ibintu vyo mu karere vy’imirongo, imirongo, ishyirwa mu ngiro n’amasezerano (Itanguriro + imihindukire). Igihe cose ukoresheje "ukuzana", wongerako ikintu kuri Stash. Iyi Stash ishobora kurabwa mu buryo burambuye n’itegeko:


```bash
rgb dump
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/090.webp)


Ivyo bizotuma hashirwaho igira dosiye irimwo amakuru yose ya Stash.


### Kwimurira na PSBT


Kugira ngo ukore ukwimurira, uzokenera gukoresha Ingodo ya Bitcoin yo mu karere kugira ngo ucungere amasezerano ya `Tapret` canke `Opret`.


#### 2013 na 2014


Akenshi, ugukorana hagati y’abaje mu nama y’ubuhinga bwa none (nk’akarorero, Alice na Bob) bibera biciye mu guhingura Ifagitirre. Iyo Alice ashaka ko Bob akora ikintu (kwimurira token, gusubira gusohora, igikorwa muri DAO, n'ibindi), Alice akora fagitire idondora amabwirizwa yiwe kuri Bob. Rero dufise:




- **Igitabu-2021** (uwatanze igitabu-2020);
- **Bob** (ni we yakira kandi agashitsa Fagitire).


Mu buryo butandukanye n’ibindi bidukikije, Fagitire ya RGB ntigarukira ku ciyumviro co kwishura gusa. Ishobora gushiramwo igisabwa cose gifitaniye isano n'amasezerano : gukuraho urufunguzo, gutora, gukora igicapo (*igicapo*) kuri NFT, n'ibindi. Ivyo bishobora gusobanurwa muri kuruhande hakorerwa amasezerano.


Itegeko rikurikira ritanga fagitire ya RGB:


```bash
$ rgb invoice $CONTRACT -i $INTERFACE $ACTION $STATE $SEAL
```


Hamwe:




- `$Contract`: Ikimenyetso c'amasezerano (*Ikiranga amasezerano*);
- `$Interface`: Aj=hakorerwaibintu hashaka gukoreshwa (nk'akarorero `RGB20`);
- `$ACTION`: izina ry'igikorwa kigaragazwa ahakorerwa ibintu (ku bijanye n'uguhindura token, ivyo bishobora kuba "Ukwimurira"). Niba Ahakorerwa ibintu hasanzwe hatanga igikorwa, ntukeneye kugisubiramwo hano;
- `$STATE`: amakuru y'imimerere azokwimurirwa (nk'akarorero, igitigiri c'ibimenyetso iyo token ishobora guhinduka irungitswe);
- `$Seal`: Serireikoreshwa e=rimwe y'uwuronka inyungu (Alice), ni ukuvuga ivyerekeye UTXO. Bob azokoresha aya makuru kugira ngo yubake ihanahanwa ry'icabona, kandi inyishu ihuye izoba iya Alice (mu *blinded UTXO* canke mu buryo butagiramwo amakuru).


Nk’akarorero, n’amabwirizwa akurikira .


```bash
alice$ CONTRACT='iZgIN9EL-2H21UgQ-x!A3uJc-WwXhCSm-$9Lwcc1-v!mUkKY'
alice$ MY_UTXO=4960acc21c175c551af84114541eace09c14d3a1bb184809f7b80916f57f9ef8:1
alice$ rgb invoice $CONTRACT -i RGB20 --amount 100 $MY_UTXO
```


Igikoresho ca CLI kizoba igikoresho ca gutanga ama fagitire nk'iki:


```bash
rgb:iZgIN9EL-2H21UgQ-x!A3uJc-WwXhCSm-$9Lwcc1-v!mUkKY/RGB20/100+utxob:zlVS28Rb-...
```


Ishobora gushikirizwa Bob biciye ku nzira iyo ariyo yose (inyandiko, kode ya QR, n’ibindi).


#### Kwimurira


Kugira ngo ushiremwo iyi fagitire:




- Bob (afise amatokeni mu stash yiwe) afise wallet ya Bitcoin. Ategerejwe gutegura transaction ya Bitcoin (mu buryo bwa PSBT, nk’akarorero `tx.psbt`) ikoresha UTXO zirimo amatokeni ya RGB akenewe, hakiyongerako UTXO imwe y’ivunjisha (change);
- Bob ikora itegeko rikurikira:


```bash
bob$ rgb transfer tx.psbt $INVOICE consignment.rgb
```




- Ibi bitanga dosiye `Consignment.RGB` irimwo:
 - Amateka y’ihinduka yerekana Alice ko ivyo bimenyetso ari ivy’ukuri;
 - Ihinduka rishasha ryimurira ibimenyetso kuri Serire ikoreshwa rimwe rya Alice;
 - Igitabo c'icabona c'amasezerano (kitashizweko umukono).
- Bob yohereza iyi dosiye `Ukubishingisha umuntu.RGB` kuri Alice (biciye kuri e-mail, kuri server yo gusangira canke kuri porotokole ya RGB-RPC, Igihuhusi, n'ibindi);
- Alice yakira `Ukubishingisha umuntu.RGB` kandi ikayemera muri Stash yayo bwite:


```bash
alice$ rgb yemera gushingisha umuntu.rgb
```




- CLI isuzuma ukuri kw'ihinduka maze ikayongera kuri Stash ya Alice. Iyo ataco bimaze, itegeko rirananirwa n'ubutumwa bw'ikosa burambuye. Ahandi ho, biraroranirwa, kandi bikavuga ko iyo nzira y’ugucuruza y’akarorero itaratangazwa ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin (Bob ararindiriye uguhabwa uruhusha kwa Alice);
- Mu buryo bwo kwemeza, itegeko `kwemera` rigarura umukono (*payslip*) Alice ashobora kohereza Bob kugira ngo amwereke ko yemeje *Ugshingisha umuntu*;
- Bob ashobora rero gutera umukono no gutangaza (`--tangaza`) ibikorwa vyiwe vya Bitcoin:


```bash
bob$ rgb check <sig> && wallet sign --publish tx.psbt
```




- Igihe iyo nzira yemejwe On-Chain, Ukwitirirwa umutungo gufatwa nk'ukurungika kwa Alice. Ingodo ya Alice, igenzura ihanahanwa ry'ugucukura, ibona Ibifashwe muminwe bishasha iboneka kuri Stash yayo.


Mu kigabane gikwirikira, tuzokwihweza neza ingene RGB yoshirwa muri Lightning Network.


## RGB kuri Lightning Network


<chapterId>0962980a-8f94-5d0f-9cd0-43d7f884a01d</chapterId>


:::id ya videwo=be25a165-6e23-488c-91d8-3dcfccc6eca1:::


Muri kino kigabane, ndasaba gusuzuma ingene RGB ishobora gukoreshwa muri Lightning Network, mu gushiramwo no kwimurira ivy’ubutunzi bwa RGB (ibimenyetso, NFT, n’ibindi) biciye mu nzira zo kwishura za off-chain.


Iciyumviro nyamukuru ni uko RGB Ihinduka rigenda (*Uko ihinduka rigenda*) ishobora kwiyemeza gukora ihanahanwa rya Bitcoin, naryonyene, rigashibora kuguma ari off-chain gushika umug=hira wa Lightning wugaye. Rero, igihe cose umurongo uvuguruwe, uko RGB ihinduka  nshasha irashobora kwinjizwa mu gikorwa gishasha co gukora, ivyo bikaba bica bihindura ubusa iyo mpinduka ya kera. Muri ubwo buryo, imirongo ya Lightning irashobora gukoreshwa mu gutanga itunga rya RGB, kandi ishobora gukoreshwa mu buryo bumwe n’ubw’amahera asanzwe ya Lightning.


### Ugukora umuhora n'ukwemeza


Kugira ngo dukore umuhora wa Lightning utwara umutungo wa RGB, turakeneye Ibintu bibiri:




- Infashanyo ya Bitcoin yogukora umhora wa 2/2 Multisig y’umurongo (UTXO y’ishimikiro y’umurongo);
- Infashanyo ya RGB, Irungika itunga kuri Multisig nyene.


Mu majambo ya Bitcoin, igikorwa co gutanga amahera kigomba kubaho kugira ngo gisigure igipimo ca UTXO, naho coba kirimwo gusa igitigiri gitoyi ca Sats (ni ikibazo gusa c’umusaruro wose mu bikorwa vy'ukwiyemeza vyo muri kazoza bisigaye hejuru y’umupaka wa Dust wose same). Nk’akarorero, Alice ashobora gufata ingingo yo gutanga ama Sats 10k n'ama USDT 500 (itangazwa nk’umutungo wa RGB). Ku bijanye n'ugutanga amahera, twongerako Ukwiyemeza (`Opret` canke `Tapret`) ishingira intahe uko RGB ihinduka.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/091.webp)


Igihe igikorwa co gutanga amahera kimaze gutegurwa (ariko kitaratangazwa), igikorwa c'ukwiyemeza kirakorwa kugira ngo umwe wese mu bagize uruhande ashobore gufunga umuhora ku ruhande rumwe igihe cose. Ivyo bikorwa bisa n'ivyo Ukwiyemeza vya kera vya Lightning, kiretse ko twongerako ikindi gisohoka kirimwo RGB Anchor (OP_RETURN canke Taproot) gihuye n'uko bimeze uguhinduka.


RGB Uguhinduka rero bijanye n'umutungo kuva kuri 2/2 Multisig y'infashanyo ikaja ku biva mukwiyemezakw'ihanahanwa. Ivyiza vy’iyi nzira ni uko umutekano w’ukobimeze ca RGB uhuye neza n’ubuhinga bwo guhana bwa Lightning: iyo Bob atangaje ukobimeze c’umurongo wa kera, Alice arashobora kumuhana no gukoresha igisohoka, kugira ngo asuire ku Sats n’ivyo vyose. Ico kintu gitera intege rero kirakomeye kuruta mbere n’ico mu muhora wa Lightning udafise itunga rya RGB, kuko umusuma ashobora gutakaza atari Sats gusa, ariko kandi n’itunga rya RGB ry’uwo muhora.


Ihanahanwa ry'ukwiyemeza yashizweko umukono na Alice ikarungikwa kwa Bob rero yoba imeze gutya:


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/092.webp)


Kandi Ihanahanwa ry'ukwiyemeza , yashizweko umukono na Bob ikarungikwa kwa Alice, izomera uku gukwirikira:


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/093.webp)


### Ibishasha vy'umuhora


Iyo habayeho ukwishyura hagati y’abafatanyabikorwa bokumuhora babiri (canke bipfuza guhindura ugutanga umutungo), barema umugwi mushasha w’ibikorwa vy'ukwiyemeza. Amafaranga ari muri Sats ku giciro cose ashobora canke ntahinduke, bivanye n’ugushirwa mu ngiro, kuko uruhara rwayo nyamukuru ari ugutuma habaho kwubaka UTXO zifise akamaro. Ku rundi ruhande, igisohoka ca OP_RETURN (canke Taproot) kigomba guhindurwa kugira ngo kibemwo ugushinga imizi kwa RGB gushasha, igereranya ugusangira gushasha kw’itunga mumuhora.


Nk’akarorero, iyo Alice arungitse amadolari 30 kwa Bob mumuhora, Ukobihinduka gushasha hazokwerekana amadolari 400 ku Alice n’amadolari 100 ku Bob. Igikorwa kijanye n'ugusezerana congerwa kuri (canke gihindurwa na) OP_RETURN/Taproot Anchor kugira ngo kigiremwo iyo mpinduka. Mufate yuko, uhereye ku mbonerahamwe ya RGB, ivyo winjiza mu guhindura biguma ari Multisig ya mbere (aho itunga rya On-Chain rihabwa mu vy’ukuri gushika umuhora wi=ugaye). Ivyo RGB isohora (ivy’ugutanga) vyonyene ni vyo bihinduka, bivanye n’ugusubira gusangira vyafashwe ingingo.


Igitabo c'ukwiyemeza kw'uguhanahana cashizweko umukono na Alice, giteguwe gukwiragizwa na Bob:


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/094.webp)


Igitabo c'uguhanahana c'ukwiyemeza cashizweko umukono na Bob, giteguwe gukwiragizwa na Alice:


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/095.webp)


### Ubuyobozi bwa HTLC


Mu vy’ukuri, Lightning Network iratuma amahera yishurwa ashobora guca mu nzira nyinshi, hakoreshejwe HTLCs (*Amasezerano Apfungiwe n’Igihe*). Ni ko biri no kuri RGB: ku kwishura kwose guca mu muhora, umusaruro wa HTLC wongerwa ku gucuruza, n'ugutanga RGB guhuye n'iyi HTLC. Gutyo, uwuzokoresha umusaruro wa HTLC (bivuye ku banga canke inyuma y’aho igihe co gufunga kirangiriye) arasubirana Sats n’itunga ry’i RGB rijana na ryo. Ku rundi ruhande, biragaragara ko ukeneye kugira amahera ahagije ku nzira mu bijanye n’itunga ryompi Sats na RGB.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/096.webp)


Ivyo RGB ikora kuri Lightning rero bitegerezwa gufatwa nk’uko bihuye n’ivyo Lightning Network ubwayo ikora. Niba wifuza kwihweza cane muri iki cigwa, ndagusavye cane ko uraba iyindi nyigisho yuzuye:


https://planb.academy/courses/34bd43ef-6683-4a5c-b239-7cb1e40a4aeb

### Ikirangamerekero ca kode ya RGB


Ubwa nyuma, imbere yo kuja mu gice gikurikira, ndashaka kubaha icegeranyo c'itegeko rikoreshwa muri RGB. Iryo tegeko rishingiye ku masomero ya Rust n’insiguro y’inkomoko yuguruye. Aha niho hari insiguro y'ububiko nyamukuru n'amasandugu:


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/097.webp)


#### Ukwemeza kuruande rw'umukiriya




- **Ububiko**: [kwemeza_uruhande rw'umukiriya](https://github.com/LNP-BP/kwemeza_uruhande_rw'umukiriya)
- **Amasandugu**: [kwemeza_uruhande_rw'umukiriya](https://amasandugu.io/amasandugu/kwemeza_uruhande rw'umukiriya), [ibimenyetso_bikoreshwa_rimwe](https://amasandugu.io/amasandugu/ibimenyetso_bikoreshwa_rimwe)


Uburongozi bw’ukwemeza off-chain n’ubuhinga bwo gukoresha rimwe Seals.


#### Deterministic Bitcoin Commitments (DBC)




- **Ububiko**: [Ishingiro rya bp](Ishingiro ry'Igihugu)
- **Isandugu**: [bp-dbc](https://isanduku.io/isanduku/bp-dbc)


Uburongozi bw’ugushinga intahe mu bikorwa vya Bitcoin (Tapret, OP_RETURN, n’ibindi).


#### Multi Protocol Commitment (MPC)




- **Ububiko**: [kwemeza_uruhande rw'umukiriya](https://github.com/LNP-BP/kwemeza_uruhande_rw'umukiriya)
- **Isandugu**: [gusuzuma_gukora](https://ibisandugu.io/ibisanduka/ugusuzuma_gukora)


Ivyiyumviro vyinshi vy’ugukorana n’ugushiramwo n’amategeko atandukanye.


#### Ubwoko bukomeye n'ugushiramwo amakuru




- **Insiguro**: [urubuga ubwoko-bukomeye.org](https://www.ubwoko-bukomeye.org/)
- **Ububiko**: [ubwoko-bukomeye](https://github.com/ubwoko-bukomeye/ubwoko-bukomeye), [gushiramwo-bukomeye](https://github.com/ubwoko-bukomeye/gushiramwo-bukomeye)
- **Amasandugu**: [ubwoko_bukomeye](https://amasandugu.io/amasandugu/ubwoko_bukomeye), [gushiramwo_amakode](https://amasandugu.io/amasandugu/gushiramwo_amakode)


Uburyo bwo kwandika bukomeye n'urutonde rw'ibintu bikoreshwa kuruhande rw'ukwemeza rw'umukiriya.


#### RGB Ishingiro




- **Ububiko**: [RGB-ishingiro](RGB-Ishingiro)
- **Isanduku**: [RGB-umutima](https://isanduku.io/isanduku/RGB-umutima)


Ishingiro ry’iyo porotokole, rigizwe n’intumbero nyamukuru y’ukwemeza RGB.


#### RGB Ububiko bw'ibitabu busanzwe & Wallet




- **Ububiko**: [Ububiko-2178-ububiko](Ububiko).
- **Isandugu**: [RGB-std](igisandugu.io/isanduku/RGB-igisandugu)


Ivyiyumviro vy’ugushirwa mu ngiro, uburongozi bwa Stash na Wallet.


#### RGB CLI




- **Ububiko**: [Ububiko-2184](Ububiko).
- **Amasandugu**: [RGB-CLI](Isanduku.io/Isandugu/RGB-CLI), [Isandugu-2187-2185]


Ivyo bikoresho bikoreshwa mu gukoresha amasezerano.


#### RGB Schema




- **Ububiko**: [Imirongo ya RGB](Imirongo ya RGB/Imirongo ya RGB/)


Irimwo ingero z’imirongo (NIA, UDA, n’ibindi) n’ingene zishirwa mu ngiro.


#### AluVM




- **Amakuru**: [AluVM.org](urubuga rwacu-2195.org/)
- **Ububiko**: [Ibisobanuro vya AluVM](Ibisobanuro vya AluVM), [Ivyiyumviro](Ivyiyumviro)
- **Amasandugu**: [AluVM](amasandugu.io/amasandugu/AluVM), [amasandugu](amasandugu.io/amasandugu/amasandugu)


Igikoresho gishingiye ku kwandika gikoreshwa mu gukoresha inyandiko zo kwemeza.


#### Urukwirikirane rwa Bitcoin - BP




- **Ububiko**: [bp-core](bp-core), [bp-std](bp-std), [bp-gW-2199](bp-gw-2199)


Ivyongeyeko vyo gushigikira urukwirikirane rwa Bitcoin (ibikorwa, ivy’uguca mu nzira, n’ibindi).


#### Ubiquitous Deterministic Computing  - UBIDECO




- **Ububiko**: [UBIDECO](UBIDECO)


Ibidukikije bifitaniye isano n’iterambere ry’ivy’ubuhinga ry’inkomoko yuguruye.


# Kwubakira kuri RGB


<partId>3b4b0d66-0c1b-505a-b5ca-4b2e57dd73c2</partId>


## DIBA n'umugambi wa Bitmask


<chapterId>dc92a5e8-ed93-5a3f-bcd0-d433932842f4</chapterId>


:::id ya videwo=2ec9a181-a8b0-4da2-b7b5-9dfaaeb10ba:::


kano gace kanyuma k’amashure gishingiye ku nsiguro zashikirijwe n’abatanga insiguro batandukanye mu nama y’ivyigwa ya RGB. Harimwo intahe n’ivyiyumviro ku RGB n’ibidukikije vyayo, hamwe n’ugushikiriza ibikoresho n’imigambi ishingiye kuri urwo rukwirikirane. Iki gice ca mbere kirongowe na Hunter Beast, ibindi bibiri bikurikira na Frederico Tenga.


### Kuva ku nyandiko ya Java gushika kuri Rust, no mubiri muri Bitcoin


Mu ntango, Hunter Beast yakora cane cane mu rurimi rw’igifaransa. Hanyuma abona **Rust**, insiguro y’amajambo yayo yasa n’iyidashimishije kandi ibabaza mu ntango. Ariko rero, yaraje gutahura ububasha bw’ururimi, ukugenzura ubwonko (*heap* na *stack*), n’umutekano n’ubushobozi bijana na vyo. Ashimika ku vy’uko Rust ari ikibanza ciza cane co kwimenyerezamwo kugira ngo umuntu atahure bimwe bigera kure ingene orodinateri ikora.


Hunter Beast avuga ivy’amateka yiwe mu migambi itandukanye mubiri muma *Altcoin*, nka Ethereum (ifise ubukomezi, TypeScript, n’ibindi), hanyuma Filecoin. Asigura ko mu ntango yatangajwe n’amasezerano amwe amwe, ariko amaherezo yumva ko menshi muri yo yamuhemukiye, atari kubera ubuhinga bwayo bwo gukoresha ibimenyetso. Aragaya inkurikizi z’amahera ziteye amakenga, uguhingura ibimenyetso vy’ugutera imbere bitera ubwoba abashoramari, n’umuce ushobora gutuma iyo migambi ikoreshwa nabi. Yaciye rero aheza afata ingingo y' **Ukuba uwemera Bitcoin gusa**, atari ukubera ko hari abantu bamwebamwe bamufunguriye amaso ku buryo bwiza bw’ubutunzi bwa Bitcoin, no ku gukomera kw’iyi nzira.


### Ugusaba kwa RGB no kwubaka ku bipande
