Ico camujijuye ata gukeka ko Bitcoin ifise akamaro, mu majambo yiwe, ni ukuvumbura RGB be n’iciyumviro c’ibice. Yemera ko ibikorwa biriho ku bindi bice vy’umubiri bishobora gusubirwamwo ku bice vy’imbere, hejuru ya Bitcoin, ata guhindura umurongo w’ishimikiro.


Muri Ruhuhuma 2022, yinjiye muri **DIBA** kugira ngo akore cane cane kuri RGB, na cane cane kungodo yitwa **Bitmask**. Iciyo gihe, Bitmask yari ikiri kuri verisiyo 0.01 kandi yariko ikoresha RGB kuri verisiyo 0.4, gusa ku bijanye no gucunga ibimenyetso bimwe bimwe. Avuga ko ivyo vyari bishingiye cane ku kwizigama nk’uko biri muri iki gihe, kuko ivyiyumviro vyari bishingiye ku serveri(Ahabikwa ibintu). Kuva ico gihe, ubwubatsi bwarateye imbere buja kuri iyo nzira, ishimwa cane n’abakoresha Bitcoin.


### Inshimikiro ry'amasezerano ya RGB


Itegeko rya **RGB** ni ryo rishasha kandi riteye imbere cane ry'iciyumviro c'ibiceri vy'amabara, ryaramaze gusuzumwa nko mu 2012-2013. Iciyo gihe, amashirahamwe menshi yariko ararondera gufatanya agaciro gatandukanye ka Bitcoin ku UTXO, ivyo vyatumye habaho ugushirwa mu ngiro kwinshi gutandukanijwe. Ukwo kutagira urugero n’ugusaba guke ico gihe vyatumye ivyo bisubizo bitaronka ikibanza kiramvye.


Ubu, RGB irahagaze kubera ubukomezi bwayo bw’ivyiyumviro n’insiguro vy’ubumwe biciye ku shirahamwe rya LNP/BP. Iryo hame rishingiye kukwemeza kuruhande rw'umu kiriya. Blockchain ya Bitcoin ibika gusa amasezerano y’ubuhinga bwa none (_amasezerano_, biciye kuri Taproot canke OP_RETURN), mu gihe amakuru menshi (Insiguro y'amasezerano, kahise yo kwimurira, n’ibindi) abikwa n’abakoresha biraba. Muri ubwo buryo, umuzigo wo kubika uragabanywa kandi ibanga ry’uguhanahana rirakomezwa, ata kuremerera Blockchain. Ubu buryo burashoboza kurema ibintu bishobora guhinduka (**RGB20** standard) canke ibintu bidasanzwe (**RGB21**), mu rwego rw’ibice kandi bishobora guhindurwa.


### Ibikorwa vya token (RGB20) n'ibintu bidasanzwe (RGB21)


Na **RGB20**, dusobanura token ishobora guhinduka kuri Bitcoin. Uwutanga amafaranga ahitamwo _ugutanga_, _ugutanga_, agaca akora _amasezerano_ ashobora guca akoramwo amafaranga. Igihe cose umuntu yimuriwe, akoresheje Bitcoin UTXO, ikora nk’igitabu ca *Serire ikoreshwa rimwe*. Ivyo bituma uwukoresha atazoshobora gukoresha umutungo umwe incuro zibiri, kuko umuntu wenyene ashobora gukoresha UTXO ari we afise urufunguzo rwo guhindura uko Amasezerano ameze ku ruhande rw'umukiriya.


**RGB21** igamije ivy'ubutunzi bidasanzwe (canke "NFT"). Ico kintu gifise Ugushiraho ya 1, kandi gishobora gufatanywa n’amakuru (dosiye y’amashusho, amajwi, n’ibindi) adondora biciye mu kibanza kinaka. Udakunze NFTs ku blockchains za bose, amakuru n’ibimenyetso vyayo vya MIME birashobora kuguma ari ivy’ibanga, bigakwiragizwa n’abandi ku bushake bwa nyen’ivyo bikoresho.


### Umuti w'ibipfukisho: Ingodo  ya RGB


Kugira ngo ubushobozi bwa RGB bukoreshwe mu bikorwa, umugambi wa **DIBA** warateguye Ingodo yitwa [Bitmask](https://bitmask.app/). Iciyumviro ni ugutanga igikoresho kitagira ububiko, gishingiye kuri Taproot, gishobora kuboneka kurubuga ngurukana bumenyi canke nk’igikoresho co kwagura murandasi. Bitmask icungera ivy'ubutunzi vya RGB20 na RGB21, kandi igashiramwo uburyo butandukanye bwo gucungera umutekano:




- Itegeko ry’ishimikiro ryanditswe muri Rust, hanyuma rikakoranywa muri ahahurira za Murandasi kugira ngo rikore mu bidukikije vya JavaScript (React);
- Imfunguruzo zikorerwa indani, hanyuma hakanyegezwa inyandikomukarere;
- Amakuru y'uko bimeze (Stash) abikwa mububiko bwa murandasi, akurikiranwa kandi ashirwa mu mfuruka biciye mu bubiko bw'ibitabu bwa **Carbonado**, bukora igikorwa co gufatanya, gukosora amakosa, inyandiko zinyegejwe, hama zikarabwa zigasuzumirwa kuri  Blake3.


Kubera iyo nyubakwa, ihanahanwary'imitungo ryose ribera kuruhande rw'umukiriya. Uvuye hanze, ihanahanwa rya Bitcoin nta kindi ariko n'ihanahanwa rya kera ryogukoresha gukoresha amahera ya Taproot, ata n’umwe yokwikeka ko naryo nyene rifise uguhindura ibimenyetso canke NFTs. Kuba ata On-Chain irengeje urugero (ntabushinguzi bw'amakuru bubikwa ku mugaragaro) biremeza urugero runaka rw’ubukerebutsi kandi bituma vyoroha kunanira ukugerageza gucengera gushoboka.


### Umutekano n'ubwubatsi busabikanijwe


Kubera ko urukwirikirane rwa RGB rusaba ko uwuriko arakora wese aguma afise kahise k'ibikorwa vyiwe vyiwe (kugira ngo yerekane ko amafaranga yarungitswe ari ayukuri), ikibazo co kubika kiravyuka. Bitmask isaba gushiramwo iyi Stash Indani, hanyuma ikayirungika kubushinguzi bwinshi canke ku bicu (ntibikenewe). Amakuru aguma apfutse n'uwukoresha biciye kuri **Carbonado**, rero umukozi ntashobora kuyasoma. Iyo habayeho ugusenyuka kw’igice, ugukosora amakosa Layer kurashobora gusubiramwo inyandiko zirimwo.


Ikoreshwa rya CRDT (_Ubwoko bw'amakuru asubiyemwo ata ngorane nimwe_) rituma verisiyo zitandukanye za Stash zishobora guhurizwa hamwe, iyo zishobora gutandukana. Umuntu wese arafise umwidegemvyo wo kwakira ayo makuru aho yipfuza hose, kuko ata node yose afise n’imwe itwara amakuru yose afitaniye isano n’ico kintu. Ivyo vyerekana neza na neza filozofiya ya *y'ukwemeza kuruhande rw'umukiriya*, aho nyen’umutungo wese afise inshingano yo kubika ibimenyamenya vy’ukuri kw’umutungo wiwe wa RGB.


### Ku bijanye n'ibirihafi y'urwo ruganda: akaguriro, ugukorana n'abandi n'ibikorwa bishasha


Ishirahamwe riri inyuma ya Bitmask ntirigarukira kugukora gusa Ingodo. DIBA ifise umugambi wo guteza imbere:




- **Akaguriro** ko guhanahana ama token, cane cane mu buryo bwa **RGB21**;
- Guhuza n’izindi ngodo (nk' *ingodo yitwa Iris*);
- Ubuhinga bwo gushiramwo irungika rikwirikirana rya RGB mw'ihanahana rimwe.


Muri ico gihe nyene, turiko turakora ku **WebBTC** canke **WebLN** (ingingo ngenderwako zishoboza imbuga gusaba Ingodo guterako ikidodo ku masezerano ya Bitcoin canke Lightning), hamwe n'ubushobozi bwo "gukoresha teleburn" ivyinjijwe vya Bitcoin (niba dushaka gusubiza mu gihugu ca Wallet).


### Gusozera


Ivyo vyose vyerekana ingene ubuhinga bwa RGB bushobora gukoreshwa no gushikira abakoresha biciye mu gutorera umuti ibibazo bikomeye. Ihinduka kuva kumbono ya Altcoin gushika kumbono ishingiye kuri Bitcoin, hamwe n’ukuvumbura *Ukwemeza kuruhande rw'umukiriya*, vyerekana inzira yumvikana neza: turatahura ko bishoboka gushirwa mu ngiro ibikorwa bitandukanye (ibimenyetso bishobora guhinduka, NFT, amasezerano y’ubwenge ya GW by-5...) ata2. y'imihigo y'ibanga ku bikorwa vya Taproot canke OP_RETURNs.


**Bitmask** Ingodo ni kimwe muri iyo nzira: ku ruhande rwa Blockchain, ivyo ubona vyose ni ugucuruza kwa Bitcoin gusanzwe; ku ruhande rw'ukoresha, ukoresha urubuga rwahakorerwa ibintu aho urema, Ihanahanwa kandi ukabika ubwoko bwose bw'itunga rya off-chain. Ico kigereranyo gitandukanya neza uko amahera ateye (Bitcoin) n’ubuhinga bwo gutanga no gutanga (RGB), mu gihe kigaragaza urugero rwo hejuru rw’ibanga n’ugushobora gutera imbere neza.


## Ibikorwa vya Bitfinex kuri RGB


<chapterId>d4d80e07-5eac-5b29-a93a-123180e97047</chapterId>


:::id ya videwo=04555813-516f-4eea-9767-7082c2ea6f01:::


Muri iki gice, twisunze ikiganiro ca Frederico Tenga, turaba urutonde rw’ibikoresho n’imigambi yashizweho n’umugwi wa Bitfinex wiyeguriye RGB, n’intumbero yo guteza imbere uguseruka kw’ibidukikije vy’ubutunzi kandi bitandukanye bikikuje iyo porotokole. Intumbero y’intango y’iryo tsinda si ugusohora igicuruzwa c’ubudandaji kanaka, ahubwo ni ugutanga ibice vy’inyubako vya porogarama, gutanga intererano ku masezerano ya RGB ubwayo, no gutanga ibimenyetso vy’ukuri vyo gushirwa mu ngiro nk’igikoresho gikora neza (*ingodo yitwa Iris *) canke igikoresho gishobora gukoreshwa na RGB-com.


### Inyuma n'intumbero


Kuva nko mu mwaka w’2022, ikigo ca Bitfinex RGB caramaze kwibanda ku gutegura urutonde rw’ubuhinga bufasha RGB gukoreshwa no kugeragezwa neza. Hariho intererano nyinshi zatanzwe:




- Ukwifatanya mu gutanga kode y’inkomoko n’insiguro y’amasezerano, harimwo kwandika ivyiyumviro vyo kwongereza ubushobozi, gukosora ibibazo, n’ibindi;
- Ibikoresho vy’abahinguzi kugira ngo borohereze gushiramwo RGB mu bikorwa vyabo;
- Guhingura igikoresho gikora neza citwa [Iris](https://iriswallet.com/) kugira ngo kigerageze kandi kigaragaze uburyo bwiza bwo gukoresha igikoresho citwa RGB;
- Guhingura node ya Lightning isanzwe, ishobora gucungera neza umuhora w'umutungo wa RGB;
- Gushigikira iyindi migwi yubaka inyishu kuri RGB, kugira ngo baremeshe ubudasa hamwe n'umura=yango ukomeye.


Ubu buryo bufise intumbero yo gupfuka uruhererekane rwose rw’ivyo bikenewe: kuva ku bubiko bw’ibitabu bwo ku rugero ruto (*[RGBlib]*), bikaba bishoboza gushirwa mu ngiro Ingodo, Ingodo, G6W node2 n’ibindi).


### Ububiko bw'ibitabu bwa RGBlib: kworohereza iterambere ry'ibikorwa vya RGB


Iciyumviro gihambaye mu gutuma habaho ukwigenga mugukora ingodo ya RGB n’ibikorwa ni ugutuma habaho ukwibanda kubikenewe gusa yoroshe bihagije kugira ngo abahinguzi ntibabwirizwe kwiga vyose ku bijanye n’ubuhinga bwo mu mutima bw’iyo porotokole. Iyi ni yo ntumbero ya **RGBlib**, yanditswe muri Rust.


RGBlib ikora nk’ikiraro hagati y’ibisabwa bishobora guhinduka cane (ariko rimwe na rimwe bikomeye) vya RGB twashoboye kwiga mu bice vya kera, n’ivyo umuhinguzi w’ibikorwa akeneye vy’ukuri. Mu yandi majambo, Ingodo (canke igikorwa) yipfuza gucunga token yoherezwa, gutanga umutungo, kugenzura, n’ibindi, irashobora kwizigira RGBlib itazi ido n’ido ryose ry’ibanga canke ubuhinga bwose bwa RGB bushobora guhindurwa.


Iduka ry’ibitabu ritanga:




- Ibikorwa vy’ugutanga (_issuance_) ivy’ubutunzi (bishobora guhinduka canke bitahinduka);
- Ubushobozi bwo kurungika (kohereza/kwakira) itunga hakoreshejwe ibintu vyoroshe (amaderesi, amafaranga, UTXOs, n’ibindi);
- Uburyo bwo kubika no gushiramwo amakuru y'uko bimeze (*ibirungikwa*) bisabwa kuri Ukwemezwa kuruhande rw'umuguzi.


RGBlib rero yizigira ivyiyumviro bikomeye vyihariye kuri RGB (Ukweza kuruhande rw'umukiriya, guhinga imizi kwa Tapret/Opret), ariko ikabishiramwo kugira ngo igikorwa ca nyuma ntikibwirizwe gusubira gutegura vyose canke gufata ingingo zishobora gutera ingorane. Ikindi, RGBlib irasanzwe iboshe mu ndimi nyinshi (Kotlin na Python), ukwi=ugurura imiryango kw’ikoreshwa rirenze isi yoroshe ya Rust.


### Ingodo yitwa Iris: akarorero k'ingodo ya RGB kuri Android


Kugira ngo RGBlib yerekane ko ikora neza, ikigo ca Bitfinex carateguye **Ingodo yitwa Iris**, kikaba ari kuri Android gusa muri iki gihe. Ni Wallet igendagenda yerekana ubumenyi bw’ukoresha busa n’ubw’ingodo ya  Bitcoin isanzwe: urashobora gutanga umutungo, ukawurungika, ukawakira, no kuraba amateka yawo, mu gihe uguma ku citegererezo co kwizigama.


Iris ifise ibintu bitari bike bishimishije:


**Gukoresha ubushinguzi bwa Electrum:**


Cokimwe n'Ingodo iyo ari yo yose, Iris arakeneye kumenya ivyerekeye ivyemezo vy'amafaranga kuri Blockchain. Aho gushiramwo node ikwiye, Iris ikoresha ubushinguzi bwa Electrum abungabungwa n’umugwi wa Bitfinex. Ariko rero, abakoresha barashobora gutunganya uushingzi bwabo canke bukoresheje ubw'uwundi muntu. Muri ubwo buryo, amafaranga y’ibikorwa vya Bitcoin arashobora kwemezwa kandi amakuru akaronswa (indexing) mu buryo bw’ibice.


**Umukozi wa RGB:**


Udakunze Bitcoin, RGB isaba Ihanahanwa ry'amakuru  y’ivya off-chain (*ibirungikwa*) hagati y’uwurungika n’uwuyakira. Kugira ngo iyo nzira yorohe, Iris itanga umuti aho uguhanahana amakuru bibera biciye ku murongo w’ivy’ubuhinga. Wallet yakira itanga *Fagitire* ivuga aho uwurungitse akwiye kohereza amakuru *y'uruhande rw'umukiriya*. Ku mburabuzi, URL yerekana proxy yakiriwe n'umugwi wa Bitfinex, ariko ushobora guhindura iyo proxy (canke kwakira iyawe). Iciyumviro ni ugusubira ku bumenyi bumenyerewe bw’abakoresha aho uwuronka iyo kode yerekana kode ya QR, uwuyirungitse na we agaca asuzuma iyo kode kugira ngo abone ivyo akora, ata bindi bikoresho bikomeye vy’inyongera.


**Ukubandanya ugusubiza inyuma:**


Mu gihe c'ivya Bitcoin, gushigikira imbuto yawe muri rusangi birahagije (naho muri iyi misi dusaba gushigikira imbuto n'ibisobanuro aho kubigira). Na RGB, ivyo ntibihagije: ukeneye kandi kuguma ufise kahise k'aho hantu (ivyo *birungikwa*) vyerekana ko vy'ukuri ufise umutungo wa RGB. Igihe cose ubonye ikimenyetso c’uko uronse amahera, ico gikoresho kirabika amakuru mashasha, ivyo bikaba ari ngirakamaro kugira ngo ukoreshe amahera mu nyuma. Iris ihita icungera ububiko bwashizwemwo mu Google Drive y'ukoresha. Ivyo ntibisaba kwizigira Google cane, kuko ububiko bushizwe mu nzira, kandi uburyo bukomeye kuruta (nk’umukozi w’umuntu ku giti ciwe) burateguwe muri kazoza kugira ngo ntihagire ingorane zo gucengera canke gukurwaho n’uwundi muntu.


**Ibindi bimenyetso:**




- Gukora Faucet kugira ngo unyarutse kugerageza canke gutanga ibimenyetso vyo kugerageza canke guteza imbere;
- Uburyo bwo gutanga impamyabumenyi (bufise aho butwarirwa) bwo gutandukanya token yemewe n’iy’ikinyoma yacaouwe ahandi kugicapo kizwi cane. Mu gihe kizoza, ico cete coshobora gukoreshwa cane (biciye kuri DNS canke ubundi buryo).


Muri vyose, Iris itanga ubumenyi bw’abakoresha buri hafi y’ubw’iyo ngodo ya Bitcoin ya kera, igapfuka ibindi bigoranye (uburongozi bwa Stash, *amateka y'ukubishinga umuntu*, n’ibindi) bivuye kuri RGBlib n’ugukoresha umukozi wa proxy.


### Ubushinguzi bwa Proxy hamwe n'uko abakoresha bameze


Ubushinguzi bwa proxy bwashizweho haruguru burakwiye gusobanurwamwo ido n’ido, kuko ari yo nzira y’ugukoresha neza. Aho ko uwurungitse ategerezwa gutanga *ivyoherezwa* ku wubirungika, igikorwa ca RGB kibera inyuma biciye ku:




- Uwuronka iyo mpapuro atanga *Fagitire* (irimwo, mu bindi, igitabu c’uburenganzira Address);
- Uwurungitse arungika (biciye ku busabe bwa HTTP) umugambi wo guhindura (*Ugushingisha umuntu*) ku wuwuserukira;
- Uwuronka uwo mugambi aragarura uwo mugambi, agashitsa *uruhande rw'umukiriya* kwemeza mu karere;
- Uwuronka iyo mpapuro aca atangaza, biciye ku muntu amusubiriza, ko yemeye (canke bishoboka ko yanse) iyo mpapuro Ukobihinduka bimeze;
- Uwurungitse arashobora kubona uko ivyemezo vyemewe kandi, iyo yemewe, agatangaza ivy’ugucuruza Bitcoin biheza ukwimurira.


Muri ubwo buryo, Igodo yitwararika nk’iyindi ngodo isanzwe. Uwukoresha ntazi intambwe zose ziri hagati. Ni ivy’ukuri ko iyo proxy iriho ubu idafise amakuru canke ngo yemezwe (ivyo bikaba bisiga amaganya ku bijanye n’ibanga n’ubunyankamugayo), ariko ivyo bintu vyiza birashoboka mu bindi bihe vya nyuma. Iciyumviro ca proxy kiguma ari ngirakamaro cane mu gusubira kurema ubumenyi bwo "kurungika kode ya QR, uracapura kugira ngo urihe".


### RGB gushiramwo kuri Lightning Network


Ikindi kintu nyamukuru igikorwa c’umugwi wa Bitfinex ni ugutuma Lightning Network ihuye n’itunga rya RGB. Intumbero ni ugutuma imirongo ya Lightning ikoreshwa muri USDT (canke iyindi token iyo ari yo yose), no kwungukira ku nyungu nk’iza Bitcoin kuri Lightning (ugucuruza hafi y’aho nyene, inzira, n’ibindi). Mu majambo nyayo, ivyo birimwo gukora node ya Lightning irahindurwa ngo ibe:




- Gufungura umurongo mu gushiramwo atari satoshis gusa, ariko n’umutungo umwe canke myinshi ya RGB mu nkunga UTXO Multisig;
- Gutanga ihanahanwa ry'ukwiyemeza rya Lightning (kuruhande rwa Bitcoin) biherekejwe n’i ry’intara rihuye RGB. Igihe cose umurongo uvuguruwe, ihinduka rya RGB risubira gusobanura ugusangira umutungo mu bisohoka vya Lightning;
- Gushoboza ugufunga kw’uruhande rumwe, aho umutungo ugarurwa mu UTXO yihariye, hakurikijwe amategeko ya Lightning Network (HTLC, igihe co gufunga, igihano, n’ibindi).


Iyo nyishu, yitwa "**RGB Lightning Node**", ukoresha LDK (*Lightning Dev Kit*) nk'ishimikiro, kandi wongerako uburyo bukenewe bwo gutera ibimenyetso vya RGB mu mihora. Ivyemezo vy’Lightning bigumya biguma uko vyari bimeze kera (ibisohoka bishobora gutoborwa, igihe...), kandi n’ibindi Anchor na RGB uko vyaribimeze bihinduka (biciye muri `Opret` canke `Tapret`). Ku mukoresha, ivyo bifungura inzira y'umuhora wa Lightning  mu bice vy'amahera canke mu kindi kintu cose gisohoka biciye kuri RGB.


### DEX ubushobozi n'ingaruka kuri Bitcoin


Igihe ibintu vyinshi bicungiwe biciye kuri Lightning, birashoboka kwiyumvira **Ihanahanawa** ku nzira imwe y’inzira ya Lighning, hakoreshejwe ubuhinga bumwe bw’amabanga n’igihe. Nk’akarorero, umukoresha A afise Bitcoin ku murongo umwe wa Lightning, uwukoresha B na we afise USDT RGB ku wundi murongo wa Lightning. Bashobora kwubaka inzira ihuza imirongo yabo ibiri kandi icarimwe Ihanahanwa ririhagati ya BTC na USDT, ataco bakeneye kwizigira. Ivyo nta kindi ariko ni **uguhinduranya uduce dutoduto** kuba mu bice vyinshi, bituma abaje hanze hafi bakibagira ko bariko barakora ubudandaji, atari uguhindura inzira gusa. Ubu buryo buratanga:




- Igihe co guhagarara kiri hasi cane, kuko vyose biguma ari off-chain kuri Lightnig.
-  **Ibanga** riteye imbere: nta n’umwe azi ko ari ubudandaji, kandi si inzira isanzwe;
- Kwirinda gutera imbere, ingorane isubira inyuma kuri On-Chain DEX;
- Ibiciro bigabanutse (ntiwishura blockspace, amafaranga y’urugendo rwa Lightning gusa).


Turashobora rero kwiyumvira ibirimwo vyose aho ama nodes ya Lightning atanga ibiciro vy’uguhindura (mu gutanga amafaranga). Buri node, iyo ishaka, irashobora gukora uruhara rwa _umuhinguzi w'isoko_, kugura no kugurisha ibintu bitandukanye kuri Lightning. Ivyo vyizigiro vy’i _layer-2_ DEX bikomeza iciyumviro c’uko bidakenewe Fork canke gukoresha blockchains z’abandi kugira ngo umuntu aronke ubuhinga bwo guhindura itunga ry’abantu bose.


Ingaruka kuri Bitcoin yoshobora kuba nziza: Ibikorwa bikorwa na Lightning (ama node, imirongo n’ibikorwa) vyokoreshwa neza cane kubera ibiharuro biva kuri izo *stablecoins*, ibivako n’ibindi bimenyetso. Abacuruzi bashaka kwishura USDT kuri Lightning boshobora kumenya mu buryo bw’ubuhinga kwishura BTC kuri Lightning (bicungiwe n’ico kirundo nyene). Ugucungera no gutanga amafaranga y’ibikorwa remezo vya Lightning Network na vyo nyene vyoshobora kwungukira ku kugwiza izo nzira zitari za BTC, ivyo bikaba vyoshobora kugirira akamaro mu buryo butaziguye abakoresha Bitcoin.


### Ukurangiza n'ahava ibikoresho


Ishirahamwe rya Bitfinex ryiyemeje RGB ryerekana, biciye mu gikorwa caryo, ubudasa bw’ibishobora gukorwa hejuru y’amasezerano. Ku ruhande rumwe, hariho RGBlib, ububiko bw’ibitabu bworohereza uguhingura Ingodo n’ibikoresho. Ku rundi ruhande, dufise Ingodo ya Iris, iyerekanwa ry'ibikorwa kuri Android ry'umukoresha w'iherezo y'ahakorerwa ibintu. Ubwa nyuma, ugushiramwo RGB muri Lightning vyerekana ko imihora ya stablecoin ishoboka, kandi yugurura inzira y’ubushobozi bwa DEX yegerejwe ku Lightning.


Ubu buryo buraguma ahanini ari ubw’igerageza kandi burabandanya gutera imbere: ububiko bw’ibitabu bwa RGBlib buriko buratunganirizwa uko tugenda, Ingodo yitwa Iris iriko iraronka ivyiza bihoraho, kandi urudodo rwihariye rwa Lightning ntiruraba umukiriya wa Lightning.


Ku bipfuza kumenya vyinshi canke gutanga, hariho uburyo bwinshi bwo kubifasha, harimwo:




- [Ibikoresho vy'ububiko bwa GitHub RGB](Ibikoresho vya RGB);
- [Urubuga rw’amakuru rwerekeye Iris Wallet](https://iriswallet.com/) kugira ngo ugerageze Ingodo kuri Android.


Mu gice gikurikira, tuzokwihweza neza ingene twotanguza node ya Lightning ya RGB.


## RLN - Node ya Lightning ya RGB


<chapterId>ecaabe32-20ba-5f8c-8ca1-a3f095792958</chapterId>


:::id=d1e9753e-6093-4a47-bcdc-da1aebaefffc:::.


Muri iki gice ca nyuma, Frederico Tenga aragutwara intambwe ku yindi mu gushinga node ya Lightning ya RGB ku bidukikije vya Regtest, kandi akakwereka ingene worema ibimenyetso vya RGB kuri rwo. Mu gutanguza ama node abiri atandukanye, uzobona kandi ingene wokwugurura umurongo w’umuco hagati yayo n’itunga ry'uguhanahana rya RGB.


Iyi video ikora nk’inyigisho, isa n’ivyo twavuze mu kigabane c’imbere, ariko cane cane yihweze kuri Lightning kuri iyi ncuro!


Igikoresho nyamukuru c’iryo reresi ni ububiko bwa Github [Igikoresho c’Umuravyo](Ibikoresho/Igikoresho/Igikoresho c’Umuravyo), ivyo bikaba bigufasha gutanguza iyo ntunganyo muri Regtest.


### Gukoresha node ya Lightning ihuye na RGB


Ivyo bifata kandi bikashira mu ngiro ivyiyumviro vyose vyavuzwe mu bice vyatanguye :




- Iciyumviro c’uko **UTXO** ibujijwe kuri 2/2 Multisig y’umuhora wa Lightning idashobora kwakira amafaranga y’ibice gusa, ariko kandi ishobora kuba Serire ikooreshwa rimwe y’itunga rya RGB (rishobora guhinduka canke ridashobora guhinduka);
- Kwongerwako, muri buri bikorwa binywanisha ama Lightning, ivy’isohoka (`Tapret` canke `Opret`) vyerekeye gushingira intahe Ukobihinduka ivya RGB;
- Ivyubatswe bifitaniye isano (bitcoind/indexer/proxy) kugira ngo vyemeze amafaranga y’ibikorwa vya Bitcoin n’amakuru y'ihanahanwa *yo ku ruhande rw’umukiriya*.


### Kwerekana node ya Lightning ya RGB


Umugambi **`Node ya Lightning ya RGB`** ni umugambi wa Rust daemon ushingiye ku `Rust-Lightning` (LDK) Fork yahinduwe kugira ngo witwararike ukubaho kw’itunga ry'Umuhora wa RGB. Iyo umurongo ufunguwe, ukubaho kw’itunga kurashobora gusobanurwa, kandi igihe cose igihugu c’umurongo gihinduwe, ihinduka rya RGB riraremwa, ryerekana ugusangira kw’itunga mu bisohoka vya Lightning. Ibi bishoboza:




- kwugurura umuhora wa Lightning kuri USDT, nk'akarorero;
- Gucira izira ibimenyetso kurubuga, itegeko nuko izonzira zifise amafaranga akwiye;
- Gukoresha igihano ca Lightning n'ubuhinga bwo gufunga igihe ataco uhinduye: gusa gushinga imizi mwihinduka rya RGB mu gisohoka c'inyongera mwihanahanwa ry'ukwiyemeza.


Kode iracari ku rwego rw'itanguriro: turahimiriza kuyikoresha muri **regtest** canke kuri **Testnet** gusa.


### Gushiramwo node


Kugira ngo dushirehamwe kandi dushiremwo `RGB-lightning-node`, dutangura dukoresheje ububiko n'ibice vyabwo, hanyuma tukarungika:


```bash
git clone https://github.com/RGB-Tools/rgb-lightning-node --recurse-submodules --shallow-submodules
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/098.webp)




- Ihitamwo rya `--recurse-submodules` na ryo nyene rikora ibikoresho bikenewe (harimwo verisiyo ya `Rust-lightning` yahinduwe);
- Ihitamwo rya `--shallow-submodules` rigabanya uburebure bw'iyi clone kugira ngo ryihute gukuraho, mu gihe riguma ritanga uburyo bwo gushika ku bikorwa vy'ingenzi.


Kuva ku muzi w'umugambi, ukoreshe itegeko rikurikira kugira ngo ushirehamwe kandi ushiremwo ibice bibiri:


```bash
cargo install --locked --debug --path .
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/099.webp)




- `--locked` urabe neza yuko verisiyo ifise aho iyoboka yakwirikijwe neza;
- `--debug` ntibitegerezwa, ariko bishobora kugufasha gushira inguvu ahantu hamwe (ushobora gukoresha `--release` niba ushaka);
- `---path .` ibwira `cargo install` gushiramwo kuva mu bubiko buriho.


Ku mpera y'iri tegeko, `rgb-lightning-node` ishirwa mungiro izoja ahabina muri `$CARGO_HOME/bin/` yawe. Utegezwa kumenyako muri runoruhandeariho hari `$PATH` yawe kugira ngo ushobore guhamagara itegeko rivuye mu bubiko ubwaribwi bwose.


### Iterambere risabwa


Kugira ngo bije mungiro, `node ya Lightning ya RGB` daemon bisaba ukuhaba hamwe n'ugutunganywa:




- Node ya bitcoind


Buri kwugurugwa kwa RLN kwose kuzokenerwa kuganira na `bitcoind` kugira ngo gutangaze kandi ikurikirane amahanahanwa yayo yokuri On-Chain. Ivyemezo (kwinjira/ikajambo banga) hama URL (umushitsi/icuma) izokenera gutangwa kuri daemon.




- **Igiharuro** (Electrum canke Esplora)


daemon itegerezwa kuba ishoboye gutanga urutonde no gutohoza amahanahanwa ya On-Chain, vy'umwihariko kugira ngo ironke UTXO umutungo washizweko. Uzokenera kwerekana neza URL y'ubushinguzi bwa Electrum canke Esplora.




- Uwuserukira **RGB**


Nk'uko vyabonetse mu bice vyatanguye, **ubushinguzi bwa proxy** ni igice (kitaringombwa, ariko kirahimirizwa gukoreshwa cane) kugirango hacagagurww ama hanahanwa y'ibirungikwa hagati y'abagenzi ba Lightning. Na none, URL itegerezwa gusobanurwa.


IDs(Ibiranga umuntu) hamwe na URLs zishirwamwo iyo daemon _yuguruwew_ biciye kuri API. Ibindi kuri ivyo mu nyuma.


### Kurungika igerageza


Kugira ngo ukoreshe neza, hariho inyandiko `regtest.sh` itangura ubwo nyene, biciye kuri Docker, urutonde rw'ibikorwa: `bitcoind`, `amashanyarazi` (indexer), `RGB-umukozi-w'ubutumwa`.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/100.webp)


Ivyo bigufasha kurungika uri indani, aho kubitunganiriza, vyatunganijwe imbere y’igihe. Irema kandi igasenyura ibikoresho n’ububiko bw’amakuru ku gusubira gutangura kwose. Tuzotangura n'ugutanguza:


```bash
./regtest.sh start
```


Iyi nyandiko izo:




- kora `docker/` ububiko bw'ugushingura;
- Gukoresha `bitcoind` mu regtest, hamwe n'urutonde `amashanyarazi` na `RGB-umukozi-w'ubutumwa`;
- Rindira gushika vyose bitanguye gukoreshwa.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/101.webp)


Igikwirikira, tuzotanguza ama node menshi ya RLN. Muduce dutandukanye, genda, nk'akarorero (kugira ngo utangure node zitatu za 3):


```bash
# 1st shell
rgb-lightning-node dataldk0/ --daemon-listening-port 3001 \
--ldk-peer-listening-port 9735 --network regtest
# 2nd shell
rgb-lightning-node dataldk1/ --daemon-listening-port 3002 \
--ldk-peer-listening-port 9736 --network regtest
# 3rd shell
rgb-lightning-node dataldk2/ --daemon-listening-port 3003 \
--ldk-peer-listening-port 9737 --network regtest
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/102.webp)




- Igikoresho `--network regtest` kigaragaza ikoreshwa ry'imiterere ya regtest;
- `--daemon-kwumviriza-icuma` yerekana ku cyuho ca REST urudodo rw'umuravyo ruzokwumviriza amahamagara ya API (JSON);
- `--ldk-urunganwe-rutega yompi` igaragaza icuma c'umuravyo P2P co kwumvirizako;
- `dataldk0/`, `dataldk1/` ni inzira zija mu bubiko (buri nzira ibika amakuru yayo ukwayo).


Ushobora kandi gukoresha amabwirizwa ku nzira zawe za RLN ukoresheje umucukumbuzi wawe:


```url
https://rgb-tools.github.io/rgb-lightning-node/
```


Kugira ngo node yugurure umuhora, itegerezwa kubanza kugira ama bitcoin kuri Aderesi yakozwe hakwirikijwe amategeko akwirikira (ku node n°1, nk’akarorero):


```bash
curl -X POST http://localhost:3001/address
```


Inyishu izoguha izoba ifise na Aderesi.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/103.webp)


Ku kigeragezo ca `bitcoind`, tuzocukura ama bitcoin makeyi. Hakoreshwa:


```bash
./regtest.sh mine 101
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/104.webp)


Mukurungika amahera kuri aderesi ya node yakozwe aho hejuru:


```bash
./regtest.sh sendtoaddress <address> <amount>
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/105.webp)


Hanyuma ugucukura ibikuta mukwemeza amahanahanwa:


```bash
./regtest.sh mine 1
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/106.webp)


### Testnet gutangura (Hadakoreshejwe Docker)


Niba ushaka kugerageza ikintu gishobora kuja mungiro, ushobora gutanguza node 3 za RLN kuri Testnet aho gutanguza muri Regtest, yerekana ibikorwa bikorerwa kukarubanda bimeze:


```bash
rgb-lightning-node dataldk0/ --daemon-listening-port 3001 \
--ldk-peer-listening-port 9735 --network testnet
rgb-lightning-node dataldk1/ --daemon-listening-port 3002 \
--ldk-peer-listening-port 9736 --network testnet
rgb-lightning-node dataldk2/ --daemon-listening-port 3003 \
--ldk-peer-listening-port 9737 --network testnet
```


Ataciriwe kirakorwa, iyo ata ntunganyo ibonetse, daemon izogerageza gukoresha:




- `ibikoni_rpc_umushitsi`: `umuyagankuba.isakofe.com`
- `Ikivuko_cy'amafaranga_rpc`: `18332`
- urutonde_url`: `ssl://umuyagankuba.isakoshi.com:50013`
- `iherezo_ry'umuserukira`: `rpcs: umuserukira.


Hakoreshejwe ukwinjira:




- `izina_ry'ukoresha_rpc`: 'ukoresha`
- `izina_ry'ukoresha_rpc`: 'akajambo banga'


Ushobora kandi guhindura uko ushaka binobinu uciye kurino API `init`/`gufungura`.


### Gutanga token ya RGB


Kugira ngo dutange token, tuzotangura kurema ama UTXO "afise amabara":


```bash
curl -X POST -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
-d '{
"up_to": false,
"num": 4,
"size": 2000000,
"fee_rate": 4.2,
"skip_sync": false
}' \
http://localhost:3001/createutxos
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/107.webp)


Birumvikana ko ushobora guhindura urutonde rw’ibintu. Kugira twemeze amaanahanwa, ducukura ama:


```bash
./regtest.sh mine 1
```


Ubu turashobora kurema umutungo wa RGB. Amategeko azotegerezwa kuvana n'ubwoko bw'umutung wipfuza kurema hamwe n'imirongo yayo. Aha ndiko ndakora NIA (*Non Inflatable Asset*) token yitwa "Plan ₿ Academy" rifise Supply y'ibice 1000. `Ugushikama` bigufasha gusobanura ukuntu ibice bishobora kugabanywa.


```bash
curl -X POST -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
-d '{
"amounts": [
1000
],
"ticker": "Plan ₿ Academy",
"name": "Plan ₿ Academy",
"precision": 0
}' \
http://localhost:3001/issueassetnia
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/108.webp)


Inyishu irimwo Inndangakintu y'umutungo y’umutungo mushasha waremwe. Ibuka kwandika iki kimenyetso. Kuvyombona, ni:


```txt
rgb:fc7fMj5S-8yz!vIl-260BEhU-Hj1skvM-ZHcjfyz-RTcWc10
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/109.webp)


Ushobora rero kuyirungika kuri On-Chain, canke ukayitanga kumuora wa Lightning. Ivyo nyene ni vyo tuzokora mu gice gikurikira.


### Kwugurura umuhora wa Lightning hamwe nokurungika umutungo kuri RGB


Utegerezwa kubanza gufatanya node ryawe n'umugenzi kuri Lightning Network ukoresheje itegeko `/connectpeer`. Mu karorero kanje, ndasuzuma node zose. Rero nzogarura urufunguzo rwa bose rw'umuhora wanje wa kabiri w'umuravyo n'iri tegeko:


```bash
curl -X 'GET' \
'http://localhost:3002/nodeinfo' \
-H 'accept: application/json'
```


Itegeko rigarura urufunguzo rwa bose rw'uruzitiro rwanje n°2:


```txt
031e81e4c5c6b6a50cbf5d85b15dad720fec92c62e84bafb34088f0488e00a8e94
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/110.webp)


Ibikurikira, tuzofungura umurongo mu kugaragaza umutungo ubereye (`Plan ₿ Academy`). Itegeko `/openchannel` rigufasha gusobanura ubunini bw'umurongo mu satoshis no guhitamwo gushiramwo umutungo wa RGB. Bivana n’ico ushaka kurema, ariko muri jewe, itegeko ni:


```bash
curl -X POST -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
-d '{
"peer_pubkey_and_opt_addr": "031e81e4c5c6b6a50cbf5d85b15dad720fec92c62e84bafb34088f0488e00a8e94@localhost:9736",
"capacity_sat": 1000000,
"push_msat": 10000000,
"asset_amount": 500,
"asset_id": "rgb:fc7fMj5S-8yz!vIl-260BEhU-Hj1skvM-ZHcjfyz-RTcWc10",
"public": true,
"with_anchors": true,
"fee_base_msat": 1000,
"fee_proportional_millionths": 0,
"temporary_channel_id": "a8b60c8ce3067b5fc881d4831323e24751daec3b64353c8df3205ec5d838f1c5"
}' \
http://localhost:3001/openchannel
```


Ibindi ubimenye hano:




- `peer_pubkey_and_opt_addr`: Ikimenyetso c'umugenzi twipfuza gufatanya (urufunguzo rwa bose twabonye mbere);
- `ubushobozi_sat`: Imihoya yose hamwe yomuri satoshis;
- `push_msat`: Amahera mu millisatoshis mu ntango yimuriwe ku mugenzi iyo umurongo ufunguwe (aha nca nshira ama Sats 10.000  kugira ngo ashobore gukora RGB yimurirwa mu nyuma);
- `asset_amount`: Igitigiri c'itunga rya RGB rizoshikirizwa umurongo;
- `asset_id`: Ikimenyetso kidasanzwe c'umutungo wa RGB ukora mu muhora;
- `public`: Yerekana nimba umuhora ukwiye gushikirizwa abantu bose kugira ngo ukoreshe umurongo ku rubuga.


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/111.webp)


Kugira ngo bemeze ihanahanwa, amabuye 6 aracukurwa:


```bash
./regtest.sh mine 6
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/112.webp)


Umuhora wa Lighning ubu waraguruwe kandi urimwo n'ibimenyetso 500 vya `Plan ₿ Academy` ku ruhande rwa node n°1. Nimba node n°2 rushaka kwakira ibimenyetso vya `Plan ₿ Academy`, rutegerezwa kuba rwakoze facitire. Ehe ingene wobikora:


```bash
curl -X POST -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
-d '{
"amt_msat": 3000000,
"expiry_sec": 420,
"asset_id": "rgb:fc7fMj5S-8yz!vIl-260BEhU-Hj1skvM-ZHcjfyz-RTcWc10",
"asset_amount": 100
}' \
http://localhost:3002/lninvoice
```


Hamwe:




- `amt_msat`: Amafaranga y’ama Satoshi (amasatoshi 3000);
- `expiry_sec`: Umwanya fagitire ihererako mumasegonda;
- `asset_id`: Ikimenyetso c'umutungo wa RGB ufitaniye isano n'umutungo wa fagitire;
- `asset_amount`: Igitigiri c'umutungo wa RGB uzorungikwa hakoreshejwe ino fagitire.


Nkinyishu, uzoronka fagitire ya RGB (nk’uko vyavuzwe mubigabane duherukirako):


```txt
lnbcrt30u1pncgd4rdqud3jxktt5w46x7unfv9kz6mn0v3jsnp4qv0grex9c6m22r9ltkzmzhddwg87eykx96zt47e5pz8sfz8qp28fgpp5jksvqtleryhvwr299qdz96qxzm24augy5agkdhltudk463lt9dassp5d6n0sqgl0c4gx52fdmutrdtqamt0y4xuz2rcgel4hpjwne08gmls9qyysgqcqpcxqzdylz5wfnkywnxvvmkvnt2x4fj6wre0gshvjtv95ervvzzg4592t2gdgchx6mkf5k45jrrdfn8j73d2f2xx4mrxycq7qzry4v4jan6uxhhacyqa4gn6plggwpq9j74tu74f2zsamtz6ymt600p8su4c4ap9g9d8ku2x3wdh6fuc8fd8pff2yzpjrf24ys3cltca9fgqut6gzj
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/113.webp)


Ubu tuzoriha iyi Fagitire kuva ku nzira ya mbere, ifise amahera akenewe n'iyi `Plan ₿ Academy` token:


```bash
curl -X POST -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
-d '{
"invoice": "lnbcrt30u1pncgd4rdqud3jxktt5w46x7unfv9kz6mn0v3jsnp4qv0grex9c6m22r9ltkzmzhddwg87eykx96zt47e5pz8sfz8qp28fgpp5jksvqtleryhvwr299qdz96qxzm24augy5agkdhltudk463lt9dassp5d6n0sqgl0c4gx52fdmutrdtqamt0y4xuz2rcgel4hpjwne08gmls9qyysgqcqpcxqzdylz5wfnkywnxvvmkvnt2x4fj6wre0gshvjtv95ervvzzg4592t2gdgchx6mkf5k45jrrdfn8j73d2f2xx4mrxycq7qzry4v4jan6uxhhacyqa4gn6plggwpq9j74tu74f2zsamtz6ymt600p8su4c4ap9g9d8ku2x3wdh6fuc8fd8pff2yzpjrf24ys3cltca9fgqut6gzj"
}' \
http://localhost:3001/sendpayment
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/114.webp)


Ukwishurwa kwarakozwe. Ivyo bishobora kugenzurwa mu gushitsa itegeko:


```bash
curl -X 'GET' \
'http://localhost:3001/listpayments' \
-H 'accept: application/json'
```


![RGB-Bitcoin](assets/en/115.webp)


Ehe ingene wokoresha node ya Lightning yahinduwe kugira ngoitware itunga rya RGB. Iryo yerekanwa rishingiye kuri:




- Ivyokugerageza (biciye muri `./igerageza.sh`) canke Testnet;
- Igikoresho c'umuravyo (`RGB-igikoresho-c'umuravyo`) gishingiye kuri `bitcoind`, urutonde n'umurongo w'umuravyo`;
- Urutonde rwa JSON REST APIs zo gufungura/gufunga imirongo, gutanga ibimenyetso, gutanga umutungo biciye kuri Lightning, n'ibindi.


Urakoze kuri iyi nzira:




- Ivy’ugukorana n’umuravyo birimwo igisohoka c’inyongera (OP_RETURN canke Taproot) n’ugushinga intahe kw’ihinduka rya RGB;
- Ivyo kwimurira amahera bikorwa mu buryo bumwe nyene n’ubw’amahera ya kera ya Lightning, ariko hakaba hakongerwako RGB token;
- Ivyiyumviro vyinshi vya RLN birashobora guhuzwa n’inzira no kugerageza kwishura mu vyiyumviro vyinshi, igihe cose hariho amahera ahagije mu bitcoins no mu mutungo RGB ku nzira.


Umugambi uguma mu rwego rwa alpha. Ni vyiza rero cane ko wigarukira ku bidukikije vyo kugerageza (regtest, Testnet).


Amahirwe yuguruwe n’iyi nzira y’uguhuza LN-RGB ni menshi cane: stablecoins kuri Lightning, DEX Layer-2, gutanga ibimenyetso bishobora guhinduka canke NFTs ku giciro gito cane... Ibice vyatanguye birerekana ubuhinga bwo kwubaka ivyiyumviro n’ubuhinga bwo kwemeza. Ubu ufise iciyumviro ngirakamaro c’ingene wotuma mwene iyo node ikora, ku bijanye n’iterambere canke ibipimo vyawe vyo muri kazoza.
